uwshcu.F90       coverage:  100.00 %func     96.01 %block

     1)   module uwshcu
     2) 
     3)   use cam_history,    only: outfld, addfld, phys_decomp
     4)   use shr_spfn_mod,   only: erfc => shr_spfn_erfc
     5)   use cam_logfile,    only: iulog
     6)   use ppgrid,         only: pcols, pver, pverp
     7)   use abortutils,     only: endrun
     8)   use spmd_utils,     only: masterproc
     9)   use wv_saturation,  only: qsat
    10) 
    11) 
    12)   implicit none
    13)   private
    14)   save
    15) 
    16)   public &
    17)      uwshcu_readnl,      &
    18)      init_uwshcu,        &
    19)      compute_uwshcu,     &
    20)      compute_uwshcu_inv
    21)   
    22)   integer , parameter :: r8 = selected_real_kind(12)    !  8 byte real
    23)   real(r8), parameter :: unset_r8 = huge(1.0_r8)
    24)   real(r8)            :: xlv                            !  Latent heat of vaporization
    25)   real(r8)            :: xlf                            !  Latent heat of fusion
    26)   real(r8)            :: xls                            !  Latent heat of sublimation = xlv + xlf
    27)   real(r8)            :: cp                             !  Specific heat of dry air
    28)   real(r8)            :: zvir                           !  rh2o/rair - 1
    29)   real(r8)            :: r                              !  Gas constant for dry air
    30)   real(r8)            :: g                              !  Gravitational constant
    31)   real(r8)            :: ep2                            !  mol wgt water vapor / mol wgt dry air 
    32)   real(r8)            :: p00                            !  Reference pressure for exner function
    33)   real(r8)            :: rovcp                          !  R/cp
    34) 
    35)   ! Tuning parameters set via namelist
    36)   real(r8) :: rpen          !  For penetrative entrainment efficiency
    37) 
    38) !===============================================================================
    39) contains
    40) !===============================================================================
    41)   
    42)   real(r8) function exnf(pressure)
    43)            real(r8), intent(in)              :: pressure
    44)            exnf = (pressure/p00)**rovcp
    45)            return
    46)   end function exnf
    47) 
    48) !===============================================================================
    49) 
    50) subroutine uwshcu_readnl(nlfile)
    51) 
    52)    use namelist_utils,  only: find_group_name
    53)    use units,           only: getunit, freeunit
    54)    use mpishorthand
    55) 
    56)    character(len=*), intent(in) :: nlfile  ! filepath for file containing namelist input
    57) 
    58)    ! Local variables
    59)    integer :: unitn, ierr
    60)    character(len=*), parameter :: subname = 'uwshcu_readnl'
    61) 
    62)    ! Namelist variables
    63)    real(r8) :: uwshcu_rpen =  unset_r8    !  For penetrative entrainment efficiency
    64) 
    65)    namelist /uwshcu_nl/ uwshcu_rpen
    66)    !-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
    67) 
    68)    if (masterproc) then
    69)       unitn = getunit()
    70)       open( unitn, file=trim(nlfile), status='old' )
    71)       call find_group_name(unitn, 'uwshcu_nl', status=ierr)
    72)       if (ierr == 0) then
    73)          read(unitn, uwshcu_nl, iostat=ierr)
    74)          if (ierr /= 0) then
    75)             call endrun(subname // ':: ERROR reading namelist')
    76)          end if
    77)       end if
    78)       close(unitn)
    79)       call freeunit(unitn)
    80)    end if
    81) 
    82) #ifdef SPMD
    83)    ! Broadcast namelist variables
    84)    call mpibcast(uwshcu_rpen,            1, mpir8,  0, mpicom)
    85) #endif
    86)    
    87)    rpen=uwshcu_rpen
    88)   
    89) 
    90) end subroutine uwshcu_readnl
    91) 
    92) !===============================================================================
    93) 
    94)   subroutine init_uwshcu( kind, xlv_in, cp_in, xlf_in, zvir_in, r_in, g_in, ep2_in )
    95) 
    96)     !------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
    97)     ! Purpose:                                                     !
    98)     ! Initialize key constants for the shallow convection package. !
    99)     !------------------------------------------------------------- !
   100) 
   101)     use cam_history,   only: outfld, addfld, phys_decomp
   102)     use ppgrid,        only: pcols, pver, pverp
   103)     implicit none
   104)     integer , intent(in) :: kind       !  kind of reals being passed in
   105)     real(r8), intent(in) :: xlv_in     !  Latent heat of vaporization
   106)     real(r8), intent(in) :: xlf_in     !  Latent heat of fusion
   107)     real(r8), intent(in) :: cp_in      !  Specific heat of dry air
   108)     real(r8), intent(in) :: zvir_in    !  rh2o/rair - 1
   109)     real(r8), intent(in) :: r_in       !  Gas constant for dry air
   110)     real(r8), intent(in) :: g_in       !  Gravitational constant
   111)     real(r8), intent(in) :: ep2_in     !  mol wgt water vapor / mol wgt dry air 
   112) 
   113)     character(len=*), parameter :: subname = 'init_uwshcu'
   114) 
   115)     ! ------------------------- !
   116)     ! Internal Output Variables !
   117)     ! ------------------------- !
   118) 
   119)     call addfld( 'qtflx_Cu'       , 'kg/m2/s' , pverp , 'A' , 'Convective qt flux'                                  , phys_decomp )
   120)     call addfld( 'slflx_Cu'       , 'J/m2/s'  , pverp , 'A' , 'Convective sl flux'                                  , phys_decomp )
   121)     call addfld( 'uflx_Cu'        , 'kg/m/s2' , pverp , 'A' , 'Convective  u flux'                                  , phys_decomp )
   122)     call addfld( 'vflx_Cu'        , 'kg/m/s2' , pverp , 'A' , 'Convective  v flux'                                  , phys_decomp )
   123) 
   124)     call addfld( 'qtten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'qt tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   125)     call addfld( 'slten_Cu'       , 'J/kg/s'  , pver  , 'A' , 'sl tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   126)     call addfld( 'uten_Cu'        , 'm/s2'    , pver  , 'A' , ' u tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   127)     call addfld( 'vten_Cu'        , 'm/s2'    , pver  , 'A' , ' v tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   128)     call addfld( 'qvten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'qv tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   129)     call addfld( 'qlten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'ql tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   130)     call addfld( 'qiten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'qi tendency by convection'                           , phys_decomp )
   131) 
   132)     call addfld( 'cbmf_Cu'        , 'kg/m2/s' , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus base mass flux'                              , phys_decomp )
   133)     call addfld( 'ufrcinvbase_Cu' , 'fraction', 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus fraction at PBL top'                         , phys_decomp )
   134)     call addfld( 'ufrclcl_Cu'     , 'fraction', 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus fraction at LCL'                             , phys_decomp )
   135)     call addfld( 'winvbase_Cu'    , 'm/s'     , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus vertical velocity at PBL top'                , phys_decomp )
   136)     call addfld( 'wlcl_Cu'        , 'm/s'     , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus vertical velocity at LCL'                    , phys_decomp )
   137)     call addfld( 'plcl_Cu'        , 'Pa'      , 1     , 'A' , 'LCL of source air'                                   , phys_decomp )
   138)     call addfld( 'pinv_Cu'        , 'Pa'      , 1     , 'A' , 'PBL top pressure'                                    , phys_decomp )
   139)     call addfld( 'plfc_Cu'        , 'Pa'      , 1     , 'A' , 'LFC of source air'                                   , phys_decomp )
   140)     call addfld( 'pbup_Cu'        , 'Pa'      , 1     , 'A' , 'Highest interface level of positive cumulus buoyancy', phys_decomp )
   141)     call addfld( 'ppen_Cu'        , 'Pa'      , 1     , 'A' , 'Highest level where cumulus w is 0'                  , phys_decomp )
   142)     call addfld( 'qtsrc_Cu'       , 'kg/kg'   , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus source air qt'                               , phys_decomp )
   143)     call addfld( 'thlsrc_Cu'      , 'K'       , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus source air thl'                              , phys_decomp )
   144)     call addfld( 'thvlsrc_Cu'     , 'K'       , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus source air thvl'                             , phys_decomp )
   145)     call addfld( 'emfkbup_Cu'     , 'kg/m2/s' , 1     , 'A' , 'Penetrative mass flux at kbup'                       , phys_decomp )
   146)     call addfld( 'cin_Cu'         , 'J/kg'    , 1     , 'A' , 'CIN upto LFC'                                        , phys_decomp )
   147)     call addfld( 'cinlcl_Cu'      , 'J/kg'    , 1     , 'A' , 'CIN upto LCL'                                        , phys_decomp )
   148)     call addfld( 'cbmflimit_Cu'   , 'kg/m2/s' , 1     , 'A' , 'cbmflimiter'                                         , phys_decomp )
   149)     call addfld( 'tkeavg_Cu'      , 'm2/s2'   , 1     , 'A' , 'Average tke within PBL for convection scheme'        , phys_decomp )
   150)     call addfld( 'zinv_Cu'        , 'm'       , 1     , 'A' , 'PBL top height'                                      , phys_decomp )
   151)     call addfld( 'rcwp_Cu'        , 'kg/m2'   , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus LWP+IWP'                                     , phys_decomp )
   152)     call addfld( 'rlwp_Cu'        , 'kg/m2'   , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus LWP'                                         , phys_decomp )
   153)     call addfld( 'riwp_Cu'        , 'kg/m2'   , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus IWP'                                         , phys_decomp )
   154)     call addfld( 'tophgt_Cu'      , 'm'       , 1     , 'A' , 'Cumulus top height'                                  , phys_decomp )
   155) 
   156)     call addfld( 'wu_Cu'          , 'm/s'     , pverp , 'A' , 'Convective updraft vertical velocity'                , phys_decomp )
   157)     call addfld( 'ufrc_Cu'        , 'fraction', pverp , 'A' , 'Convective updraft fractional area'                  , phys_decomp )
   158)     call addfld( 'qtu_Cu'         , 'kg/kg'   , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft qt'                                  , phys_decomp )
   159)     call addfld( 'thlu_Cu'        , 'K'       , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft thl'                                 , phys_decomp )
   160)     call addfld( 'thvu_Cu'        , 'K'       , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft thv'                                 , phys_decomp )
   161)     call addfld( 'uu_Cu'          , 'm/s'     , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft uwnd'                                , phys_decomp )
   162)     call addfld( 'vu_Cu'          , 'm/s'     , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft vwnd'                                , phys_decomp )
   163)     call addfld( 'qtu_emf_Cu'     , 'kg/kg'   , pverp , 'A' , 'qt of penatratively entrained air'                   , phys_decomp )
   164)     call addfld( 'thlu_emf_Cu'    , 'K'       , pverp , 'A' , 'thl of penatratively entrained air'                  , phys_decomp )
   165)     call addfld( 'uu_emf_Cu'      , 'm/s'     , pverp , 'A' , 'uwnd of penatratively entrained air'                 , phys_decomp )
   166)     call addfld( 'vu_emf_Cu'      , 'm/s'     , pverp , 'A' , 'vwnd of penatratively entrained air'                 , phys_decomp )
   167)     call addfld( 'umf_Cu'         , 'kg/m2/s' , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft mass flux'                           , phys_decomp )
   168)     call addfld( 'uemf_Cu'        , 'kg/m2/s' , pverp , 'A' , 'Cumulus net ( updraft + entrainment ) mass flux'     , phys_decomp )
   169)     call addfld( 'qcu_Cu'         , 'kg/kg'   , pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft LWC+IWC'                             , phys_decomp )
   170)     call addfld( 'qlu_Cu'         , 'kg/kg'   , pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft LWC'                                 , phys_decomp )
   171)     call addfld( 'qiu_Cu'         , 'kg/kg'   , pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus updraft IWC'                                 , phys_decomp )
   172)     call addfld( 'cufrc_Cu'       , 'fraction', pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus cloud fraction'                              , phys_decomp )
   173)     call addfld( 'fer_Cu'         , '1/m'     , pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus lateral fractional entrainment rate'         , phys_decomp )
   174)     call addfld( 'fdr_Cu'         , '1/m'     , pver  , 'A' , 'Cumulus lateral fractional detrainment Rate'         , phys_decomp )
   175) 
   176)     call addfld( 'dwten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Expellsion rate of cumulus cloud water to env.'      , phys_decomp )
   177)     call addfld( 'diten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Expellsion rate of cumulus ice water to env.'        , phys_decomp )
   178)     call addfld( 'qrten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Production rate of rain by cumulus'                  , phys_decomp )
   179)     call addfld( 'qsten_Cu'       , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Production rate of snow by cumulus'                  , phys_decomp )
   180)     call addfld( 'flxrain_Cu'     , 'kg/m2/s' , pverp , 'A' , 'Rain flux induced by Cumulus'                        , phys_decomp )
   181)     call addfld( 'flxsnow_Cu'     , 'kg/m2/s' , pverp , 'A' , 'Snow flux induced by Cumulus'                        , phys_decomp )
   182)     call addfld( 'ntraprd_Cu'     , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Net production rate of rain by Cumulus'              , phys_decomp )
   183)     call addfld( 'ntsnprd_Cu'     , 'kg/kg/s' , pver  , 'A' , 'Net production rate of snow by Cumulus'              , phys_decomp )
   184) 
   185)     call addfld( 'excessu_Cu'     , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'Updraft saturation excess'                           , phys_decomp )
   186)     call addfld( 'excess0_Cu'     , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'Environmental saturation excess'                     , phys_decomp )
   187)     call addfld( 'xc_Cu'          , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'Critical mixing ratio'                               , phys_decomp )
   188)     call addfld( 'aquad_Cu'       , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'aquad'                                               , phys_decomp )
   189)     call addfld( 'bquad_Cu'       , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'bquad'                                               , phys_decomp )
   190)     call addfld( 'cquad_Cu'       , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'cquad'                                               , phys_decomp )
   191)     call addfld( 'bogbot_Cu'      , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'Cloud buoyancy at the bottom interface'              , phys_decomp )
   192)     call addfld( 'bogtop_Cu'      , 'no'      , pver  , 'A' , 'Cloud buoyancy at the top interface'                 , phys_decomp )
   193) 
   194)     call addfld('exit_UWCu_Cu'    , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_UWCu'                                           , phys_decomp )
   195)     call addfld('exit_conden_Cu'  , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_conden'                                         , phys_decomp )
   196)     call addfld('exit_klclmkx_Cu' , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_klclmkx'                                        , phys_decomp )
   197)     call addfld('exit_klfcmkx_Cu' , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_klfcmkx'                                        , phys_decomp )
   198)     call addfld('exit_ufrc_Cu'    , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_ufrc'                                           , phys_decomp )
   199)     call addfld('exit_wtw_Cu'     , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_wtw'                                            , phys_decomp )
   200)     call addfld('exit_drycore_Cu' , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_drycore'                                        , phys_decomp )
   201)     call addfld('exit_wu_Cu'      , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_wu'                                             , phys_decomp )
   202)     call addfld('exit_cufilter_Cu', 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_cufilter'                                       , phys_decomp )
   203)     call addfld('exit_kinv1_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_kinv1'                                          , phys_decomp )
   204)     call addfld('exit_rei_Cu'     , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'exit_rei'                                            , phys_decomp )
   205) 
   206)     call addfld('limit_shcu_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_shcu'                                          , phys_decomp )
   207)     call addfld('limit_negcon_Cu' , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_negcon'                                        , phys_decomp )
   208)     call addfld('limit_ufrc_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_ufrc'                                          , phys_decomp )
   209)     call addfld('limit_ppen_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_ppen'                                          , phys_decomp )
   210)     call addfld('limit_emf_Cu'    , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_emf'                                           , phys_decomp )
   211)     call addfld('limit_cinlcl_Cu' , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_cinlcl'                                        , phys_decomp )
   212)     call addfld('limit_cin_Cu'    , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_cin'                                           , phys_decomp )
   213)     call addfld('limit_cbmf_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_cbmf'                                          , phys_decomp )
   214)     call addfld('limit_rei_Cu'    , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'limit_rei'                                           , phys_decomp )
   215)     call addfld('ind_delcin_Cu'   , 'no'      , 1     , 'A' , 'ind_delcin'                                          , phys_decomp )
   216) 
   217)     if( kind .ne. r8 ) then
   218)         write(iulog,*) subname//': ERROR -- real KIND does not match internal specification.'
   219)         call endrun(subname//': ERROR -- real KIND does not match internal specification.')
   220)     endif
   221) 
   222)     xlv   = xlv_in
   223)     xlf   = xlf_in
   224)     xls   = xlv + xlf
   225)     cp    = cp_in
   226)     zvir  = zvir_in
   227)     r     = r_in
   228)     g     = g_in
   229)     ep2   = ep2_in
   230)     p00   = 1.e5_r8
   231)     rovcp = r/cp
   232) 
   233)     if (rpen == unset_r8) then
   234)        call endrun(subname//': uwshcu_rpen must be set in the namelist')
   235)     end if
   236) 
   237)     if ( masterproc ) then 
   238)        write(iulog,*) subname//': tuning parameters: rpen=',rpen
   239)     endif
   240) 
   241)   end subroutine init_uwshcu
   242) 
   243)   subroutine compute_uwshcu_inv( mix      , mkx        , iend          , ncnst     , dt       ,  & 
   244)                                  ps0_inv  , zs0_inv    , p0_inv        , z0_inv    , dp0_inv  ,  &
   245)                                  u0_inv   , v0_inv     , qv0_inv       , ql0_inv   , qi0_inv  ,  &
   246)                                  t0_inv   , s0_inv     , tr0_inv       ,                         &
   247)                                  tke_inv  , cldfrct_inv, concldfrct_inv, pblh      , cush     ,  & 
   248)                                  umf_inv  , slflx_inv  , qtflx_inv     ,                         & 
   249)                                  flxprc1_inv, flxsnow1_inv,     				 &
   250)                                  qvten_inv, qlten_inv  , qiten_inv     ,                         &
   251)                                  sten_inv , uten_inv   , vten_inv      , trten_inv ,             &  
   252)                                  qrten_inv, qsten_inv  , precip        , snow      , evapc_inv,  &
   253)                                  cufrc_inv, qcu_inv    , qlu_inv       , qiu_inv   ,             &   
   254)                                  cbmf     , qc_inv     , rliq          ,                         &
   255)                                  cnt_inv  , cnb_inv    , lchnk         , dpdry0_inv )
   256) 
   257)     implicit none
   258)     integer , intent(in)    :: lchnk     
   259)     integer , intent(in)    :: mix
   260)     integer , intent(in)    :: mkx
   261)     integer , intent(in)    :: iend
   262)     integer , intent(in)    :: ncnst
   263)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dt                       !  Time step : 2*delta_t [ s ]
   264)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: ps0_inv(mix,mkx+1)       !  Environmental pressure at the interfaces [ Pa ]
   265)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: zs0_inv(mix,mkx+1)       !  Environmental height at the interfaces   [ m ]
   266)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: p0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental pressure at the layer mid-point [ Pa ]
   267)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: z0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental height at the layer mid-point [ m ]
   268)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dp0_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Environmental layer pressure thickness [ Pa ] > 0.
   269)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dpdry0_inv(mix,mkx)      !  Environmental dry layer pressure thickness [ Pa ]
   270)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: u0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental zonal wind [ m/s ]
   271)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: v0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental meridional wind [ m/s ]
   272)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: qv0_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Environmental water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   273)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: ql0_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Environmental liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   274)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: qi0_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Environmental ice specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   275)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: t0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental temperature [ K ]
   276)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: s0_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental dry static energy [ J/kg ]
   277)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: tr0_inv(mix,mkx,ncnst)   !  Environmental tracers [ #, kg/kg ]
   278)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: tke_inv(mix,mkx+1)       !  Turbulent kinetic energy at the interfaces [ m2/s2 ]
   279)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: cldfrct_inv(mix,mkx)     !  Total cloud fraction at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   280)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: concldfrct_inv(mix,mkx)  !  Total convective ( shallow + deep ) cloud fraction
   281)                                                         !  at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   282)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: pblh(mix)                !  Height of PBL [ m ]
   283)     real(r8), intent(inout) :: cush(mix)                !  Convective scale height [ m ]
   284)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: umf_inv(mix,mkx+1)       !  Updraft mass flux at the interfaces [ kg/m2/s ]
   285)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qvten_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Tendency of water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   286)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qlten_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Tendency of liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   287)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qiten_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Tendency of ice specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   288)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: sten_inv(mix,mkx)        !  Tendency of dry static energy [ J/kg/s ]
   289)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: uten_inv(mix,mkx)        !  Tendency of zonal wind [ m/s2 ]
   290)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: vten_inv(mix,mkx)        !  Tendency of meridional wind [ m/s2 ]
   291)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: trten_inv(mix,mkx,ncnst) !  Tendency of tracers [ #/s, kg/kg/s ]
   292)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qrten_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Tendency of rain water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   293)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qsten_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Tendency of snow specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   294)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: precip(mix)              !  Precipitation ( rain + snow ) flux at the surface [ m/s ]
   295)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: snow(mix)                !  Snow flux at the surface [ m/s ]
   296)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: evapc_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Evaporation of precipitation [ kg/kg/s ]
   297)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: rliq(mix)                !  Vertical integral of tendency of detrained cloud condensate qc [ m/s ]
   298)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: slflx_inv(mix,mkx+1)     !  Updraft liquid static energy flux [ J/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   299)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qtflx_inv(mix,mkx+1)     !  Updraft total water flux [ kg/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   300)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: flxprc1_inv(mix,mkx+1)   ! uw grid-box mean rain+snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
   301)                                                         ! for physics buffer calls in convect_shallow.F90
   302)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: flxsnow1_inv(mix,mkx+1)  ! uw grid-box mean snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
   303)                                                         ! for physics buffer calls in convect_shallow.F90
   304) 
   305)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cufrc_inv(mix,mkx)       !  Shallow cumulus cloud fraction at the layer mid-point [ fraction ]
   306)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qcu_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Liquid+ice specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   307)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qlu_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Liquid water specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   308)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qiu_inv(mix,mkx)         !  Ice specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   309)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qc_inv(mix,mkx)          !  Tendency of cumulus condensate detrained into the environment [ kg/kg/s ]
   310)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cbmf(mix)                !  Cumulus base mass flux [ kg/m2/s ]
   311)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cnt_inv(mix)             !  Cumulus top  interface index, cnt = kpen [ no ]
   312)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cnb_inv(mix)             !  Cumulus base interface index, cnb = krel - 1 [ no ]
   313) 
   314)     real(r8)                :: ps0(mix,0:mkx)           !  Environmental pressure at the interfaces [ Pa ]
   315)     real(r8)                :: zs0(mix,0:mkx)           !  Environmental height at the interfaces   [ m ]
   316)     real(r8)                :: p0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental pressure at the layer mid-point [ Pa ]
   317)     real(r8)                :: z0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental height at the layer mid-point [ m ]
   318)     real(r8)                :: dp0(mix,mkx)             !  Environmental layer pressure thickness [ Pa ] > 0.
   319)     real(r8)                :: dpdry0(mix,mkx)          !  Environmental dry layer pressure thickness [ Pa ]
   320)     real(r8)                :: u0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental zonal wind [ m/s ]
   321)     real(r8)                :: v0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental meridional wind [ m/s ]
   322)     real(r8)                :: tke(mix,0:mkx)           !  Turbulent kinetic energy at the interfaces [ m2/s2 ]
   323)     real(r8)                :: cldfrct(mix,mkx)         !  Total cloud fraction at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   324)     real(r8)                :: concldfrct(mix,mkx)      !  Total convective ( shallow + deep ) cloud fraction
   325)                                                         ! at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   326)     real(r8)                :: qv0(mix,mkx)             !  Environmental water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   327)     real(r8)                :: ql0(mix,mkx)             !  Environmental liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   328)     real(r8)                :: qi0(mix,mkx)             !  Environmental ice specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   329)     real(r8)                :: t0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental temperature [ K ]
   330)     real(r8)                :: s0(mix,mkx)              !  Environmental dry static energy [ J/kg ]
   331)     real(r8)                :: tr0(mix,mkx,ncnst)       !  Environmental tracers [ #, kg/kg ]
   332)     real(r8)                :: umf(mix,0:mkx)           !  Updraft mass flux at the interfaces [ kg/m2/s ]
   333)     real(r8)                :: qvten(mix,mkx)           !  Tendency of water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   334)     real(r8)                :: qlten(mix,mkx)           !  Tendency of liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   335)     real(r8)                :: qiten(mix,mkx)           !  tendency of ice specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   336)     real(r8)                :: sten(mix,mkx)            !  Tendency of static energy [ J/kg/s ]
   337)     real(r8)                :: uten(mix,mkx)            !  Tendency of zonal wind [ m/s2 ]
   338)     real(r8)                :: vten(mix,mkx)            !  Tendency of meridional wind [ m/s2 ]
   339)     real(r8)                :: trten(mix,mkx,ncnst)     !  Tendency of tracers [ #/s, kg/kg/s ]
   340)     real(r8)                :: qrten(mix,mkx)           !  Tendency of rain water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   341)     real(r8)                :: qsten(mix,mkx)           !  Tendency of snow speficif humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   342)     real(r8)                :: evapc(mix,mkx)           !  Tendency of evaporation of precipitation [ kg/kg/s ]
   343)     real(r8)                :: slflx(mix,0:mkx)         !  Updraft liquid static energy flux [ J/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   344)     real(r8)                :: qtflx(mix,0:mkx)         !  Updraft total water flux [ kg/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   345)     real(r8)                :: flxprc1(mix,0:mkx)       ! uw grid-box mean rain+snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
   346)                                                         ! for physics buffer calls in convect_shallow.F90
   347)     real(r8)                :: flxsnow1(mix,0:mkx)      ! uw grid-box mean snow flux (kg m^-2 s^-1)
   348)                                                         ! for physics buffer calls in convect_shallow.F90
   349)     real(r8)                :: cufrc(mix,mkx)           !  Shallow cumulus cloud fraction at the layer mid-point [ fraction ]
   350)     real(r8)                :: qcu(mix,mkx)             !  Condensate water specific humidity within cumulus updraft
   351)                                                         ! at the layer mid-point [ kg/kg ]
   352)     real(r8)                :: qlu(mix,mkx)             !  Liquid water specific humidity within cumulus updraft
   353)                                                         ! at the layer mid-point [ kg/kg ]
   354)     real(r8)                :: qiu(mix,mkx)             !  Ice specific humidity within cumulus updraft
   355)                                                         ! at the layer mid-point [ kg/kg ]
   356)     real(r8)                :: qc(mix,mkx)              !  Tendency of cumulus condensate detrained into the environment [ kg/kg/s ]
   357)     real(r8)                :: cnt(mix)                 !  Cumulus top  interface index, cnt = kpen [ no ]
   358)     real(r8)                :: cnb(mix)                 !  Cumulus base interface index, cnb = krel - 1 [ no ] 
   359)     integer                 :: k                        !  Vertical index for local fields [ no ] 
   360)     integer                 :: k_inv                    !  Vertical index for incoming fields [ no ]
   361)     integer                 :: m                        !  Tracer index [ no ]
   362) 
   363)     do k = 1, mkx
   364)        k_inv               = mkx + 1 - k
   365)        p0(:iend,k)         = p0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   366)        u0(:iend,k)         = u0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   367)        v0(:iend,k)         = v0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   368)        z0(:iend,k)         = z0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   369)        dp0(:iend,k)        = dp0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   370)        dpdry0(:iend,k)     = dpdry0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   371)        qv0(:iend,k)        = qv0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   372)        ql0(:iend,k)        = ql0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   373)        qi0(:iend,k)        = qi0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   374)        t0(:iend,k)         = t0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   375)        s0(:iend,k)         = s0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   376)        cldfrct(:iend,k)    = cldfrct_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   377)        concldfrct(:iend,k) = concldfrct_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   378)        do m = 1, ncnst
   379)           tr0(:iend,k,m)   = tr0_inv(:iend,k_inv,m)
   380)        enddo
   381)     enddo
   382)     
   383)     do k = 0, mkx
   384)        k_inv               = mkx + 1 - k
   385)        ps0(:iend,k)        = ps0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   386)        zs0(:iend,k)        = zs0_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   387)        tke(:iend,k)        = tke_inv(:iend,k_inv)
   388)     end do
   389) 
   390)     call compute_uwshcu( mix  , mkx    , iend      , ncnst , dt   , &
   391)                          ps0  , zs0    , p0        , z0    , dp0  , &
   392)                          u0   , v0     , qv0       , ql0   , qi0  , & 
   393)                          t0   , s0     , tr0       ,                & 
   394)                          tke  , cldfrct, concldfrct, pblh  , cush , & 
   395)                          umf  , slflx  , qtflx     ,                &  
   396)                          flxprc1  , flxsnow1  ,		            &
   397)                          qvten, qlten  , qiten     ,                & 
   398)                          sten , uten   , vten      , trten ,        &
   399)                          qrten, qsten  , precip    , snow  , evapc, &
   400)                          cufrc, qcu    , qlu       , qiu   ,        &
   401)                          cbmf , qc     , rliq      ,                &
   402)                          cnt  , cnb    , lchnk     , dpdry0 )
   403) 
   404)     ! Reverse cloud top/base interface indices
   405) 
   406)        cnt_inv(:iend) = mkx + 1 - cnt(:iend)
   407)        cnb_inv(:iend) = mkx + 1 - cnb(:iend)
   408) 
   409)     do k = 0, mkx
   410)        k_inv                  = mkx + 1 - k
   411)        umf_inv(:iend,k_inv)   = umf(:iend,k)       
   412)        slflx_inv(:iend,k_inv) = slflx(:iend,k)     
   413)        qtflx_inv(:iend,k_inv) = qtflx(:iend,k)
   414)        flxprc1_inv(:iend,k_inv) = flxprc1(:iend,k)     ! reversed for output to cam
   415)        flxsnow1_inv(:iend,k_inv) = flxsnow1(:iend,k)   ! ""
   416)     end do
   417) 
   418)     do k = 1, mkx
   419)        k_inv                         = mkx + 1 - k
   420)        qvten_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = qvten(:iend,k)   
   421)        qlten_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = qlten(:iend,k)   
   422)        qiten_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = qiten(:iend,k)   
   423)        sten_inv(:iend,k_inv)         = sten(:iend,k)    
   424)        uten_inv(:iend,k_inv)         = uten(:iend,k)    
   425)        vten_inv(:iend,k_inv)         = vten(:iend,k)    
   426)        qrten_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = qrten(:iend,k)   
   427)        qsten_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = qsten(:iend,k)   
   428)        evapc_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = evapc(:iend,k)
   429)        cufrc_inv(:iend,k_inv)        = cufrc(:iend,k)   
   430)        qcu_inv(:iend,k_inv)          = qcu(:iend,k)     
   431)        qlu_inv(:iend,k_inv)          = qlu(:iend,k)     
   432)        qiu_inv(:iend,k_inv)          = qiu(:iend,k)     
   433)        qc_inv(:iend,k_inv)           = qc(:iend,k)      
   434)        do m = 1, ncnst
   435)           trten_inv(:iend,k_inv,m)   = trten(:iend,k,m) 
   436)        enddo
   437) 
   438)     enddo
   439) 
   440)   end subroutine compute_uwshcu_inv
   441) 
   442)   subroutine compute_uwshcu( mix      , mkx       , iend         , ncnst    , dt        , &
   443)                              ps0_in   , zs0_in    , p0_in        , z0_in    , dp0_in    , &
   444)                              u0_in    , v0_in     , qv0_in       , ql0_in   , qi0_in    , &
   445)                              t0_in    , s0_in     , tr0_in       ,                        &
   446)                              tke_in   , cldfrct_in, concldfrct_in,  pblh_in , cush_inout, & 
   447)                              umf_out  , slflx_out , qtflx_out    ,                        &
   448)                              flxprc1_out  , flxsnow1_out  , 			 	  &
   449)                              qvten_out, qlten_out , qiten_out    ,                        & 
   450)                              sten_out , uten_out  , vten_out     , trten_out,             &
   451)                              qrten_out, qsten_out , precip_out   , snow_out , evapc_out , &
   452)                              cufrc_out, qcu_out   , qlu_out      , qiu_out  ,             &
   453)                              cbmf_out , qc_out    , rliq_out     ,                        &
   454)                              cnt_out  , cnb_out   , lchnk        , dpdry0_in )
   455) 
   456)     ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
   457)     !                                                              !  
   458)     !  University of Washington Shallow Convection Scheme          !
   459)     !                                                              !
   460)     !  Described in Park and Bretherton. 2008. J. Climate :        !
   461)     !                                                              !
   462)     ! 'The University of Washington shallow convection and         !
   463)     !  moist turbulent schemes and their impact on climate         !
   464)     !  simulations with the Community Atmosphere Model'            !
   465)     !                                                              !
   466)     !  Coded by Sungsu Park. Oct.2005.                             ! 
   467)     !                        May.2008.                             !
   468)     !  For questions, send an email to sungsup@ucar.edu or         ! 
   469)     !                                  sungsu@atmos.washington.edu !
   470)     !                                                              !
   471)     ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
   472)  
   473)     use cam_history,     only : outfld, addfld, phys_decomp
   474)     use constituents,    only : qmin, cnst_get_type_byind, cnst_get_ind
   475)     use wv_saturation,   only : findsp_vc
   476) 
   477)     implicit none
   478) 
   479)     ! ---------------------- !
   480)     ! Input-Output Variables !
   481)     ! ---------------------- !
   482) 
   483)     integer , intent(in)    :: lchnk
   484)     integer , intent(in)    :: mix
   485)     integer , intent(in)    :: mkx
   486)     integer , intent(in)    :: iend
   487)     integer , intent(in)    :: ncnst
   488)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dt                             !  Time step : 2*delta_t [ s ]
   489)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: ps0_in(mix,0:mkx)              !  Environmental pressure at the interfaces [ Pa ]
   490)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: zs0_in(mix,0:mkx)              !  Environmental height at the interfaces [ m ]
   491)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: p0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental pressure at the layer mid-point [ Pa ]
   492)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: z0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental height at the layer mid-point [ m ]
   493)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dp0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Environmental layer pressure thickness [ Pa ] > 0.
   494)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: dpdry0_in(mix,mkx)             !  Environmental dry layer pressure thickness [ Pa ]
   495)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: u0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental zonal wind [ m/s ]
   496)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: v0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental meridional wind [ m/s ]
   497)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: qv0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Environmental water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   498)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: ql0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Environmental liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   499)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: qi0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Environmental ice specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   500)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: t0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental temperature [ K ]
   501)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: s0_in(mix,mkx)                 !  Environmental dry static energy [ J/kg ]
   502)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: tr0_in(mix,mkx,ncnst)          !  Environmental tracers [ #, kg/kg ]
   503)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: tke_in(mix,0:mkx)              !  Turbulent kinetic energy at the interfaces [ m2/s2 ]
   504)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: cldfrct_in(mix,mkx)            !  Total cloud fraction at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   505)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: concldfrct_in(mix,mkx)         !  Total convective cloud fraction
   506)                                                               ! at the previous time step [ fraction ]
   507)     real(r8), intent(in)    :: pblh_in(mix)                   !  Height of PBL [ m ]
   508)     real(r8), intent(inout) :: cush_inout(mix)                !  Convective scale height [ m ]
   509) 
   510)     real(r8)                   tw0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Wet bulb temperature [ K ]
   511)     real(r8)                   qw0_in(mix,mkx)                !  Wet-bulb specific humidity [ kg/kg ]
   512) 
   513)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: umf_out(mix,0:mkx)             !  Updraft mass flux at the interfaces [ kg/m2/s ]
   514)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qvten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of water vapor specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   515)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qlten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of liquid water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   516)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qiten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of ice specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   517)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: sten_out(mix,mkx)              !  Tendency of dry static energy [ J/kg/s ]
   518)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: uten_out(mix,mkx)              !  Tendency of zonal wind [ m/s2 ]
   519)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: vten_out(mix,mkx)              !  Tendency of meridional wind [ m/s2 ]
   520)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: trten_out(mix,mkx,ncnst)       !  Tendency of tracers [ #/s, kg/kg/s ]
   521)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qrten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of rain water specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   522)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qsten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of snow specific humidity [ kg/kg/s ]
   523)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: precip_out(mix)                !  Precipitation ( rain + snow ) rate at surface [ m/s ]
   524)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: snow_out(mix)                  !  Snow rate at surface [ m/s ]
   525)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: evapc_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of evaporation of precipitation [ kg/kg/s ]
   526)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: slflx_out(mix,0:mkx)           !  Updraft/pen.entrainment liquid static energy flux
   527)                                                               ! [ J/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   528)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qtflx_out(mix,0:mkx)           !  updraft/pen.entrainment total water flux [ kg/kg * kg/m2/s ]
   529)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: flxprc1_out(mix,0:mkx)         ! precip (rain+snow) flux
   530)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: flxsnow1_out(mix,0:mkx)        ! snow flux
   531)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cufrc_out(mix,mkx)             !  Shallow cumulus cloud fraction at the layer mid-point [ fraction ]
   532)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qcu_out(mix,mkx)               !  Condensate water specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   533)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qlu_out(mix,mkx)               !  Liquid water specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   534)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qiu_out(mix,mkx)               !  Ice specific humidity within cumulus updraft [ kg/kg ]
   535)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cbmf_out(mix)                  !  Cloud base mass flux [ kg/m2/s ]
   536)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: qc_out(mix,mkx)                !  Tendency of detrained cumulus condensate
   537)                                                               ! into the environment [ kg/kg/s ]
   538)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: rliq_out(mix)                  !  Vertical integral of qc_out [ m/s ]
   539)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cnt_out(mix)                   !  Cumulus top  interface index, cnt = kpen [ no ]
   540)     real(r8), intent(out)   :: cnb_out(mix)                   !  Cumulus base interface index, cnb = krel - 1 [ no ] 
   541) 
   542)     !
   543)     ! Internal Output Variables
   544)     !
   545) 
   546)     real(r8)                   qtten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of qt [ kg/kg/s ]
   547)     real(r8)                   slten_out(mix,mkx)             !  Tendency of sl [ J/kg/s ]
   548)     real(r8)                   ufrc_out(mix,0:mkx)            !  Updraft fractional area at the interfaces [ fraction ]
   549)     real(r8)                   uflx_out(mix,0:mkx)            !  Updraft/pen.entrainment zonal momentum flux [ m/s/m2/s ]
   550)     real(r8)                   vflx_out(mix,0:mkx)            !  Updraft/pen.entrainment meridional momentum flux [ m/s/m2/s ]
   551)     real(r8)                   fer_out(mix,mkx)               !  Fractional lateral entrainment rate [ 1/Pa ]
   552)     real(r8)                   fdr_out(mix,mkx)               !  Fractional lateral detrainment rate [ 1/Pa ]
   553)     real(r8)                   cinh_out(mix)                  !  Convective INhibition upto LFC (CIN) [ J/kg ]
   554)     real(r8)                   trflx_out(mix,0:mkx,ncnst)     !  Updraft/pen.entrainment tracer flux [ #/m2/s, kg/kg/m2/s ] 
   555)    
   556)     ! -------------------------------------------- !
   557)     ! One-dimensional variables at each grid point !
   558)     ! -------------------------------------------- !
   559) 
   560)     ! 1. Input variables
   561) 
   562)     real(r8)    ps0(0:mkx)                                    !  Environmental pressure at the interfaces [ Pa ]
   563)     real(r8)    zs0(0:mkx)                                    !  Environmental height at the interfaces [ m ]
   564)     real(r8)    p0(mkx)                                       !  Environmental pressure at the layer mid-point [ Pa ]
   565)     real(r8)    z0(mkx)                                       !  Environmental height at the layer mid-point [ m ]

   904)     real(r8)  ind_delcin(mix)
   905) 
   906)     real(r8) :: ufrcinvbase_s, ufrclcl_s, winvbase_s, wlcl_s, plcl_s, pinv_s, plfc_s, &
   907)                 qtsrc_s, thlsrc_s, thvlsrc_s, emfkbup_s, cinlcl_s, pbup_s, ppen_s, cbmflimit_s, &
   908)                 tkeavg_s, zinv_s, rcwp_s, rlwp_s, riwp_s 
   909)     real(r8) :: ufrcinvbase, winvbase, pinv, zinv, emfkbup, cbmflimit, rho0rel  
   910) 
   911)     !----- Variables for implicit CIN computation
   912) 
   913)     real(r8), dimension(mkx)         :: qv0_s  , ql0_s   , qi0_s   , s0_s    , u0_s    ,           & 
   914)                                         v0_s   , t0_s    , qt0_s   , thl0_s  , thvl0_s , qvten_s , &
   915)                                         qlten_s, qiten_s , qrten_s , qsten_s , sten_s  , evapc_s , &
   916)                                         uten_s , vten_s  , cufrc_s , qcu_s   , qlu_s   , qiu_s   , &
   917)                                         fer_s  , fdr_s   , qc_s    , qtten_s , slten_s 
   918)     real(r8), dimension(0:mkx)       :: umf_s  , slflx_s , qtflx_s , ufrc_s  , uflx_s , vflx_s
   919)     real(r8)                         :: cush_s , precip_s, snow_s  , cin_s   , rliq_s, cbmf_s, cnt_s, cnb_s
   920)     real(r8)                         :: cin_i,cin_f,del_CIN,ke,alpha,thlj
   921)     real(r8)                         :: cinlcl_i,cinlcl_f,del_cinlcl
   922)     integer                          :: iter
   923) 
   924)     real(r8), dimension(mkx,ncnst)   :: tr0_s, trten_s
   925)     real(r8), dimension(0:mkx,ncnst) :: trflx_s
   926) 
   927)     !----- Variables for temporary storages
   928) 
   929)     real(r8), dimension(mkx)         :: qv0_o, ql0_o, qi0_o, t0_o, s0_o, u0_o, v0_o
   930)     real(r8), dimension(mkx)         :: qt0_o    , thl0_o   , thvl0_o   ,                         &
   931)                                         qvten_o  , qlten_o  , qiten_o   , qrten_o   , qsten_o ,   &
   932)                                         sten_o   , uten_o   , vten_o    , qcu_o     , qlu_o   ,   & 
   933)                                         qiu_o    , cufrc_o  , evapc_o   ,                         &
   934)                                         thv0bot_o, thv0top_o, thvl0bot_o, thvl0top_o,             &
   935)                                         ssthl0_o , ssqt0_o  , ssu0_o    , ssv0_o    , qc_o    ,   &
   936)                                         qtten_o  , slten_o  
   937)     real(r8), dimension(0:mkx)       :: umf_o    , slflx_o  , qtflx_o   , ufrc_o 
   938)     real(r8), dimension(mix)         :: cush_o   , precip_o , snow_o    , rliq_o, cbmf_o, cnt_o, cnb_o
   939)     real(r8), dimension(0:mkx)       :: uflx_o   , vflx_o
   940)     real(r8)                         :: tkeavg_o , thvlmin_o, qtsrc_o  , thvlsrc_o, thlsrc_o ,    &
   941)                                         usrc_o   , vsrc_o   , plcl_o   , plfc_o   ,               &
   942)                                         thv0lcl_o, cinlcl_o 
   943)     integer                          :: kinv_o   , klcl_o   , klfc_o  
   944) 
   945)     real(r8), dimension(mkx,ncnst)   :: tr0_o
   946)     real(r8), dimension(mkx,ncnst)   :: trten_o, sstr0_o  
   947)     real(r8), dimension(0:mkx,ncnst) :: trflx_o
   948)     real(r8), dimension(ncnst)       :: trsrc_o
   949)     integer                          :: ixnumliq, ixnumice, ixcldliq, ixcldice
   950) 
   951)     ! ------------------ !
   952)     !                    !
   953)     ! Define Parameters  !
   954)     !                    !
   955)     ! ------------------ !
   956) 
   957)     ! ------------------------ !
   958)     ! Iterative xc calculation !
   959)     ! ------------------------ !
   960) 
   961)     integer , parameter              :: niter_xc = 2
   962) 
   963)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------- !
   964)     ! Choice of 'CIN = cin' (.true.) or 'CIN = cinlcl' (.false.). !
   965)     !                                                             !
   966)     ! Feb 2007, Bundy: Note that use_CINcin = .false. will try to !
   967)     ! use a variable (del_cinlcl) that is not currently set       !
   968)     !                                                             !
   969)     ! Sept 2012, Santos: The fact that this is still true over 5  !
   970)     ! years later suggests that this option needs to be           !
   971)     ! fixed or abandoned.                                         !
   972)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------- !
   973) 
   974)     logical , parameter              :: use_CINcin = .true.
   975) 
   976)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------- !
   977)     ! Choice of 'explicit' ( 1 ) or 'implicit' ( 2 )  CIN.            !
   978)     !                                                                 !
   979)     ! When choose 'CIN = cinlcl' above,  it is recommended not to use ! 
   980)     ! implicit CIN, i.e., do 'NOT' choose simultaneously :            !
   981)     !            [ 'use_CINcin=.false. & 'iter_cin=2' ]               !
   982)     ! since 'cinlcl' will be always set to zero whenever LCL is below !
   983)     ! the PBL top interface in the current code. So, averaging cinlcl !
   984)     ! of two iter_cin steps is likely not so good. Except that,   all !
   985)     ! the other combinations of  'use_CINcin'  & 'iter_cin' are OK.   !
   986)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------- !
   987) 
   988)     integer , parameter              :: iter_cin = 2
   989) 
   990)     ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
   991)     ! Choice of 'self-detrainment' by negative buoyancy in calculating !
   992)     ! cumulus updraft mass flux at the top interface in each layer.    !
   993)     ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
   994) 
   995)     logical , parameter              :: use_self_detrain = .false.
   996)     
   997)     ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
   998)     ! Cumulus momentum flux : turn-on (.true.) or off (.false.) !
   999)     ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  1000) 
  1001)     logical , parameter              :: use_momenflx = .true.
  1002) 
  1003)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1004)     ! Penetrative Entrainment : Cumulative ( .true. , original ) or Non-Cumulative ( .false. )  !
  1005)     ! This option ( .false. ) is designed to reduce the sensitivity to the vertical resolution. !
  1006)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1007) 
  1008)     logical , parameter              :: use_cumpenent = .true.
  1009) 
  1010)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1011)     ! Computation of the grid-mean condensate tendency.                                                               !
  1012)     !     use_expconten = .true.  : explcitly compute tendency by condensate detrainment and compensating subsidence  !
  1013)     !     use_expconten = .false. : use the original proportional condensate tendency equation. ( original )          !
  1014)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1015) 
  1016)     logical , parameter              :: use_expconten = .true.
  1017) 
  1018)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1019)     ! Treatment of reserved condensate                                                                                !
  1020)     !     use_unicondet = .true.  : detrain condensate uniformly over the environment ( original )                    !
  1021)     !     use_unicondet = .false. : detrain condensate into the pre-existing stratus                                  !
  1022)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1023) 
  1024)     logical , parameter              :: use_unicondet = .false.
  1025) 
  1026)     ! ----------------------- !
  1027)     ! For lateral entrainment !
  1028)     ! ----------------------- !
  1029) 
  1030)     parameter (rle = 0.1_r8)         !  For critical stopping distance for lateral entrainment [no unit]
  1031) !   parameter (rkm = 16.0_r8)        !  Determine the amount of air that is involved in buoyancy-sorting [no unit] 
  1032)     parameter (rkm = 14.0_r8)        !  Determine the amount of air that is involved in buoyancy-sorting [no unit]
  1033) 
  1034)     parameter (rkfre = 1.0_r8)       !  Vertical velocity variance as fraction of  tke. 
  1035)     parameter (rmaxfrac = 0.10_r8)   !  Maximum allowable 'core' updraft fraction
  1036)     parameter (mumin1 = 0.906_r8)    !  Normalized CIN ('mu') corresponding to 'rmaxfrac' at the PBL top
  1037)                                      !  obtaind by inverting 'rmaxfrac = 0.5*erfc(mumin1)'.
  1038)                                      !  [rmaxfrac:mumin1]=[ 0.05:1.163, 0.075:1.018, 0.1:0.906, 0.15:0.733, 0.2:0.595, 0.25:0.477]
  1039)     parameter (rbuoy = 1.0_r8)       !  For nonhydrostatic pressure effects on updraft [no unit]
  1040)     parameter (rdrag = 1.0_r8)       !  Drag coefficient [no unit]
  1041) 
  1042)     parameter (epsvarw = 5.e-4_r8)   !  Variance of w at PBL top by meso-scale component [m2/s2]          
  1043)     parameter (PGFc = 0.7_r8)        !  This is used for calculating vertical variations cumulus  
  1044)                                      !  'u' & 'v' by horizontal PGF during upward motion [no unit]
  1045) 
  1046)     ! ---------------------------------------- !
  1047)     ! Bulk microphysics controlling parameters !
  1048)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1049)     ! criqc    : Maximum condensate that can be hold by cumulus updraft [kg/kg]   !
  1050)     ! frc_rasn : Fraction of precipitable condensate in the expelled cloud water  !
  1051)     !            from cumulus updraft. The remaining fraction ('1-frc_rasn')  is  !
  1052)     !            'suspended condensate'.                                          !
  1053)     !                0 : all expelled condensate is 'suspended condensate'        ! 
  1054)     !                1 : all expelled condensate is 'precipitable condensate'     !
  1055)     ! kevp     : Evaporative efficiency                                           !
  1056)     ! noevap_krelkpen : No evaporation from 'krel' to 'kpen' layers               ! 
  1057)     ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !    
  1058) 
  1059)     parameter ( criqc    = 0.7e-3_r8 ) 
  1060)     parameter ( frc_rasn = 1.0_r8    )
  1061)     parameter ( kevp     = 2.e-6_r8  )
  1062)     logical, parameter :: noevap_krelkpen = .false.
  1063) 
  1064)     !------------------------!
  1065)     !                        !
  1066)     ! Start Main Calculation !
  1067)     !                        !
  1068)     !------------------------!
  1069) 
  1070)     call cnst_get_ind( 'NUMLIQ', ixnumliq )
  1071)     call cnst_get_ind( 'NUMICE', ixnumice )
  1072) 
  1073)     call cnst_get_ind( 'CLDLIQ', ixcldliq )
  1074)     call cnst_get_ind( 'CLDICE', ixcldice )
  1075) 
  1076) 
  1077) 
  1078) 
  1079)     ! ------------------------------------------------------- !
  1080)     ! Initialize output variables defined for all grid points !
  1081)     ! ------------------------------------------------------- !
  1082) 
  1083)     umf_out(:iend,0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1084)     slflx_out(:iend,0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8
  1085)     qtflx_out(:iend,0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8

  1087)     flxsnow1_out(:iend,0:mkx)    = 0.0_r8

  1089)     qlten_out(:iend,:mkx)        = 0.0_r8

  1118) 
  1119)     trten_out(:iend,:mkx,:ncnst) = 0.0_r8
  1120)     trflx_out(:iend,0:mkx,:ncnst)= 0.0_r8
  1121)     
  1122)     ufrcinvbase_out(:iend)       = 0.0_r8
  1123)     ufrclcl_out(:iend)           = 0.0_r8
  1124)     winvbase_out(:iend)          = 0.0_r8

  1176)     exit_klfcmkx(:iend)          = 0.0_r8 
  1177)     exit_ufrc(:iend)             = 0.0_r8 
  1178)     exit_wtw(:iend)              = 0.0_r8 
  1179)     exit_drycore(:iend)          = 0.0_r8

  1186)     limit_negcon(:iend)          = 0.0_r8 
  1187)     limit_ufrc(:iend)            = 0.0_r8
  1188)     limit_ppen(:iend)            = 0.0_r8
  1189)     limit_emf(:iend)             = 0.0_r8
  1190)     limit_cinlcl(:iend)          = 0.0_r8
  1191)     limit_cin(:iend)             = 0.0_r8
  1192)     limit_cbmf(:iend)            = 0.0_r8
  1193)     limit_rei(:iend)             = 0.0_r8
  1194) 
  1195)     ind_delcin(:iend)            = 0.0_r8
  1196) 
  1197)     !--------------------------------------------------------------!
  1198)     !                                                              !
  1199)     ! Start the column i loop where i is a horizontal column index !
  1200)     !                                                              !
  1201)     !--------------------------------------------------------------!
  1202) 
  1203)     ! Compute wet-bulb temperature and specific humidity
  1204)     ! for treating evaporation of precipitation.
  1205) 
  1206)     ! "True" means ice will be taken into account
  1207)     do k = 1, mkx
  1208)        call findsp_vc(qv0_in(:iend,k), t0_in(:iend,k), p0_in(:iend,k), .true., &
  1209)             tw0_in(:iend,k), qw0_in(:iend,k))
  1210)     end do
  1211) 
  1212)     do i = 1, iend                                      
  1213) 
  1214)       id_exit = .false.
  1215) 
  1216)       ! -------------------------------------------- !
  1217)       ! Define 1D input variables at each grid point !
  1218)       ! -------------------------------------------- !
  1219) 
  1220)       ps0(0:mkx)       = ps0_in(i,0:mkx)
  1221)       zs0(0:mkx)       = zs0_in(i,0:mkx)
  1222)       p0(:mkx)         = p0_in(i,:mkx)
  1223)       z0(:mkx)         = z0_in(i,:mkx)
  1224)       dp0(:mkx)        = dp0_in(i,:mkx)
  1225)       dpdry0(:mkx)     = dpdry0_in(i,:mkx)
  1226)       u0(:mkx)         = u0_in(i,:mkx)
  1227)       v0(:mkx)         = v0_in(i,:mkx)
  1228)       qv0(:mkx)        = qv0_in(i,:mkx)
  1229)       ql0(:mkx)        = ql0_in(i,:mkx)
  1230)       qi0(:mkx)        = qi0_in(i,:mkx)
  1231)       t0(:mkx)         = t0_in(i,:mkx)
  1232)       s0(:mkx)         = s0_in(i,:mkx)
  1233)       tke(0:mkx)       = tke_in(i,0:mkx)
  1234)       cldfrct(:mkx)    = cldfrct_in(i,:mkx)
  1235)       concldfrct(:mkx) = concldfrct_in(i,:mkx)
  1236)       pblh             = pblh_in(i)
  1237)       cush             = cush_inout(i)
  1238)       do m = 1, ncnst
  1239)          tr0(:mkx,m)   = tr0_in(i,:mkx,m)
  1240)       enddo
  1241) 
  1242)       ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  1243)       ! Compute other basic thermodynamic variables directly from ! 
  1244)       ! the input variables at each grid point                    !
  1245)       ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  1246) 
  1247)       !----- 1. Compute internal environmental variables
  1248)       
  1249)       exn0(:mkx)   = (p0(:mkx)/p00)**rovcp
  1250)       exns0(0:mkx) = (ps0(0:mkx)/p00)**rovcp
  1251)       qt0(:mkx)    = (qv0(:mkx) + ql0(:mkx) + qi0(:mkx))
  1252)       thl0(:mkx)   = (t0(:mkx) - xlv*ql0(:mkx)/cp - xls*qi0(:mkx)/cp)/exn0(:mkx)
  1253)       thvl0(:mkx)  = (1._r8 + zvir*qt0(:mkx))*thl0(:mkx)
  1254) 
  1255)       !----- 2. Compute slopes of environmental variables in each layer
  1256)       !         Dimension of ssthl0(:mkx) is implicit.
  1257) 
  1258)       ssthl0       = slope(mkx,thl0,p0) 
  1259)       ssqt0        = slope(mkx,qt0 ,p0)
  1260)       ssu0         = slope(mkx,u0  ,p0)
  1261)       ssv0         = slope(mkx,v0  ,p0)
  1262)       do m = 1, ncnst
  1263)          sstr0(:mkx,m) = slope(mkx,tr0(:mkx,m),p0)
  1264)       enddo     
  1265)  
  1266)       !----- 3. Compute "thv0" and "thvl0" at the top/bottom interfaces in each layer
  1267)       !         There are computed from the reconstructed thl, qt at the top/bottom.
  1268) 
  1269)       do k = 1, mkx
  1270) 
  1271)          thl0bot = thl0(k) + ssthl0(k)*(ps0(k-1) - p0(k))
  1272)          qt0bot  = qt0(k)  + ssqt0(k) *(ps0(k-1) - p0(k))
  1273)          call conden(ps0(k-1),thl0bot,qt0bot,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1274)          if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1275)              exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1276)              id_exit = .true.
  1277)              go to 333
  1278)          end if
  1279)          thv0bot(k)  = thj*(1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij)
  1280)          thvl0bot(k) = thl0bot*(1._r8 + zvir*qt0bot)
  1281)           
  1282)          thl0top = thl0(k) + ssthl0(k)*(ps0(k) - p0(k))
  1283)          qt0top  =  qt0(k) + ssqt0(k) *(ps0(k) - p0(k))
  1284)          call conden(ps0(k),thl0top,qt0top,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1285)          if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1286)              exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1287)              id_exit = .true.
  1288)              go to 333
  1289)          end if 
  1290)          thv0top(k)  = thj*(1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij)
  1291)          thvl0top(k) = thl0top*(1._r8 + zvir*qt0top)
  1292) 
  1293)       end do
  1294) 
  1295)       ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1296)       ! Save input and related environmental thermodynamic variables !
  1297)       ! for use at "iter_cin=2" when "del_CIN >= 0"                  !
  1298)       ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1299) 
  1300)       qv0_o(:mkx)          = qv0(:mkx)
  1301)       ql0_o(:mkx)          = ql0(:mkx)
  1302)       qi0_o(:mkx)          = qi0(:mkx)
  1303)       t0_o(:mkx)           = t0(:mkx)
  1304)       s0_o(:mkx)           = s0(:mkx)
  1305)       u0_o(:mkx)           = u0(:mkx)
  1306)       v0_o(:mkx)           = v0(:mkx)
  1307)       qt0_o(:mkx)          = qt0(:mkx)
  1308)       thl0_o(:mkx)         = thl0(:mkx)
  1309)       thvl0_o(:mkx)        = thvl0(:mkx)
  1310)       ssthl0_o(:mkx)       = ssthl0(:mkx)
  1311)       ssqt0_o(:mkx)        = ssqt0(:mkx)
  1312)       thv0bot_o(:mkx)      = thv0bot(:mkx)
  1313)       thv0top_o(:mkx)      = thv0top(:mkx)
  1314)       thvl0bot_o(:mkx)     = thvl0bot(:mkx)
  1315)       thvl0top_o(:mkx)     = thvl0top(:mkx)
  1316)       ssu0_o(:mkx)         = ssu0(:mkx) 
  1317)       ssv0_o(:mkx)         = ssv0(:mkx) 
  1318)       do m = 1, ncnst
  1319)          tr0_o(:mkx,m)     = tr0(:mkx,m)
  1320)          sstr0_o(:mkx,m)   = sstr0(:mkx,m)
  1321)       enddo 
  1322) 
  1323)       ! ---------------------------------------------- !
  1324)       ! Initialize output variables at each grid point !
  1325)       ! ---------------------------------------------- !
  1326) 
  1327)       umf(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1328)       emf(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1329)       slflx(0:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1330)       qtflx(0:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1331)       uflx(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1332)       vflx(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1333)       qvten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1334)       qlten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1335)       qiten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1336)       sten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1337)       uten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1338)       vten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1339)       qrten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1340)       qsten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1341)       dwten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1342)       diten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1343)       precip              = 0.0_r8
  1344)       snow                = 0.0_r8
  1345)       evapc(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1346)       cufrc(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1347)       qcu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1348)       qlu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1349)       qiu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1350)       fer(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1351)       fdr(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1352)       cin                 = 0.0_r8
  1353)       cbmf                = 0.0_r8
  1354)       qc(:mkx)            = 0.0_r8
  1355)       qc_l(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1356)       qc_i(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1357)       rliq                = 0.0_r8
  1358)       cnt                 = real(mkx, r8)
  1359)       cnb                 = 0.0_r8
  1360)       qtten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1361)       slten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8   
  1362)       ufrc(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8  
  1363) 
  1364)       thlu(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1365)       qtu(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1366)       uu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1367)       vu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1368)       wu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1369)       thvu(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1370)       thlu_emf(0:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1371)       qtu_emf(0:mkx)      = 0.0_r8
  1372)       uu_emf(0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8
  1373)       vu_emf(0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8
  1374)       
  1375)       ufrcinvbase         = 0.0_r8
  1376)       ufrclcl             = 0.0_r8
  1377)       winvbase            = 0.0_r8
  1378)       wlcl                = 0.0_r8
  1379)       emfkbup             = 0.0_r8 
  1380)       cbmflimit           = 0.0_r8
  1381)       excessu_arr(:mkx)   = 0.0_r8
  1382)       excess0_arr(:mkx)   = 0.0_r8
  1383)       xc_arr(:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1384)       aquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1385)       bquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1386)       cquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1387)       bogbot_arr(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1388)       bogtop_arr(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1389) 
  1390)       uemf(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1391)       comsub(:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1392)       qlten_sink(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1393)       qiten_sink(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8 
  1394)       nlten_sink(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1395)       niten_sink(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8 
  1396) 
  1397)       do m = 1, ncnst
  1398)          trflx(0:mkx,m)   = 0.0_r8
  1399)          trten(:mkx,m)    = 0.0_r8
  1400)          tru(0:mkx,m)     = 0.0_r8
  1401)          tru_emf(0:mkx,m) = 0.0_r8
  1402)       enddo
  1403) 
  1404)     !-----------------------------------------------! 
  1405)     ! Below 'iter' loop is for implicit CIN closure !
  1406)     !-----------------------------------------------!
  1407) 
  1408)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1409)     ! It is important to note that this iterative cin loop is located at the outest !
  1410)     ! shell of the code. Thus, source air properties can also be changed during the !
  1411)     ! iterative cin calculation, because cumulus convection induces non-zero fluxes !
  1412)     ! even at interfaces below PBL top height through 'fluxbelowinv' subroutine.    !
  1413)     ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1414) 
  1415)     do iter = 1, iter_cin
  1416) 
  1417)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1418)        ! Cumulus scale height                                                   ! 
  1419)        ! In contrast to the premitive code, cumulus scale height is iteratively !
  1420)        ! calculated at each time step, and at each iterative cin step.          !
  1421)        ! It is not clear whether I should locate below two lines within or  out !
  1422)        ! of the iterative cin loop.                                             !
  1423)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1424) 
  1425)        tscaleh = cush                        
  1426)        cush    = -1._r8
  1427) 
  1428)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1429)        ! Find PBL top height interface index, 'kinv-1' where 'kinv' is the layer !
  1430)        ! index with PBLH in it. When PBLH is exactly at interface, 'kinv' is the !
  1431)        ! layer index having PBLH as a lower interface.                           !
  1432)        ! In the previous code, I set the lower limit of 'kinv' by 2  in order to !
  1433)        ! be consistent with the other parts of the code. However in the modified !
  1434)        ! code, I allowed 'kinv' to be 1 & if 'kinv = 1', I just exit the program !
  1435)        ! without performing cumulus convection. This new approach seems to be    !
  1436)        ! more reasonable: if PBL height is within 'kinv=1' layer, surface is STL !
  1437)        ! interface (bflxs <= 0) and interface just above the surface should be   !
  1438)        ! either non-turbulent (Ri>0.19) or stably turbulent (0<=Ri<0.19 but this !
  1439)        ! interface is identified as a base external interface of upperlying CL.  !
  1440)        ! Thus, when 'kinv=1', PBL scheme guarantees 'bflxs <= 0'.  For this case !
  1441)        ! it is reasonable to assume that cumulus convection does not happen.     !
  1442)        ! When these is SBCL, PBL height from the PBL scheme is likely to be very !
  1443)        ! close at 'kinv-1' interface, but not exactly, since 'zi' information is !
  1444)        ! changed between two model time steps. In order to ensure correct identi !
  1445)        ! fication of 'kinv' for general case including SBCL, I imposed an offset !
  1446)        ! of 5 [m] in the below 'kinv' finding block.                             !
  1447)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1448)        
  1449)        do k = mkx - 1, 1, -1 
  1450)           if( (pblh + 5._r8 - zs0(k))*(pblh + 5._r8 - zs0(k+1)) .lt. 0._r8 ) then
  1451)                kinv = k + 1 
  1452)                go to 15
  1453)           endif 
  1454)        end do
  1455)        kinv = 1
  1456) 15     continue    
  1457) 
  1458)        if( kinv .le. 1 ) then          
  1459)            exit_kinv1(i) = 1._r8
  1460)            id_exit = .true.
  1461)            go to 333
  1462)        endif
  1463)        ! From here, it must be 'kinv >= 2'.
  1464) 
  1465)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1466)        ! Find PBL averaged tke ('tkeavg') and minimum 'thvl' ('thvlmin') in the PBL !
  1467)        ! In the current code, 'tkeavg' is obtained by averaging all interfacial TKE !
  1468)        ! within the PBL. However, in order to be conceptually consistent with   PBL !
  1469)        ! scheme, 'tkeavg' should be calculated by considering surface buoyancy flux.!
  1470)        ! If surface buoyancy flux is positive ( bflxs >0 ), surface interfacial TKE !
  1471)        ! should be included in calculating 'tkeavg', while if bflxs <= 0,   surface !
  1472)        ! interfacial TKE should not be included in calculating 'tkeavg'.   I should !
  1473)        ! modify the code when 'bflxs' is available as an input of cumulus scheme.   !
  1474)        ! 'thvlmin' is a minimum 'thvl' within PBL obtained by comparing top &  base !
  1475)        ! interface values of 'thvl' in each layers within the PBL.                  !
  1476)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1477)        
  1478)        dpsum    = 0._r8
  1479)        tkeavg   = 0._r8
  1480)        thvlmin  = 1000._r8
  1481)        do k = 0, kinv - 1   ! Here, 'k' is an interfacial layer index.  
  1482)           if( k .eq. 0 ) then
  1483)               dpi = ps0(0) - p0(1)
  1484)           elseif( k .eq. (kinv-1) ) then 
  1485)               dpi = p0(kinv-1) - ps0(kinv-1)
  1486)           else
  1487)               dpi = p0(k) - p0(k+1)
  1488)           endif 
  1489)           dpsum  = dpsum  + dpi  
  1490)           tkeavg = tkeavg + dpi*tke(k) 
  1491)           if( k .ne. 0 ) thvlmin = min(thvlmin,min(thvl0bot(k),thvl0top(k)))
  1492)        end do
  1493)        tkeavg  = tkeavg/dpsum
  1494) 
  1495)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1496)        ! Find characteristics of cumulus source air: qtsrc,thlsrc,usrc,vsrc !
  1497)        ! Note that 'thlsrc' was con-cocked using 'thvlsrc' and 'qtsrc'.     !
  1498)        ! 'qtsrc' is defined as the lowest layer mid-point value;   'thlsrc' !
  1499)        ! is from 'qtsrc' and 'thvlmin=thvlsrc'; 'usrc' & 'vsrc' are defined !
  1500)        ! as the values just below the PBL top interface.                    !
  1501)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1502) 
  1503)        qtsrc   = qt0(1)                     
  1504)        thvlsrc = thvlmin 
  1505)        thlsrc  = thvlsrc / ( 1._r8 + zvir * qtsrc )  
  1506)        usrc    = u0(kinv-1) + ssu0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )             
  1507)        vsrc    = v0(kinv-1) + ssv0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )             
  1508)        do m = 1, ncnst
  1509)           trsrc(m) = tr0(1,m)
  1510)        enddo 
  1511) 
  1512)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1513)        ! Find LCL of the source air and a layer index containing LCL (klcl) !
  1514)        ! When the LCL is exactly at the interface, 'klcl' is a layer index  ! 
  1515)        ! having 'plcl' as the lower interface similar to the 'kinv' case.   !
  1516)        ! In the previous code, I assumed that if LCL is located within the  !
  1517)        ! lowest model layer ( 1 ) or the top model layer ( mkx ), then  no  !
  1518)        ! convective adjustment is performed and just exited.   However, in  !
  1519)        ! the revised code, I relaxed the first constraint and  even though  !
  1520)        ! LCL is at the lowest model layer, I allowed cumulus convection to  !
  1521)        ! be initiated. For this case, cumulus convection should be started  !
  1522)        ! from the PBL top height, as shown in the following code.           !
  1523)        ! When source air is already saturated even at the surface, klcl is  !
  1524)        ! set to 1.                                                          !
  1525)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1526) 
  1527)        plcl = qsinvert(qtsrc,thlsrc,ps0(0))
  1528)        do k = 0, mkx
  1529)           if( ps0(k) .lt. plcl ) then
  1530)               klcl = k
  1531)               go to 25
  1532)           endif           
  1533)        end do
  1534)        klcl = mkx
  1535) 25     continue
  1536)        klcl = max(1,klcl)
  1537)      
  1538)        if( plcl .lt. 30000._r8 ) then               
  1539)      ! if( klcl .eq. mkx ) then          
  1540)            exit_klclmkx(i) = 1._r8
  1541)            id_exit = .true.
  1542)            go to 333
  1543)        endif
  1544) 
  1545)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1546)        ! Calculate environmental virtual potential temperature at LCL, !
  1547)        !'thv0lcl' which is solely used in the 'cin' calculation. Note  !
  1548)        ! that 'thv0lcl' is calculated first by calculating  'thl0lcl'  !
  1549)        ! and 'qt0lcl' at the LCL, and performing 'conden' afterward,   !
  1550)        ! in fully consistent with the other parts of the code.         !
  1551)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1552) 
  1553)        thl0lcl = thl0(klcl) + ssthl0(klcl) * ( plcl - p0(klcl) )
  1554)        qt0lcl  = qt0(klcl)  + ssqt0(klcl)  * ( plcl - p0(klcl) )
  1555)        call conden(plcl,thl0lcl,qt0lcl,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1556)        if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1557)            exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1558)            id_exit = .true.
  1559)            go to 333
  1560)        end if
  1561)        thv0lcl = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir * qvj - qlj - qij )
  1562) 
  1563)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1564)        ! Compute Convective Inhibition, 'cin' & 'cinlcl' [J/kg]=[m2/s2] TKE unit. !
  1565)        !                                                                          !
  1566)        ! 'cin' (cinlcl) is computed from the PBL top interface to LFC (LCL) using ! 
  1567)        ! piecewisely reconstructed environmental profiles, assuming environmental !
  1568)        ! buoyancy profile within each layer ( or from LCL to upper interface in   !
  1569)        ! each layer ) is simply a linear profile. For the purpose of cin (cinlcl) !
  1570)        ! calculation, we simply assume that lateral entrainment does not occur in !
  1571)        ! updrafting cumulus plume, i.e., cumulus source air property is conserved.!
  1572)        ! Below explains some rules used in the calculations of cin (cinlcl).   In !
  1573)        ! general, both 'cin' and 'cinlcl' are calculated from a PBL top interface !
  1574)        ! to LCL and LFC, respectively :                                           !
  1575)        ! 1. If LCL is lower than the PBL height, cinlcl = 0 and cin is calculated !
  1576)        !    from PBL height to LFC.                                               !
