  1577)        ! 2. If LCL is higher than PBL height,   'cinlcl' is calculated by summing !
  1578)        !    both positive and negative cloud buoyancy up to LCL using 'single_cin'!
  1579)        !    From the LCL to LFC, however, only negative cloud buoyancy is counted !
  1580)        !    to calculate final 'cin' upto LFC.                                    !
  1581)        ! 3. If either 'cin' or 'cinlcl' is negative, they are set to be zero.     !
  1582)        ! In the below code, 'klfc' is the layer index containing 'LFC' similar to !
  1583)        ! 'kinv' and 'klcl'.                                                       !
  1584)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  1585) 
  1586)         cin    = 0._r8
  1587)         cinlcl = 0._r8
  1588)         plfc   = 0._r8
  1589)         klfc   = mkx
  1590) 
  1591)         ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1592)         ! Case 1. LCL height is higher than PBL interface ( 'pLCL <= ps0(kinv-1)' ) !
  1593)         ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1594) 
  1595)         if( klcl .ge. kinv ) then
  1596) 
  1597)             do k = kinv, mkx - 1
  1598)                if( k .lt. klcl ) then
  1599)                    thvubot = thvlsrc
  1600)                    thvutop = thvlsrc  
  1601)                    cin     = cin + single_cin(ps0(k-1),thv0bot(k),ps0(k),thv0top(k),thvubot,thvutop)
  1602)                elseif( k .eq. klcl ) then
  1603)                    !----- Bottom to LCL
  1604)                    thvubot = thvlsrc
  1605)                    thvutop = thvlsrc
  1606)                    cin     = cin + single_cin(ps0(k-1),thv0bot(k),plcl,thv0lcl,thvubot,thvutop)
  1607)                    if( cin .lt. 0._r8 ) limit_cinlcl(i) = 1._r8
  1608)                    cinlcl  = max(cin,0._r8)
  1609)                    cin     = cinlcl
  1610)                    !----- LCL to Top
  1611)                    thvubot = thvlsrc
  1612)                    call conden(ps0(k),thlsrc,qtsrc,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1613)                    if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1614)                        exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1615)                        id_exit = .true.
  1616)                        go to 333
  1617)                    end if
  1618)                    thvutop = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )
  1619)                    call getbuoy(plcl,thv0lcl,ps0(k),thv0top(k),thvubot,thvutop,plfc,cin)
  1620)                    if( plfc .gt. 0._r8 ) then 
  1621)                        klfc = k 
  1622)                        go to 35
  1623)                    end if
  1624)                else
  1625)                    thvubot = thvutop
  1626)                    call conden(ps0(k),thlsrc,qtsrc,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1627)                    if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1628)                        exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1629)                        id_exit = .true.
  1630)                        go to 333
  1631)                    end if
  1632)                    thvutop = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )
  1633)                    call getbuoy(ps0(k-1),thv0bot(k),ps0(k),thv0top(k),thvubot,thvutop,plfc,cin)
  1634)                    if( plfc .gt. 0._r8 ) then 
  1635)                        klfc = k
  1636)                        go to 35
  1637)                    end if 
  1638)                endif
  1639)             end do        
  1640) 
  1641)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1642)        ! Case 2. LCL height is lower than PBL interface ( 'pLCL > ps0(kinv-1)' ) !
  1643)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1644) 
  1645)        else
  1646)           cinlcl = 0._r8 
  1647)           do k = kinv, mkx - 1
  1648)              call conden(ps0(k-1),thlsrc,qtsrc,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1649)              if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1650)                  exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1651)                  id_exit = .true.
  1652)                  go to 333
  1653)              end if
  1654)              thvubot = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )
  1655)              call conden(ps0(k),thlsrc,qtsrc,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  1656)              if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  1657)                  exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  1658)                  id_exit = .true.
  1659)                  go to 333
  1660)              end if
  1661)              thvutop = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )
  1662)              call getbuoy(ps0(k-1),thv0bot(k),ps0(k),thv0top(k),thvubot,thvutop,plfc,cin)
  1663)              if( plfc .gt. 0._r8 ) then 
  1664)                  klfc = k
  1665)                  go to 35
  1666)              end if 
  1667)           end do
  1668)        endif  ! End of CIN case selection
  1669) 
  1670)  35    continue
  1671)        if( cin .lt. 0._r8 ) limit_cin(i) = 1._r8
  1672)        cin = max(0._r8,cin)
  1673)        if( klfc .ge. mkx ) then
  1674)            klfc = mkx
  1675)          ! write(iulog,*) 'klfc >= mkx'
  1676)            exit_klfcmkx(i) = 1._r8
  1677)            id_exit = .true.
  1678)            go to 333
  1679)        endif
  1680) 
  1681)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1682)        ! In order to calculate implicit 'cin' (or 'cinlcl'), save the initially !
  1683)        ! calculated 'cin' and 'cinlcl', and other related variables. These will !
  1684)        ! be restored after calculating implicit CIN.                            !
  1685)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1686) 
  1687)        if( iter .eq. 1 ) then 
  1688)            cin_i       = cin
  1689)            cinlcl_i    = cinlcl
  1690)            ke          = rbuoy / ( rkfre * tkeavg + epsvarw ) 
  1691)            kinv_o      = kinv     
  1692)            klcl_o      = klcl     
  1693)            klfc_o      = klfc    
  1694)            plcl_o      = plcl    
  1695)            plfc_o      = plfc     
  1696)            tkeavg_o    = tkeavg   
  1697)            thvlmin_o   = thvlmin
  1698)            qtsrc_o     = qtsrc    
  1699)            thvlsrc_o   = thvlsrc  
  1700)            thlsrc_o    = thlsrc
  1701)            usrc_o      = usrc     
  1702)            vsrc_o      = vsrc     
  1703)            thv0lcl_o   = thv0lcl  
  1704)            do m = 1, ncnst
  1705)               trsrc_o(m) = trsrc(m)
  1706)            enddo
  1707)        endif   
  1708) 
  1709)      ! Modification : If I impose w = max(0.1_r8, w) up to the top interface of
  1710)      !                klfc, I should only use cinlfc.  That is, if I want to
  1711)      !                use cinlcl, I should not impose w = max(0.1_r8, w).
  1712)      !                Using cinlcl is equivalent to treating only 'saturated'
  1713)      !                moist convection. Note that in this sense, I should keep
  1714)      !                the functionality of both cinlfc and cinlcl.
  1715)      !                However, the treatment of penetrative entrainment level becomes
  1716)      !                ambiguous if I choose 'cinlcl'. Thus, the best option is to use
  1717)      !                'cinlfc'.
  1718) 
  1719)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1720)        ! Calculate implicit 'cin' by averaging initial and final cins.    Note that !
  1721)        ! implicit CIN is adopted only when cumulus convection stabilized the system,!
  1722)        ! i.e., only when 'del_CIN >0'. If 'del_CIN<=0', just use explicit CIN. Note !
  1723)        ! also that since 'cinlcl' is set to zero whenever LCL is below the PBL top, !
  1724)        ! (see above CIN calculation part), the use of 'implicit CIN=cinlcl'  is not !
  1725)        ! good. Thus, when using implicit CIN, always try to only use 'implicit CIN= !
  1726)        ! cin', not 'implicit CIN=cinlcl'. However, both 'CIN=cin' and 'CIN=cinlcl'  !
  1727)        ! are good when using explicit CIN.                                          !
  1728)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1729) 
  1730)        if( iter .ne. 1 ) then
  1731) 
  1732)            cin_f = cin
  1733)            cinlcl_f = cinlcl
  1734)            if( use_CINcin ) then
  1735)                del_CIN = cin_f - cin_i
  1736)            else
  1737)                del_CIN = cinlcl_f - cinlcl_i
  1738)            endif
  1739) 
  1740)            if( del_CIN .gt. 0._r8 ) then
  1741) 
  1742)                ! -------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1743)                ! Calculate implicit 'cin' and 'cinlcl'. Note that when we chose !
  1744)                ! to use 'implicit CIN = cin', choose 'cinlcl = cinlcl_i' below: !
  1745)                ! because iterative CIN only aims to obtain implicit CIN,  once  !
  1746)                ! we obtained 'implicit CIN=cin', it is good to use the original !
  1747)                ! profiles information for all the other variables after that.   !
  1748)                ! Note 'cinlcl' will be explicitly used in calculating  'wlcl' & !
  1749)                ! 'ufrclcl' after calculating 'winv' & 'ufrcinv'  at the PBL top !
  1750)                ! interface later, after calculating 'cbmf'.                     !
  1751)                ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1752)          
  1753)                alpha = compute_alpha( del_CIN, ke ) 
  1754)                cin   = cin_i + alpha * del_CIN
  1755)                if( use_CINcin ) then
  1756)                    cinlcl = cinlcl_i                 
  1757)                else
  1758)                    cinlcl = cinlcl_i + alpha * del_cinlcl   
  1759)                endif
  1760) 
  1761)                ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1762)                ! Restore the original values from the previous 'iter_cin' step (1) !
  1763)                ! to compute correct tendencies for (n+1) time step by implicit CIN !
  1764)                ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  1765) 
  1766)                kinv      = kinv_o     
  1767)                klcl      = klcl_o     
  1768)                klfc      = klfc_o    
  1769)                plcl      = plcl_o    
  1770)                plfc      = plfc_o     
  1771)                tkeavg    = tkeavg_o   
  1772)                thvlmin   = thvlmin_o
  1773)                qtsrc     = qtsrc_o    
  1774)                thvlsrc   = thvlsrc_o  
  1775)                thlsrc    = thlsrc_o
  1776)                usrc      = usrc_o     
  1777)                vsrc      = vsrc_o     
  1778)                thv0lcl   = thv0lcl_o  
  1779)                do m = 1, ncnst
  1780)                   trsrc(m) = trsrc_o(m)
  1781)                enddo
  1782) 
  1783)                qv0(:mkx)            = qv0_o(:mkx)
  1784)                ql0(:mkx)            = ql0_o(:mkx)
  1785)                qi0(:mkx)            = qi0_o(:mkx)
  1786)                t0(:mkx)             = t0_o(:mkx)
  1787)                s0(:mkx)             = s0_o(:mkx)
  1788)                u0(:mkx)             = u0_o(:mkx)
  1789)                v0(:mkx)             = v0_o(:mkx)
  1790)                qt0(:mkx)            = qt0_o(:mkx)
  1791)                thl0(:mkx)           = thl0_o(:mkx)
  1792)                thvl0(:mkx)          = thvl0_o(:mkx)
  1793)                ssthl0(:mkx)         = ssthl0_o(:mkx)
  1794)                ssqt0(:mkx)          = ssqt0_o(:mkx)
  1795)                thv0bot(:mkx)        = thv0bot_o(:mkx)
  1796)                thv0top(:mkx)        = thv0top_o(:mkx)
  1797)                thvl0bot(:mkx)       = thvl0bot_o(:mkx)
  1798)                thvl0top(:mkx)       = thvl0top_o(:mkx)
  1799)                ssu0(:mkx)           = ssu0_o(:mkx) 
  1800)                ssv0(:mkx)           = ssv0_o(:mkx) 
  1801)                do m = 1, ncnst
  1802)                   tr0(:mkx,m)   = tr0_o(:mkx,m)
  1803)                   sstr0(:mkx,m) = sstr0_o(:mkx,m)
  1804)                enddo
  1805) 
  1806)                ! ------------------------------------------------------ !
  1807)                ! Initialize all fluxes, tendencies, and other variables ! 
  1808)                ! in association with cumulus convection.                !
  1809)                ! ------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  1810) 
  1811)                umf(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1812)                emf(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1813)                slflx(0:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1814)                qtflx(0:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1815)                uflx(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1816)                vflx(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1817)                qvten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1818)                qlten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1819)                qiten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1820)                sten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1821)                uten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1822)                vten(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1823)                qrten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1824)                qsten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1825)                dwten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1826)                diten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1827)                precip              = 0.0_r8
  1828)                snow                = 0.0_r8
  1829)                evapc(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1830)                cufrc(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1831)                qcu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1832)                qlu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1833)                qiu(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1834)                fer(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1835)                fdr(:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1836)                qc(:mkx)            = 0.0_r8
  1837)                qc_l(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1838)                qc_i(:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1839)                rliq                = 0.0_r8
  1840)                cbmf                = 0.0_r8
  1841)                cnt                 = real(mkx, r8)
  1842)                cnb                 = 0.0_r8
  1843)                qtten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1844)                slten(:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1845)                ufrc(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1846) 
  1847)                thlu(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1848)                qtu(0:mkx)          = 0.0_r8
  1849)                uu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1850)                vu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1851)                wu(0:mkx)           = 0.0_r8
  1852)                thvu(0:mkx)         = 0.0_r8
  1853)                thlu_emf(0:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1854)                qtu_emf(0:mkx)      = 0.0_r8
  1855)                uu_emf(0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8
  1856)                vu_emf(0:mkx)       = 0.0_r8
  1857)              
  1858)                do m = 1, ncnst
  1859)                   trflx(0:mkx,m)   = 0.0_r8
  1860)                   trten(:mkx,m)    = 0.0_r8
  1861)                   tru(0:mkx,m)     = 0.0_r8
  1862)                   tru_emf(0:mkx,m) = 0.0_r8
  1863)                enddo
  1864) 
  1865)                ! -------------------------------------------------- !
  1866)                ! Below are diagnostic output variables for detailed !
  1867)                ! analysis of cumulus scheme.                        !
  1868)                ! -------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1869) 
  1870)                ufrcinvbase         = 0.0_r8
  1871)                ufrclcl             = 0.0_r8
  1872)                winvbase            = 0.0_r8
  1873)                wlcl                = 0.0_r8
  1874)                emfkbup             = 0.0_r8 
  1875)                cbmflimit           = 0.0_r8
  1876)                excessu_arr(:mkx)   = 0.0_r8
  1877)                excess0_arr(:mkx)   = 0.0_r8
  1878)                xc_arr(:mkx)        = 0.0_r8
  1879)                aquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1880)                bquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1881)                cquad_arr(:mkx)     = 0.0_r8
  1882)                bogbot_arr(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1883)                bogtop_arr(:mkx)    = 0.0_r8
  1884) 
  1885)           else ! When 'del_CIN < 0', use explicit CIN instead of implicit CIN.
  1886)            
  1887)                ! ----------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1888)                ! Identifier showing whether explicit or implicit CIN is used !
  1889)                ! ----------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  1890) 
  1891)                ind_delcin(i) = 1._r8             
  1892)    
  1893)                ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  1894)                ! Restore original output values of "iter_cin = 1" and exit !
  1895)                ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  1896) 
  1897)                umf_out(i,0:mkx)         = umf_s(0:mkx)
  1898)                qvten_out(i,:mkx)        = qvten_s(:mkx)
  1899)                qlten_out(i,:mkx)        = qlten_s(:mkx)  
  1900)                qiten_out(i,:mkx)        = qiten_s(:mkx)
  1901)                sten_out(i,:mkx)         = sten_s(:mkx)
  1902)                uten_out(i,:mkx)         = uten_s(:mkx)  
  1903)                vten_out(i,:mkx)         = vten_s(:mkx)
  1904)                qrten_out(i,:mkx)        = qrten_s(:mkx)
  1905)                qsten_out(i,:mkx)        = qsten_s(:mkx)  
  1906)                precip_out(i)            = precip_s
  1907)                snow_out(i)              = snow_s
  1908)                evapc_out(i,:mkx)        = evapc_s(:mkx)
  1909)                cush_inout(i)            = cush_s
  1910)                cufrc_out(i,:mkx)        = cufrc_s(:mkx)  
  1911)                slflx_out(i,0:mkx)       = slflx_s(0:mkx)  
  1912)                qtflx_out(i,0:mkx)       = qtflx_s(0:mkx)
  1913)                qcu_out(i,:mkx)          = qcu_s(:mkx)    
  1914)                qlu_out(i,:mkx)          = qlu_s(:mkx)  
  1915)                qiu_out(i,:mkx)          = qiu_s(:mkx)  
  1916)                cbmf_out(i)              = cbmf_s
  1917)                qc_out(i,:mkx)           = qc_s(:mkx)  
  1918)                rliq_out(i)              = rliq_s
  1919)                cnt_out(i)               = cnt_s
  1920)                cnb_out(i)               = cnb_s
  1921)                do m = 1, ncnst
  1922)                   trten_out(i,:mkx,m)   = trten_s(:mkx,m)
  1923)                enddo  
  1924)              
  1925)                ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  1926)                ! Below are diagnostic output variables for detailed analysis of cumulus scheme. !
  1927)                ! The order of vertical index is reversed for this internal diagnostic output.   !
  1928)                ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !   
  1929) 
  1930)                fer_out(i,mkx:1:-1)      = fer_s(:mkx)  
  1931)                fdr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)      = fdr_s(:mkx)  
  1932)                cinh_out(i)              = cin_s
  1933)                cinlclh_out(i)           = cinlcl_s
  1934)                qtten_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = qtten_s(:mkx)
  1935)                slten_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = slten_s(:mkx)
  1936)                ufrc_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = ufrc_s(0:mkx)
  1937)                uflx_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = uflx_s(0:mkx)  
  1938)                vflx_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = vflx_s(0:mkx)  
  1939) 
  1940)                ufrcinvbase_out(i)       = ufrcinvbase_s
  1941)                ufrclcl_out(i)           = ufrclcl_s 
  1942)                winvbase_out(i)          = winvbase_s
  1943)                wlcl_out(i)              = wlcl_s
  1944)                plcl_out(i)              = plcl_s
  1945)                pinv_out(i)              = pinv_s    
  1946)                plfc_out(i)              = plfc_s    
  1947)                pbup_out(i)              = pbup_s
  1948)                ppen_out(i)              = ppen_s    
  1949)                qtsrc_out(i)             = qtsrc_s
  1950)                thlsrc_out(i)            = thlsrc_s
  1951)                thvlsrc_out(i)           = thvlsrc_s
  1952)                emfkbup_out(i)           = emfkbup_s
  1953)                cbmflimit_out(i)         = cbmflimit_s
  1954)                tkeavg_out(i)            = tkeavg_s
  1955)                zinv_out(i)              = zinv_s
  1956)                rcwp_out(i)              = rcwp_s
  1957)                rlwp_out(i)              = rlwp_s
  1958)                riwp_out(i)              = riwp_s
  1959) 
  1960)                wu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)       = wu_s(0:mkx)
  1961)                qtu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)      = qtu_s(0:mkx)
  1962)                thlu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = thlu_s(0:mkx)
  1963)                thvu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = thvu_s(0:mkx)
  1964)                uu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)       = uu_s(0:mkx)
  1965)                vu_out(i,mkx:0:-1)       = vu_s(0:mkx)
  1966)                qtu_emf_out(i,mkx:0:-1)  = qtu_emf_s(0:mkx)
  1967)                thlu_emf_out(i,mkx:0:-1) = thlu_emf_s(0:mkx)
  1968)                uu_emf_out(i,mkx:0:-1)   = uu_emf_s(0:mkx)
  1969)                vu_emf_out(i,mkx:0:-1)   = vu_emf_s(0:mkx)
  1970)                uemf_out(i,mkx:0:-1)     = uemf_s(0:mkx)
  1971) 
  1972)                dwten_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = dwten_s(:mkx)
  1973)                diten_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = diten_s(:mkx)
  1974)                flxrain_out(i,mkx:0:-1)  = flxrain_s(0:mkx)
  1975)                flxsnow_out(i,mkx:0:-1)  = flxsnow_s(0:mkx)
  1976)                ntraprd_out(i,mkx:1:-1)  = ntraprd_s(:mkx)
  1977)                ntsnprd_out(i,mkx:1:-1)  = ntsnprd_s(:mkx)
  1978) 
  1979)                excessu_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)  = excessu_arr_s(:mkx)
  1980)                excess0_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)  = excess0_arr_s(:mkx)
  1981)                xc_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)       = xc_arr_s(:mkx)
  1982)                aquad_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = aquad_arr_s(:mkx)
  1983)                bquad_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = bquad_arr_s(:mkx)
  1984)                cquad_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)    = cquad_arr_s(:mkx)
  1985)                bogbot_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)   = bogbot_arr_s(:mkx)
  1986)                bogtop_arr_out(i,mkx:1:-1)   = bogtop_arr_s(:mkx)
  1987) 
  1988)                do m = 1, ncnst
  1989)                   trflx_out(i,mkx:0:-1,m)   = trflx_s(0:mkx,m)  
  1990)                   tru_out(i,mkx:0:-1,m)     = tru_s(0:mkx,m)
  1991)                   tru_emf_out(i,mkx:0:-1,m) = tru_emf_s(0:mkx,m)
  1992)                enddo
  1993) 
  1994)                id_exit = .false.
  1995)                go to 333
  1996) 
  1997)           endif
  1998) 
  1999)        endif    
  2000) 
  2001)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2002)        ! Define a release level, 'prel' and release layer, 'krel'.          !
  2003)        ! 'prel' is the lowest level from which buoyancy sorting occurs, and !
  2004)        ! 'krel' is the layer index containing 'prel' in it, similar to  the !
  2005)        ! previous definitions of 'kinv', 'klcl', and 'klfc'.    In order to !
  2006)        ! ensure that only PBL scheme works within the PBL,  if LCL is below !
  2007)        ! PBL top height, then 'krel = kinv', while if LCL is above  PBL top !
  2008)        ! height, then 'krel = klcl'.   Note however that regardless of  the !
  2009)        ! definition of 'krel', cumulus convection induces fluxes within PBL !
  2010)        ! through 'fluxbelowinv'.  We can make cumulus convection start from !
  2011)        ! any level, even within the PBL by appropriately defining 'krel'  & !
  2012)        ! 'prel' here. Then it must be accompanied by appropriate definition !
  2013)        ! of source air properties, CIN, and re-setting of 'fluxbelowinv', & !
  2014)        ! many other stuffs.                                                 !
  2015)        ! Note that even when 'prel' is located above the PBL top height, we !
  2016)        ! still have cumulus convection between PBL top height and 'prel':   !
  2017)        ! we simply assume that no lateral mixing occurs in this range.      !
  2018)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2019) 
  2020)        if( klcl .lt. kinv ) then
  2021)            krel    = kinv
  2022)            prel    = ps0(krel-1)
  2023)            thv0rel = thv0bot(krel) 
  2024)        else
  2025)            krel    = klcl
  2026)            prel    = plcl 
  2027)            thv0rel = thv0lcl
  2028)        endif  
  2029) 
  2030)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2031)        ! Calculate cumulus base mass flux ('cbmf'), fractional area ('ufrcinv'), and !
  2032)        ! and mean vertical velocity (winv) of cumulus updraft at PBL top interface.  !
  2033)        ! Also, calculate updraft fractional area (ufrclcl) and vertical velocity  at !
  2034)        ! the LCL (wlcl). When LCL is below PBLH, cinlcl = 0 and 'ufrclcl = ufrcinv', !
  2035)        ! and 'wlcl = winv.                                                           !
  2036)        ! Only updrafts strong enough to overcome CIN can rise over PBL top interface.! 
  2037)        ! Thus,  in order to calculate cumulus mass flux at PBL top interface, 'cbmf',!
  2038)        ! we need to know 'CIN' ( the strength of potential energy barrier ) and      !
  2039)        ! 'sigmaw' ( a standard deviation of updraft vertical velocity at the PBL top !
  2040)        ! interface, a measure of turbulentce strength in the PBL ).   Naturally, the !
  2041)        ! ratio of these two variables, 'mu' - normalized CIN by TKE- is key variable !
  2042)        ! controlling 'cbmf'.  If 'mu' becomes large, only small fraction of updrafts !
  2043)        ! with very strong TKE can rise over the PBL - both 'cbmf' and 'ufrc' becomes !
  2044)        ! small, but 'winv' becomes large ( this can be easily understood by PDF of w !
  2045)        ! at PBL top ).  If 'mu' becomes small, lots of updraft can rise over the PBL !
  2046)        ! top - both 'cbmf' and 'ufrc' becomes large, but 'winv' becomes small. Thus, !
  2047)        ! all of the key variables associated with cumulus convection  at the PBL top !
  2048)        ! - 'cbmf', 'ufrc', 'winv' where 'cbmf = rho*ufrc*winv' - are a unique functi !
  2049)        ! ons of 'mu', normalized CIN. Although these are uniquely determined by 'mu',! 
  2050)        ! we usually impose two comstraints on 'cbmf' and 'ufrc': (1) because we will !
  2051)        ! simply assume that subsidence warming and drying of 'kinv-1' layer in assoc !
  2052)        ! iation with 'cbmf' at PBL top interface is confined only in 'kinv-1' layer, !
  2053)        ! cbmf must not be larger than the mass within the 'kinv-1' layer. Otherwise, !
  2054)        ! instability will occur due to the breaking of stability con. If we consider !
  2055)        ! semi-Lagrangian vertical advection scheme and explicitly consider the exten !
  2056)        ! t of vertical movement of each layer in association with cumulus mass flux, !
  2057)        ! we don't need to impose this constraint. However,  using a  semi-Lagrangian !
  2058)        ! scheme is a future research subject. Note that this constraint should be ap !
  2059)        ! plied for all interfaces above PBL top as well as PBL top interface.   As a !
  2060)        ! result, this 'cbmf' constraint impose a 'lower' limit on mu - 'mumin0'. (2) !
  2061)        ! in order for mass flux parameterization - rho*(w'a')= M*(a_c-a_e) - to   be !
  2062)        ! valid, cumulus updraft fractional area should be much smaller than 1.    In !
  2063)        ! current code, we impose 'rmaxfrac = 0.1 ~ 0.2'   through the whole vertical !
  2064)        ! layers where cumulus convection occurs. At the PBL top interface,  the same !
  2065)        ! constraint is made by imposing another lower 'lower' limit on mu, 'mumin1'. !
  2066)        ! After that, also limit 'ufrclcl' to be smaller than 'rmaxfrac' by 'mumin2'. !
  2067)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2068)        
  2069)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2070)        ! Calculate normalized CIN, 'mu' satisfying all the three constraints imposed !
  2071)        ! on 'cbmf'('mumin0'), 'ufrc' at the PBL top - 'ufrcinv' - ( by 'mumin1' from !
  2072)        ! a parameter sentence), and 'ufrc' at the LCL - 'ufrclcl' ( by 'mumin2').    !
  2073)        ! Note that 'cbmf' does not change between PBL top and LCL  because we assume !
  2074)        ! that buoyancy sorting does not occur when cumulus updraft is unsaturated.   !
  2075)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2076)    
  2077)        if( use_CINcin ) then       
  2078)            wcrit = sqrt( 2._r8 * cin * rbuoy )      
  2079)        else
  2080)            wcrit = sqrt( 2._r8 * cinlcl * rbuoy )   
  2081)        endif
  2082)        sigmaw = sqrt( rkfre * tkeavg + epsvarw )
  2083)        mu = wcrit/sigmaw/1.4142_r8                  
  2084)        if( mu .ge. 3._r8 ) then
  2085)          ! write(iulog,*) 'mu >= 3'
  2086)            id_exit = .true.
  2087)            go to 333
  2088)        endif
  2089)        rho0inv = ps0(kinv-1)/(r*thv0top(kinv-1)*exns0(kinv-1))
  2090)        cbmf = (rho0inv*sigmaw/2.5066_r8)*exp(-mu**2)
  2091)        ! 1. 'cbmf' constraint
  2092)        cbmflimit = 0.9_r8*dp0(kinv-1)/g/dt
  2093)        mumin0 = 0._r8
  2094)        if( cbmf .gt. cbmflimit ) mumin0 = sqrt(-log(2.5066_r8*cbmflimit/rho0inv/sigmaw))
  2095)        ! 2. 'ufrcinv' constraint
  2096)        mu = max(max(mu,mumin0),mumin1)
  2097)        ! 3. 'ufrclcl' constraint      
  2098)        mulcl = sqrt(2._r8*cinlcl*rbuoy)/1.4142_r8/sigmaw
  2099)        mulclstar = sqrt(max(0._r8,2._r8*(exp(-mu**2)/2.5066_r8)**2*(1._r8/erfc(mu)**2-0.25_r8/rmaxfrac**2)))
  2100)        if( mulcl .gt. 1.e-8_r8 .and. mulcl .gt. mulclstar ) then
  2101)            mumin2 = compute_mumin2(mulcl,rmaxfrac,mu)
  2102)            if( mu .gt. mumin2 ) then
  2103)                write(iulog,*) 'Critical error in mu calculation in UW_ShCu'
  2104)                call endrun
  2105)            endif
  2106)            mu = max(mu,mumin2)
  2107)            if( mu .eq. mumin2 ) limit_ufrc(i) = 1._r8
  2108)        endif
  2109)        if( mu .eq. mumin0 ) limit_cbmf(i) = 1._r8
  2110)        if( mu .eq. mumin1 ) limit_ufrc(i) = 1._r8
  2111) 
  2112)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !    
  2113)        ! Calculate final ['cbmf','ufrcinv','winv'] at the PBL top interface. !
  2114)        ! Note that final 'cbmf' here is obtained in such that 'ufrcinv' and  !
  2115)        ! 'ufrclcl' are smaller than ufrcmax with no instability.             !
  2116)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2117) 
  2118)        cbmf = (rho0inv*sigmaw/2.5066_r8)*exp(-mu**2)                       
  2119)        winv = sigmaw*(2._r8/2.5066_r8)*exp(-mu**2)/erfc(mu)
  2120)        ufrcinv = cbmf/winv/rho0inv
  2121) 
  2122)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2123)        ! Calculate ['ufrclcl','wlcl'] at the LCL. When LCL is below PBL top, !
  2124)        ! it automatically becomes 'ufrclcl = ufrcinv' & 'wlcl = winv', since !
  2125)        ! it was already set to 'cinlcl=0' if LCL is below PBL top interface. !
  2126)        ! Note 'cbmf' at the PBL top is the same as 'cbmf' at the LCL.  Note  !
  2127)        ! also that final 'cbmf' here is obtained in such that 'ufrcinv' and  !
  2128)        ! 'ufrclcl' are smaller than ufrcmax and there is no instability.     !
  2129)        ! By construction, it must be 'wlcl > 0' but for assurance, I checked !
  2130)        ! this again in the below block. If 'ufrclcl < 0.1%', just exit.      !
  2131)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2132) 
  2133)        wtw = winv * winv - 2._r8 * cinlcl * rbuoy
  2134)        if( wtw .le. 0._r8 ) then
  2135)          ! write(iulog,*) 'wlcl < 0 at the LCL'
  2136)            exit_wtw(i) = 1._r8
  2137)            id_exit = .true.
  2138)            go to 333
  2139)        endif
  2140)        wlcl = sqrt(wtw)
  2141)        ufrclcl = cbmf/wlcl/rho0inv
  2142)        wrel = wlcl
  2143)        if( ufrclcl .le. 0.0001_r8 ) then
  2144)          ! write(iulog,*) 'ufrclcl <= 0.0001' 
  2145)            exit_ufrc(i) = 1._r8
  2146)            id_exit = .true.
  2147)            go to 333
  2148)        endif
  2149)        ufrc(krel-1) = ufrclcl
  2150) 
  2151)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2152)        ! Below is just diagnostic output for detailed analysis of cumulus scheme !
  2153)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2154) 
  2155)        ufrcinvbase        = ufrcinv
  2156)        winvbase           = winv
  2157)        umf(kinv-1:krel-1) = cbmf   
  2158)        wu(kinv-1:krel-1)  = winv   
  2159) 
  2160)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2161)        ! Define updraft properties at the level where buoyancy sorting starts to be !
  2162)        ! happening, i.e., by definition, at 'prel' level within the release layer.  !
  2163)        ! Because no lateral entrainment occurs upto 'prel', conservative scalars of ! 
  2164)        ! cumulus updraft at release level is same as those of source air.  However, ! 
  2165)        ! horizontal momentums of source air are modified by horizontal PGF forcings ! 
  2166)        ! from PBL top interface to 'prel'.  For this case, we should add additional !
  2167)        ! horizontal momentum from PBL top interface to 'prel' as will be done below !
  2168)        ! to 'usrc' and 'vsrc'. Note that below cumulus updraft properties - umf, wu,!
  2169)        ! thlu, qtu, thvu, uu, vu - are defined all interfaces not at the layer mid- !
  2170)        ! point. From the index notation of cumulus scheme, wu(k) is the cumulus up- !
  2171)        ! draft vertical velocity at the top interface of k layer.                   !
  2172)        ! Diabatic horizontal momentum forcing should be treated as a kind of 'body' !
  2173)        ! forcing without actual mass exchange between convective updraft and        !
  2174)        ! environment, but still taking horizontal momentum from the environment to  !
  2175)        ! the convective updrafts. Thus, diabatic convective momentum transport      !
  2176)        ! vertically redistributes environmental horizontal momentum.                !
  2177)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2178) 
  2179)        emf(krel-1)  = 0._r8
  2180)        umf(krel-1)  = cbmf
  2181)        wu(krel-1)   = wrel
  2182)        thlu(krel-1) = thlsrc
  2183)        qtu(krel-1)  = qtsrc
  2184)        call conden(prel,thlsrc,qtsrc,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2185)        if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2186)            exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2187)            id_exit = .true.
  2188)            go to 333
  2189)        endif
  2190)        thvu(krel-1) = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )       
  2191) 
  2192)        uplus = 0._r8
  2193)        vplus = 0._r8
  2194)        if( krel .eq. kinv ) then
  2195)            uplus = PGFc * ssu0(kinv) * ( prel - ps0(kinv-1) )
  2196)            vplus = PGFc * ssv0(kinv) * ( prel - ps0(kinv-1) )
  2197)        else
  2198)            do k = kinv, max(krel-1,kinv)
  2199)               uplus = uplus + PGFc * ssu0(k) * ( ps0(k) - ps0(k-1) )
  2200)               vplus = vplus + PGFc * ssv0(k) * ( ps0(k) - ps0(k-1) )
  2201)            end do
  2202)            uplus = uplus + PGFc * ssu0(krel) * ( prel - ps0(krel-1) )
  2203)            vplus = vplus + PGFc * ssv0(krel) * ( prel - ps0(krel-1) )
  2204)        end if
  2205)        uu(krel-1) = usrc + uplus
  2206)        vu(krel-1) = vsrc + vplus      
  2207) 
  2208)        do m = 1, ncnst
  2209)           tru(krel-1,m)  = trsrc(m)
  2210)        enddo
  2211) 
  2212)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2213)        ! Define environmental properties at the level where buoyancy sorting occurs !
  2214)        ! ('pe', normally, layer midpoint except in the 'krel' layer). In the 'krel' !
  2215)        ! layer where buoyancy sorting starts to occur, however, 'pe' is defined     !
  2216)        ! differently because LCL is regarded as lower interface for mixing purpose. !
  2217)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2218) 
  2219)        pe      = 0.5_r8 * ( prel + ps0(krel) )
  2220)        dpe     = prel - ps0(krel)
  2221)        exne    = exnf(pe)
  2222)        thvebot = thv0rel
  2223)        thle    = thl0(krel) + ssthl0(krel) * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2224)        qte     = qt0(krel)  + ssqt0(krel)  * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2225)        ue      = u0(krel)   + ssu0(krel)   * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2226)        ve      = v0(krel)   + ssv0(krel)   * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2227)        do m = 1, ncnst
  2228)           tre(m) = tr0(krel,m)  + sstr0(krel,m) * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2229)        enddo
  2230) 
  2231)        !-------------------------! 
  2232)        ! Buoyancy-Sorting Mixing !
  2233)        !-------------------------!------------------------------------------------ !
  2234)        !                                                                           !
  2235)        !  In order to complete buoyancy-sorting mixing at layer mid-point, and so  ! 
  2236)        !  calculate 'updraft mass flux, updraft w velocity, conservative scalars'  !
  2237)        !  at the upper interface of each layer, we need following 3 information.   ! 
  2238)        !                                                                           !
  2239)        !  1. Pressure where mixing occurs ('pe'), and temperature at 'pe' which is !
  2240)        !     necessary to calculate various thermodynamic coefficients at pe. This !
  2241)        !     temperature is obtained by undiluted cumulus properties lifted to pe. ! 
  2242)        !  2. Undiluted updraft properties at pe - conservative scalar and vertical !
  2243)        !     velocity -which are assumed to be the same as the properties at lower !
  2244)        !     interface only for calculation of fractional lateral entrainment  and !
  2245)        !     detrainment rate ( fer(k) and fdr(k) [Pa-1] ), respectively.    Final !
  2246)        !     values of cumulus conservative scalars and w at the top interface are !
  2247)        !     calculated afterward after obtaining fer(k) & fdr(k).                 !
  2248)        !  3. Environmental properties at pe.                                       !
  2249)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2250)        
  2251)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  2252)        ! Define cumulus scale height.                                             !
  2253)        ! Cumulus scale height is defined as the maximum height cumulus can reach. !
  2254)        ! In case of premitive code, cumulus scale height ('cush')  at the current !
  2255)        ! time step was assumed to be the same as 'cush' of previous time step.    !
  2256)        ! However, I directly calculated cush at each time step using an iterative !
  2257)        ! method. Note that within the cumulus scheme, 'cush' information is  used !
  2258)        ! only at two places during buoyancy-sorting process:                      !
  2259)        ! (1) Even negatively buoyancy mixtures with strong vertical velocity      !
  2260)        !     enough to rise up to 'rle*scaleh' (rle = 0.1) from pe are entrained  !
  2261)        !     into cumulus updraft,                                                !  
  2262)        ! (2) The amount of mass that is involved in buoyancy-sorting mixing       !
  2263)        !      process at pe is rei(k) = rkm/scaleh/rho*g [Pa-1]                   !
  2264)        ! In terms of (1), I think critical stopping distance might be replaced by !
  2265)        ! layer thickness. In future, we will use rei(k) = (0.5*rkm/z0(k)/rho/g).  !
  2266)        ! In the premitive code,  'scaleh' was largely responsible for the jumping !
  2267)        ! variation of precipitation amount.                                       !
  2268)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !   
  2269) 
  2270)        scaleh = tscaleh
  2271)        if( tscaleh .lt. 0.0_r8 ) scaleh = 1000._r8 
  2272) 
  2273)      ! Save time : Set iter_scaleh = 1. This will automatically use 'cush' from the previous time step
  2274)      !             at the first implicit iteration. At the second implicit iteration, it will use
  2275)      !             the updated 'cush' by the first implicit cin. So, this updating has an effect of
  2276)      !             doing one iteration for cush calculation, which is good. 
  2277)      !             So, only this setting of 'iter_scaleh = 1' is sufficient-enough to save computation time.
  2278)      ! OK
  2279) 
  2280)        do iter_scaleh = 1, 3
  2281) 
  2282)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2283)        ! Initialization of 'kbup' and 'kpen'                              !
  2284)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2285)        ! 'kbup' is the top-most layer in which cloud buoyancy is positive !
  2286)        ! both at the top and bottom interface of the layer. 'kpen' is the !
  2287)        ! layer upto which cumulus panetrates ,i.e., cumulus w at the base !
  2288)        ! interface is positive, but becomes negative at the top interface.!
  2289)        ! Here, we initialize 'kbup' and 'kpen'. These initializations are !  
  2290)        ! not trivial but important, expecially   in calculating turbulent !
  2291)        ! fluxes without confliction among several physics as explained in !
  2292)        ! detail in the part of turbulent fluxes calculation later.   Note !
  2293)        ! that regardless of whether 'kbup' and 'kpen' are updated or  not !
  2294)        ! during updraft motion,  penetrative entrainments are dumped down !
  2295)        ! across the top interface of 'kbup' later.      More specifically,!
  2296)        ! penetrative entrainment heat and moisture fluxes are  calculated !
  2297)        ! from the top interface of 'kbup' layer  to the base interface of !
  2298)        ! 'kpen' layer. Because of this, initialization of 'kbup' & 'kpen' !
  2299)        ! influence the convection system when there are not updated.  The !  
  2300)        ! below initialization of 'kbup = krel' assures  that  penetrative !
  2301)        ! entrainment fluxes always occur at interfaces above the PBL  top !
  2302)        ! interfaces (i.e., only at interfaces k >=kinv ), which seems  to !
  2303)        ! be attractable considering that the most correct fluxes  at  the !
  2304)        ! PBL top interface can be ontained from the 'fluxbelowinv'  using !
  2305)        ! reconstructed PBL height.                                        ! 
  2306)        ! The 'kbup = krel'(after going through the whole buoyancy sorting !
  2307)        ! proces during updraft motion) implies that cumulus updraft  from !
  2308)        ! the PBL top interface can not reach to the LFC,so that 'kbup' is !
  2309)        ! not updated during upward. This means that cumulus updraft   did !
  2310)        ! not fully overcome the buoyancy barrier above just the PBL top.  !
  2311)        ! If 'kpen' is not updated either ( i.e., cumulus cannot rise over !
  2312)        ! the top interface of release layer),penetrative entrainment will !
  2313)        ! not happen at any interfaces.  If cumulus updraft can rise above !
  2314)        ! the release layer but cannot fully overcome the buoyancy barrier !
  2315)        ! just above PBL top interface, penetratve entrainment   occurs at !
  2316)        ! several above interfaces, including the top interface of release ! 
  2317)        ! layer. In the latter case, warming and drying tendencies will be !
  2318)        ! be initiated in 'krel' layer. Note current choice of 'kbup=krel' !
  2319)        ! is completely compatible with other flux physics without  double !
  2320)        ! or miss counting turbulent fluxes at any interface. However, the !
  2321)        ! alternative choice of 'kbup=krel-1' also has itw own advantage - !
  2322)        ! when cumulus updraft cannot overcome buoyancy barrier just above !
  2323)        ! PBL top, entrainment warming and drying are concentrated in  the !
  2324)        ! 'kinv-1' layer instead of 'kinv' layer for this case. This might !
  2325)        ! seems to be more dynamically reasonable, but I will choose the   !
  2326)        ! 'kbup = krel' choice since it is more compatible  with the other !
  2327)        ! parts of the code, expecially, when we chose ' use_emf=.false. ' !
  2328)        ! as explained in detail in turbulent flux calculation part.       !
  2329)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2330) 
  2331)        kbup    = krel
  2332)        kpen    = krel
  2333)        
  2334)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2335)        ! Since 'wtw' is continuously updated during vertical motion,  !
  2336)        ! I need below initialization command within this 'iter_scaleh'!
  2337)        ! do loop. Similarily, I need initializations of environmental !
  2338)        ! properties at 'krel' layer as below.                         !
  2339)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2340) 
  2341)        wtw     = wlcl * wlcl
  2342)        pe      = 0.5_r8 * ( prel + ps0(krel) )
  2343)        dpe     = prel - ps0(krel)
  2344)        exne    = exnf(pe)
  2345)        thvebot = thv0rel
  2346)        thle    = thl0(krel) + ssthl0(krel) * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2347)        qte     = qt0(krel)  + ssqt0(krel)  * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2348)        ue      = u0(krel)   + ssu0(krel)   * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2349)        ve      = v0(krel)   + ssv0(krel)   * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2350)        do m = 1, ncnst
  2351)           tre(m) = tr0(krel,m)  + sstr0(krel,m)  * ( pe - p0(krel) )
  2352)        enddo
  2353) 
  2354)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2355)        ! Cumulus rises upward from 'prel' ( or base interface of  'krel' layer ) !
  2356)        ! until updraft vertical velocity becomes zero.                           !
  2357)        ! Buoyancy sorting is performed via two stages. (1) Using cumulus updraft !
  2358)        ! properties at the base interface of each layer,perform buoyancy sorting !
  2359)        ! at the layer mid-point, 'pe',  and update cumulus properties at the top !
  2360)        ! interface, and then  (2) by averaging updated cumulus properties at the !
  2361)        ! top interface and cumulus properties at the base interface,   calculate !
  2362)        ! cumulus updraft properties at pe that will be used  in buoyancy sorting !
  2363)        ! mixing - thlue, qtue and, wue.  Using this averaged properties, perform !
  2364)        ! buoyancy sorting again at pe, and re-calculate fer(k) and fdr(k). Using !
  2365)        ! this recalculated fer(k) and fdr(k),  finally calculate cumulus updraft !
  2366)        ! properties at the top interface - thlu, qtu, thvu, uu, vu. In the below,!
  2367)        ! 'iter_xc = 1' performs the first stage, while 'iter_xc= 2' performs the !
  2368)        ! second stage. We can increase the number of iterations, 'nter_xc'.as we !
  2369)        ! want, but a sample test indicated that about 3 - 5 iterations  produced !
  2370)        ! satisfactory converent solution. Finally, identify 'kbup' and 'kpen'.   !
  2371)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2372)        
  2373)        do k = krel, mkx - 1 ! Here, 'k' is a layer index.
  2374) 
  2375)           km1 = k - 1
  2376) 
  2377)           thlue = thlu(km1)
  2378)           qtue  = qtu(km1)    
  2379)           wue   = wu(km1)
  2380)           wtwb  = wtw  
  2381) 
  2382)        do iter_xc = 1, niter_xc
  2383)           
  2384)           wtw = wu(km1) * wu(km1)
  2385) 
  2386)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2387)           ! Calculate environmental and cumulus saturation 'excess' at 'pe'. !
  2388)           ! Note that in order to calculate saturation excess, we should use ! 
  2389)           ! liquid water temperature instead of temperature  as the argument !
  2390)           ! of "qsat". But note normal argument of "qsat" is temperature.    !
  2391)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2392) 
  2393)           call conden(pe,thle,qte,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2394)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2395)               exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2396)               id_exit = .true.
  2397)               go to 333
  2398)           end if
  2399)           thv0j    = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir*qvj - qlj - qij )
  2400)           rho0j    = pe / ( r * thv0j * exne )
  2401)           qsat_arg = thle*exne     
  2402)           call qsat(qsat_arg, pe, es, qs)
  2403)           excess0  = qte - qs
  2404) 
  2405)           call conden(pe,thlue,qtue,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2406)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2407)               exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2408)               id_exit = .true.
  2409)               go to 333
  2410)           end if
  2411)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2412)           ! Detrain excessive condensate larger than 'criqc' from the cumulus ! 
  2413)           ! updraft before performing buoyancy sorting. All I should to do is !
  2414)           ! to update 'thlue' &  'que' here. Below modification is completely !
  2415)           ! compatible with the other part of the code since 'thule' & 'qtue' !
  2416)           ! are used only for buoyancy sorting. I found that as long as I use !
  2417)           ! 'niter_xc >= 2',  detraining excessive condensate before buoyancy !
  2418)           ! sorting has negligible influence on the buoyancy sorting results. !   
  2419)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2420)           if( (qlj + qij) .gt. criqc ) then
  2421)                exql  = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qlj / ( qlj + qij )
  2422)                exqi  = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qij / ( qlj + qij )
  2423)                qtue  = qtue - exql - exqi
  2424)                thlue = thlue + (xlv/cp/exne)*exql + (xls/cp/exne)*exqi 
  2425)           endif
  2426)           call conden(pe,thlue,qtue,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2427)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2428)               exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2429)               id_exit = .true.
  2430)               go to 333
  2431)           end if
  2432)           thvj     = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir * qvj - qlj - qij )
  2433)           tj       = thj * exne ! This 'tj' is used for computing thermo. coeffs. below
  2434)           qsat_arg = thlue*exne
  2435)           call qsat(qsat_arg, pe, es, qs)
  2436)           excessu  = qtue - qs
  2437) 
  2438)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2439)           ! Calculate critical mixing fraction, 'xc'. Mixture with mixing ratio !
  2440)           ! smaller than 'xc' will be entrained into cumulus updraft.  Both the !
  2441)           ! saturated updrafts with 'positive buoyancy' or 'negative buoyancy + ! 
  2442)           ! strong vertical velocity enough to rise certain threshold distance' !
  2443)           ! are kept into the updraft in the below program. If the core updraft !
  2444)           ! is unsaturated, we can set 'xc = 0' and let the cumulus  convection !
  2445)           ! still works or we may exit.                                         !
  2446)           ! Current below code does not entrain unsaturated mixture. However it !
  2447)           ! should be modified such that it also entrain unsaturated mixture.   !
  2448)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2449) 
  2450)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2451)           ! cridis : Critical stopping distance for buoyancy sorting purpose. !
  2452)           !          scaleh is only used here.                                !
  2453)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2454) 
  2455)             cridis = rle*scaleh                 ! Original code
  2456)           ! cridis = 1._r8*(zs0(k) - zs0(k-1))  ! New code
  2457)  
  2458)           ! ---------------- !
  2459)           ! Buoyancy Sorting !
  2460)           ! ---------------- !                   
  2461) 
  2462)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2463)           ! Case 1 : When both cumulus and env. are unsaturated or saturated. !
  2464)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2465) 
  2466)           if( ( excessu .le. 0._r8 .and. excess0 .le. 0._r8 ) .or. ( excessu .ge. 0._r8 .and. excess0 .ge. 0._r8 ) ) then
  2467)                 xc = min(1._r8,max(0._r8,1._r8-2._r8*rbuoy*g*cridis/wue**2._r8*(1._r8-thvj/thv0j)))
  2468)               ! Below 3 lines are diagnostic output not influencing
  2469)               ! numerical calculations.
  2470)                 aquad = 0._r8
  2471)                 bquad = 0._r8
  2472)                 cquad = 0._r8
  2473)           else
  2474)           ! -------------------------------------------------- !
  2475)           ! Case 2 : When either cumulus or env. is saturated. !
  2476)           ! -------------------------------------------------- !
  2477)               xsat    = excessu / ( excessu - excess0 );
  2478)               thlxsat = thlue + xsat * ( thle - thlue );
  2479)               qtxsat  = qtue  + xsat * ( qte - qtue );
  2480)               call conden(pe,thlxsat,qtxsat,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2481)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2482)                   exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2483)                   id_exit = .true.
  2484)                   go to 333
  2485)               end if
  2486)               thvxsat = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir * qvj - qlj - qij )               
  2487)               ! -------------------------------------------------- !
  2488)               ! kk=1 : Cumulus Segment, kk=2 : Environment Segment !
  2489)               ! -------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2490)               do kk = 1, 2 
  2491)                    if( kk .eq. 1 ) then
  2492)                        thv_x0 = thvj;
  2493)                        thv_x1 = ( 1._r8 - 1._r8/xsat ) * thvj + ( 1._r8/xsat ) * thvxsat;
  2494)                    else
  2495)                        thv_x1 = thv0j;
  2496)                        thv_x0 = ( xsat / ( xsat - 1._r8 ) ) * thv0j + ( 1._r8/( 1._r8 - xsat ) ) * thvxsat;
  2497)                    endif
  2498)                    aquad =  wue**2;
  2499)                    bquad =  2._r8*rbuoy*g*cridis*(thv_x1 - thv_x0)/thv0j - 2._r8*wue**2;
  2500)                    cquad =  2._r8*rbuoy*g*cridis*(thv_x0 -  thv0j)/thv0j +       wue**2;
  2501)                    if( kk .eq. 1 ) then
  2502)                        if( ( bquad**2-4._r8*aquad*cquad ) .ge. 0._r8 ) then
  2503)                              call roots(aquad,bquad,cquad,xs1,xs2,status)
  2504)                              x_cu = min(1._r8,max(0._r8,min(xsat,min(xs1,xs2))))
  2505)                        else
  2506)                              x_cu = xsat;
  2507)                        endif
  2508)                    else 
  2509)                        if( ( bquad**2-4._r8*aquad*cquad) .ge. 0._r8 ) then
  2510)                              call roots(aquad,bquad,cquad,xs1,xs2,status)
  2511)                              x_en = min(1._r8,max(0._r8,max(xsat,min(xs1,xs2))))
  2512)                        else
  2513)                              x_en = 1._r8;
  2514)                        endif
  2515)                    endif
  2516)               enddo
  2517)               if( x_cu .eq. xsat ) then
  2518)                   xc = max(x_cu, x_en);
  2519)               else
  2520)                   xc = x_cu;
  2521)               endif
  2522)           endif
  2523) 
  2524)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2525)           ! Compute fractional lateral entrainment & detrainment rate in each layers.!
  2526)           ! The unit of rei(k), fer(k), and fdr(k) is [Pa-1].  Alternative choice of !
  2527)           ! 'rei(k)' is also shown below, where coefficient 0.5 was from approximate !
  2528)           ! tuning against the BOMEX case.                                           !
  2529)           ! In order to prevent the onset of instability in association with cumulus !
  2530)           ! induced subsidence advection, cumulus mass flux at the top interface  in !
  2531)           ! any layer should be smaller than ( 90% of ) total mass within that layer.!
  2532)           ! I imposed limits on 'rei(k)' as below,  in such that stability condition ! 
  2533)           ! is always satisfied.                                                     !
  2534)           ! Below limiter of 'rei(k)' becomes negative for some cases, causing error.!
  2535)           ! So, for the time being, I came back to the original limiter.             !
  2536)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2537)           ee2    = xc**2
  2538)           ud2    = 1._r8 - 2._r8*xc + xc**2
  2539)         ! rei(k) = ( rkm / scaleh / g / rho0j )        ! Default.
  2540)           rei(k) = ( 0.5_r8 * rkm / z0(k) / g /rho0j ) ! Alternative.
  2541)           if( xc .gt. 0.5_r8 ) rei(k) = min(rei(k),0.9_r8*log(dp0(k)/g/dt/umf(km1) + 1._r8)/dpe/(2._r8*xc-1._r8))
  2542)           fer(k) = rei(k) * ee2
  2543)           fdr(k) = rei(k) * ud2
  2544) 
  2545)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2546)           ! Iteration Start due to 'maxufrc' constraint [ ****************************** ] ! 
  2547)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2548) 
  2549)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2550)           ! Calculate cumulus updraft mass flux and penetrative entrainment mass flux. !
  2551)           ! Note that  non-zero penetrative entrainment mass flux will be asigned only !
  2552)           ! to interfaces from the top interface of 'kbup' layer to the base interface !
  2553)           ! of 'kpen' layer as will be shown later.                                    !
  2554)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2555) 
  2556)           umf(k) = umf(km1) * exp( dpe * ( fer(k) - fdr(k) ) )
  2557)           emf(k) = 0._r8    
  2558) 
  2559)           ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  2560)           ! Compute cumulus updraft properties at the top interface.  !
  2561)           ! Also use Tayler expansion in order to treat limiting case !
  2562)           ! --------------------------------------------------------- !
  2563) 
  2564)           if( fer(k)*dpe .lt. 1.e-4_r8 ) then
  2565)               thlu(k) = thlu(km1) + ( thle + ssthl0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 - thlu(km1) ) * fer(k) * dpe
  2566)               qtu(k)  =  qtu(km1) + ( qte  +  ssqt0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -  qtu(km1) ) * fer(k) * dpe
  2567)               uu(k)   =   uu(km1) + ( ue   +   ssu0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -   uu(km1) ) * fer(k) * dpe - PGFc * ssu0(k) * dpe
  2568)               vu(k)   =   vu(km1) + ( ve   +   ssv0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -   vu(km1) ) * fer(k) * dpe - PGFc * ssv0(k) * dpe
  2569)               do m = 1, ncnst
  2570)                  tru(k,m)  =  tru(km1,m) + ( tre(m)  + sstr0(k,m) * dpe / 2._r8  -  tru(km1,m) ) * fer(k) * dpe
  2571)               enddo
  2572)           else
  2573)               thlu(k) = ( thle + ssthl0(k) / fer(k) - ssthl0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 ) -          &
  2574)                         ( thle + ssthl0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 - thlu(km1) + ssthl0(k) / fer(k) ) * exp(-fer(k) * dpe)
  2575)               qtu(k)  = ( qte  +  ssqt0(k) / fer(k) -  ssqt0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 ) -          &  
  2576)                         ( qte  +  ssqt0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -  qtu(km1) +  ssqt0(k) / fer(k) ) * exp(-fer(k) * dpe)
  2577)               uu(k) =   ( ue + ( 1._r8 - PGFc ) * ssu0(k) / fer(k) - ssu0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 ) - &
  2578)                         ( ue +     ssu0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -   uu(km1) + ( 1._r8 - PGFc ) * ssu0(k) / fer(k) ) * exp(-fer(k) * dpe)
  2579)               vu(k) =   ( ve + ( 1._r8 - PGFc ) * ssv0(k) / fer(k) - ssv0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 ) - &
  2580)                         ( ve +     ssv0(k) * dpe / 2._r8 -   vu(km1) + ( 1._r8 - PGFc ) * ssv0(k) / fer(k) ) * exp(-fer(k) * dpe)
  2581)               do m = 1, ncnst
  2582)                  tru(k,m)  = ( tre(m)  + sstr0(k,m) / fer(k) - sstr0(k,m) * dpe / 2._r8 ) - &  
  2583)                              ( tre(m)  + sstr0(k,m) * dpe / 2._r8 - tru(km1,m) + sstr0(k,m) / fer(k) ) * exp(-fer(k) * dpe)
  2584)               enddo
  2585)           end if
  2586) 
  2587)           !------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2588)           ! Expel some of cloud water and ice from cumulus  updraft at the top !
  2589)           ! interface.  Note that this is not 'detrainment' term  but a 'sink' !
  2590)           ! term of cumulus updraft qt ( or one part of 'source' term of  mean !
  2591)           ! environmental qt ). At this stage, as the most simplest choice, if !
  2592)           ! condensate amount within cumulus updraft is larger than a critical !
  2593)           ! value, 'criqc', expels the surplus condensate from cumulus updraft !
  2594)           ! to the environment. A certain fraction ( e.g., 'frc_sus' ) of this !
  2595)           ! expelled condesnate will be in a form that can be suspended in the !
  2596)           ! layer k where it was formed, while the other fraction, '1-frc_sus' ! 
  2597)           ! will be in a form of precipitatble (e.g.,can potentially fall down !
  2598)           ! across the base interface of layer k ). In turn we should describe !
  2599)           ! subsequent falling of precipitable condensate ('1-frc_sus') across !
  2600)           ! the base interface of the layer k, &  evaporation of precipitating !
  2601)           ! water in the below layer k-1 and associated evaporative cooling of !
  2602)           ! the later, k-1, and falling of 'non-evaporated precipitating water !
  2603)           ! ( which was initially formed in layer k ) and a newly-formed preci !
  2604)           ! pitable water in the layer, k-1', across the base interface of the !
  2605)           ! lower layer k-1.  Cloud microphysics should correctly describe all !
  2606)           ! of these process.  In a near future, I should significantly modify !
  2607)           ! this cloud microphysics, including precipitation-induced downdraft !
  2608)           ! also.                                                              !
  2609)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2610) 
  2611)           call conden(ps0(k),thlu(k),qtu(k),thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2612)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2613)               exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2614)               id_exit = .true.
  2615)               go to 333
  2616)           end if
  2617)           if( (qlj + qij) .gt. criqc ) then
  2618)                exql    = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qlj / ( qlj + qij )
  2619)                exqi    = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qij / ( qlj + qij )
  2620)                ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2621)                ! It is very important to re-update 'qtu' and 'thlu'  at the upper ! 
  2622)                ! interface after expelling condensate from cumulus updraft at the !
  2623)                ! top interface of the layer. As mentioned above, this is a 'sink' !
  2624)                ! of cumulus qt (or equivalently, a 'source' of environmentasl qt),!
  2625)                ! not a regular convective'detrainment'.                           !
  2626)                ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2627)                qtu(k)  = qtu(k) - exql - exqi
  2628)                thlu(k) = thlu(k) + (xlv/cp/exns0(k))*exql + (xls/cp/exns0(k))*exqi 
  2629)                ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2630)                ! Expelled cloud condensate into the environment from the updraft. ! 
  2631)                ! After all the calculation later, 'dwten' and 'diten' will have a !
  2632)                ! unit of [ kg/kg/s ], because it is a tendency of qt. Restoration !
  2633)                ! of 'dwten' and 'diten' to this correct unit through  multiplying !
  2634)                ! 'umf(k)*g/dp0(k)' will be performed later after finally updating !
  2635)                ! 'umf' using a 'rmaxfrac' constraint near the end of this updraft !
  2636)                ! buoyancy sorting loop.                                           !
  2637)                ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2638)                dwten(k) = exql   
  2639)                diten(k) = exqi
  2640)           else
  2641)                dwten(k) = 0._r8
  2642)                diten(k) = 0._r8
  2643)           endif
  2644)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2645)           ! Update 'thvu(k)' after detraining condensate from cumulus updraft.!
  2646)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2647)           call conden(ps0(k),thlu(k),qtu(k),thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2648)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2649)               exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2650)               id_exit = .true.
  2651)               go to 333
  2652)           end if  
  2653)           thvu(k) = thj * ( 1._r8 + zvir * qvj - qlj - qij )
  2654) 
  2655)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2656)           ! Calculate updraft vertical velocity at the upper interface. !
  2657)           ! In order to calculate 'wtw' at the upper interface, we use  !
  2658)           ! 'wtw' at the lower interface. Note  'wtw'  is continuously  ! 
  2659)           ! updated as cumulus updraft rises.                           !
  2660)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------- !
  2661) 
  2662)           bogbot = rbuoy * ( thvu(km1) / thvebot  - 1._r8 ) ! Cloud buoyancy at base interface
  2663)           bogtop = rbuoy * ( thvu(k) / thv0top(k) - 1._r8 ) ! Cloud buoyancy at top  interface
  2664) 
  2665)           delbog = bogtop - bogbot
  2666)           drage  = fer(k) * ( 1._r8 + rdrag )
  2667)           expfac = exp(-2._r8*drage*dpe)
  2668) 
  2669)           wtwb = wtw
  2670)           if( drage*dpe .gt. 1.e-3_r8 ) then
  2671)               wtw = wtw*expfac + (delbog + (1._r8-expfac)*(bogbot + delbog/(-2._r8*drage*dpe)))/(rho0j*drage)
  2672)           else
  2673)               wtw = wtw + dpe * ( bogbot + bogtop ) / rho0j
  2674)           endif
  2675) 
  2676)         ! Force the plume rise at least to klfc of the undiluted plume.
  2677)         ! Because even the below is not complete, I decided not to include this.
  2678) 
  2679)         ! if( k .le. klfc ) then
  2680)         !     wtw = max( 1.e-2_r8, wtw )
  2681)         ! endif 
  2682)          
  2683)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2684)           ! Repeat 'iter_xc' iteration loop until 'iter_xc = niter_xc'.    !
  2685)           ! Also treat the case even when wtw < 0 at the 'kpen' interface. !
  2686)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !  
  2687)           
  2688)           if( wtw .gt. 0._r8 ) then   
  2689)               thlue = 0.5_r8 * ( thlu(km1) + thlu(k) )
  2690)               qtue  = 0.5_r8 * ( qtu(km1)  +  qtu(k) )         
  2691)               wue   = 0.5_r8 *   sqrt( max( wtwb + wtw, 0._r8 ) )
  2692)           else
  2693)               go to 111
  2694)           endif 
  2695) 
  2696)        enddo ! End of 'iter_xc' loop  
  2697) 
  2698)    111 continue
  2699) 
  2700)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  2701)           ! Add the contribution of self-detrainment  to vertical variations of cumulus !
  2702)           ! updraft mass flux. The reason why we are trying to include self-detrainment !
  2703)           ! is as follows.  In current scheme,  vertical variation of updraft mass flux !
  2704)           ! is not fully consistent with the vertical variation of updraft vertical w.  !
  2705)           ! For example, within a given layer, let's assume that  cumulus w is positive !
  2706)           ! at the base interface, while negative at the top interface. This means that !
  2707)           ! cumulus updraft cannot reach to the top interface of the layer. However,    !
  2708)           ! cumulus updraft mass flux at the top interface is not zero according to the !
  2709)           ! vertical tendency equation of cumulus mass flux.   Ideally, cumulus updraft ! 
  2710)           ! mass flux at the top interface should be zero for this case. In order to    !
  2711)           ! assures that cumulus updraft mass flux goes to zero when cumulus updraft    ! 
  2712)           ! vertical velocity goes to zero, we are imposing self-detrainment term as    !
  2713)           ! below by considering layer-mean cloud buoyancy and cumulus updraft vertical !
  2714)           ! velocity square at the top interface. Use of auto-detrainment term will  be !
  2715)           ! determined by setting 'use_self_detrain=.true.' in the parameter sentence.  !
  2716)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2717)      
  2718)           if( use_self_detrain ) then
  2719)               autodet = min( 0.5_r8*g*(bogbot+bogtop)/(max(wtw,0._r8)+1.e-4_r8), 0._r8 ) 
  2720)               umf(k)  = umf(k) * exp( 0.637_r8*(dpe/rho0j/g) * autodet )   
  2721)           end if      
  2722)           if( umf(k) .eq. 0._r8 ) wtw = -1._r8
  2723) 
  2724)           ! -------------------------------------- !
  2725)           ! Below block is just a dignostic output !
  2726)           ! -------------------------------------- ! 
  2727) 
  2728)           excessu_arr(k) = excessu
  2729)           excess0_arr(k) = excess0
  2730)           xc_arr(k)      = xc
  2731)           aquad_arr(k)   = aquad
  2732)           bquad_arr(k)   = bquad
  2733)           cquad_arr(K)   = cquad
  2734)           bogbot_arr(k)  = bogbot
  2735)           bogtop_arr(k)  = bogtop
  2736) 
  2737)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2738)           ! 'kbup' is the upper most layer in which cloud buoyancy  is positive ! 
  2739)           ! both at the base and top interface.  'kpen' is the upper most layer !
  2740)           ! up to cumulus can reach. Usually, 'kpen' is located higher than the !
  2741)           ! 'kbup'. Note we initialized these by 'kbup = krel' & 'kpen = krel'. !
  2742)           ! As explained before, it is possible that only 'kpen' is updated,    !
  2743)           ! while 'kbup' keeps its initialization value. For this case, current !
  2744)           ! scheme will simply turns-off penetrative entrainment fluxes and use ! 
  2745)           ! normal buoyancy-sorting fluxes for 'kbup <= k <= kpen-1' interfaces,!
  2746)           ! in order to describe shallow continental cumulus convection.        !
  2747)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2748)           
  2749)         ! if( bogbot .gt. 0._r8 .and. bogtop .gt. 0._r8 ) then 
  2750)         ! if( bogtop .gt. 0._r8 ) then          
  2751)           if( bogtop .gt. 0._r8 .and. wtw .gt. 0._r8 ) then 
  2752)               kbup = k
  2753)           end if
  2754) 
  2755)           if( wtw .le. 0._r8 ) then
  2756)               kpen = k
  2757)               go to 45
  2758)           end if
  2759) 
  2760)           wu(k) = sqrt(wtw)
  2761)           if( wu(k) .gt. 100._r8 ) then
  2762)               exit_wu(i) = 1._r8
  2763)               id_exit = .true.
  2764)               go to 333
  2765)           endif
  2766) 
  2767)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2768)           ! Iteration end due to 'rmaxfrac' constraint [ ***************************** ] ! 
  2769)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2770) 
  2771)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2772)           ! Calculate updraft fractional area at the upper interface and set upper ! 
  2773)           ! limit to 'ufrc' by 'rmaxfrac'. In order to keep the consistency  among !
  2774)           ! ['ufrc','umf','wu (or wtw)'], if ufrc is limited by 'rmaxfrac', either !
  2775)           ! 'umf' or 'wu' should be changed. Although both 'umf' and 'wu (wtw)' at !
  2776)           ! the current upper interface are used for updating 'umf' & 'wu'  at the !
  2777)           ! next upper interface, 'umf' is a passive variable not influencing  the !
  2778)           ! buoyancy sorting process in contrast to 'wtw'. This is a reason why we !
  2779)           ! adjusted 'umf' instead of 'wtw'. In turn we updated 'fdr' here instead !
  2780)           ! of 'fer',  which guarantees  that all previously updated thermodynamic !
  2781)           ! variables at the upper interface before applying 'rmaxfrac' constraint !
  2782)           ! are already internally consistent,  even though 'ufrc'  is  limited by !
  2783)           ! 'rmaxfrac'. Thus, we don't need to go through interation loop again.If !
  2784)           ! If we update 'fer' however, we should go through above iteration loop. !
  2785)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2786)             
  2787)           rhos0j  = ps0(k) / ( r * 0.5_r8 * ( thv0bot(k+1) + thv0top(k) ) * exns0(k) )
  2788)           ufrc(k) = umf(k) / ( rhos0j * wu(k) )
  2789)           if( ufrc(k) .gt. rmaxfrac ) then
  2790)               limit_ufrc(i) = 1._r8 
  2791)               ufrc(k) = rmaxfrac
  2792)               umf(k)  = rmaxfrac * rhos0j * wu(k)
  2793)               fdr(k)  = fer(k) - log( umf(k) / umf(km1) ) / dpe
  2794)           endif
  2795) 
  2796)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2797)           ! Update environmental properties for at the mid-point of next !
  2798)           ! upper layer for use in buoyancy sorting.                     !
  2799)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  2800) 
  2801)           pe      = p0(k+1)
  2802)           dpe     = dp0(k+1)
  2803)           exne    = exn0(k+1)
  2804)           thvebot = thv0bot(k+1)
  2805)           thle    = thl0(k+1)
  2806)           qte     = qt0(k+1)
  2807)           ue      = u0(k+1)
  2808)           ve      = v0(k+1) 
  2809)           do m = 1, ncnst
  2810)              tre(m)  = tr0(k+1,m)
  2811)           enddo
  2812) 
  2813)        end do   ! End of cumulus updraft loop from the 'krel' layer to 'kpen' layer.
  2814)        
  2815)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2816)        ! Up to this point, we finished all of buoyancy sorting processes from the 'krel' !
  2817)        ! layer to 'kpen' layer: at the top interface of individual layers, we calculated !
  2818)        ! updraft and penetrative mass fluxes [ umf(k) & emf(k) = 0 ], updraft fractional !
  2819)        ! area [ ufrc(k) ],  updraft vertical velocity [ wu(k) ],  updraft  thermodynamic !
  2820)        ! variables [thlu(k),qtu(k),uu(k),vu(k),thvu(k)]. In the layer,we also calculated !
  2821)        ! fractional entrainment-detrainment rate [ fer(k), fdr(k) ], and detrainment ten !
  2822)        ! dency of water and ice from cumulus updraft [ dwten(k), diten(k) ]. In addition,!
  2823)        ! we updated and identified 'krel' and 'kpen' layer index, if any.  In the 'kpen' !
  2824)        ! layer, we calculated everything mentioned above except the 'wu(k)' and 'ufrc(k)'!
  2825)        ! since a real value of updraft vertical velocity is not defined at the kpen  top !
  2826)        ! interface (note 'ufrc' at the top interface of layer is calculated from 'umf(k)'!
  2827)        ! and 'wu(k)'). As mentioned before, special treatment is required when 'kbup' is !
  2828)        ! not updated and so 'kbup = krel'.                                               !
  2829)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2830)        
  2831)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2832)        ! During the 'iter_scaleh' iteration loop, non-physical ( with non-zero values ) !
  2833)        ! values can remain in the variable arrays above (also 'including' in case of wu !
  2834)        ! and ufrc at the top interface) the 'kpen' layer. This can happen when the kpen !
  2835)        ! layer index identified from the 'iter_scaleh = 1' iteration loop is located at !
  2836)        ! above the kpen layer index identified from   'iter_scaleh = 3' iteration loop. !
  2837)        ! Thus, in the following calculations, we should only use the values in each     !
  2838)        ! variables only up to finally identified 'kpen' layer & 'kpen' interface except ! 
  2839)        ! 'wu' and 'ufrc' at the top interface of 'kpen' layer.    Note that in order to !
  2840)        ! prevent any problems due to these non-physical values, I re-initialized    the !
  2841)        ! values of [ umf(kpen:mkx), emf(kpen:mkx), dwten(kpen+1:mkx), diten(kpen+1:mkx),! 
  2842)        ! fer(kpen:mkx), fdr(kpen+1:mkx), ufrc(kpen:mkx) ] to be zero after 'iter_scaleh'!
  2843)        ! do loop.                                                                       !
  2844)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2845)        
  2846)  45    continue
  2847)
