  2848)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2849)        ! Calculate 'ppen( < 0 )', updarft penetrative distance from the lower interface !
  2850)        ! of 'kpen' layer. Note that bogbot & bogtop at the 'kpen' layer either when fer !
  2851)        ! is zero or non-zero was already calculated above.                              !
  2852)        ! It seems that below qudarature solving formula is valid only when bogbot < 0.  !
  2853)        ! Below solving equation is clearly wrong ! I should revise this !               !
  2854)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  2855)             
  2856)        if( drage .eq. 0._r8 ) then
  2857)            aquad =  ( bogtop - bogbot ) / ( ps0(kpen) - ps0(kpen-1) )
  2858)            bquad =  2._r8 * bogbot
  2859)            cquad = -wu(kpen-1)**2 * rho0j
  2860)            call roots(aquad,bquad,cquad,xc1,xc2,status)
  2861)            if( status .eq. 0 ) then
  2862)                if( xc1 .le. 0._r8 .and. xc2 .le. 0._r8 ) then
  2863)                    ppen = max( xc1, xc2 )
  2864)                    ppen = min( 0._r8,max( -dp0(kpen), ppen ) )  
  2865)                elseif( xc1 .gt. 0._r8 .and. xc2 .gt. 0._r8 ) then
  2866)                    ppen = -dp0(kpen)
  2867)                    write(iulog,*) 'Warning : UW-Cumulus penetrates upto kpen interface'
  2868)                else
  2869)                    ppen = min( xc1, xc2 )
  2870)                    ppen = min( 0._r8,max( -dp0(kpen), ppen ) )  
  2871)                endif
  2872)            else
  2873)                ppen = -dp0(kpen)
  2874)                write(iulog,*) 'Warning : UW-Cumulus penetrates upto kpen interface'
  2875)            endif       
  2876)        else 
  2877)            ppen = compute_ppen(wtwb,drage,bogbot,bogtop,rho0j,dp0(kpen))
  2878)        endif
  2879)        if( ppen .eq. -dp0(kpen) .or. ppen .eq. 0._r8 ) limit_ppen(i) = 1._r8
  2880) 
  2881)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2882)        ! Re-calculate the amount of expelled condensate from cloud updraft    !
  2883)        ! at the cumulus top. This is necessary for refined calculations of    !
  2884)        ! bulk cloud microphysics at the cumulus top. Note that ppen < 0._r8   !
  2885)        ! In the below, I explicitly calculate 'thlu_top' & 'qtu_top' by       !
  2886)        ! using non-zero 'fer(kpen)'.                                          !    
  2887)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2888) 
  2889)        if( fer(kpen)*(-ppen) .lt. 1.e-4_r8 ) then
  2890)            thlu_top = thlu(kpen-1) + ( thl0(kpen) + ssthl0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8 - thlu(kpen-1) ) * fer(kpen) * (-ppen)
  2891)            qtu_top  =  qtu(kpen-1) + (  qt0(kpen) +  ssqt0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8  - qtu(kpen-1) ) * fer(kpen) * (-ppen)
  2892)        else
  2893)            thlu_top = ( thl0(kpen) + ssthl0(kpen) / fer(kpen) - ssthl0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8 ) - &
  2894)                       ( thl0(kpen) + ssthl0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8 - thlu(kpen-1) + ssthl0(kpen) / fer(kpen) ) &
  2895)                       * exp(-fer(kpen) * (-ppen))
  2896)            qtu_top  = ( qt0(kpen)  +  ssqt0(kpen) / fer(kpen) -  ssqt0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8 ) - &  
  2897)                       ( qt0(kpen)  +  ssqt0(kpen) * (-ppen) / 2._r8 -  qtu(kpen-1) +  ssqt0(kpen) / fer(kpen) ) &
  2898)                       * exp(-fer(kpen) * (-ppen))
  2899)        end if
  2900) 
  2901)        call conden(ps0(kpen-1)+ppen,thlu_top,qtu_top,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  2902)        if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  2903)            exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  2904)            id_exit = .true.
  2905)            go to 333
  2906)        end if
  2907)        exntop = ((ps0(kpen-1)+ppen)/p00)**rovcp
  2908)        if( (qlj + qij) .gt. criqc ) then
  2909)             dwten(kpen) = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qlj / ( qlj + qij )
  2910)             diten(kpen) = ( ( qlj + qij ) - criqc ) * qij / ( qlj + qij )
  2911)             qtu_top  = qtu_top - dwten(kpen) - diten(kpen)
  2912)             thlu_top = thlu_top + (xlv/cp/exntop)*dwten(kpen) + (xls/cp/exntop)*diten(kpen) 
  2913)        else
  2914)             dwten(kpen) = 0._r8
  2915)             diten(kpen) = 0._r8
  2916)        endif      
  2917)  
  2918)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2919)        ! Calculate cumulus scale height as the top height that cumulus can reach.!
  2920)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2921)        
  2922)        rhos0j = ps0(kpen-1)/(r*0.5_r8*(thv0bot(kpen)+thv0top(kpen-1))*exns0(kpen-1))  
  2923)        cush   = zs0(kpen-1) - ppen/rhos0j/g
  2924)        scaleh = cush 
  2925) 
  2926)     end do   ! End of 'iter_scaleh' loop.   
  2927) 
  2928)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !   
  2929)        ! The 'forcedCu' is logical identifier saying whether cumulus updraft  !
  2930)        ! overcome the buoyancy barrier just above the PBL top. If it is true, !
  2931)        ! cumulus did not overcome the barrier -  this is a shallow convection !
  2932)        ! with negative cloud buoyancy, mimicking  shallow continental cumulus !
  2933)        ! convection. Depending on 'forcedCu' parameter, treatment of heat  &  !
  2934)        ! moisture fluxes at the entraining interfaces, 'kbup <= k < kpen - 1' !
  2935)        ! will be set up in a different ways, as will be shown later.          !
  2936)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  2937)  
  2938)        if( kbup .eq. krel ) then 
  2939)            forcedCu = .true.
  2940)            limit_shcu(i) = 1._r8
  2941)        else
  2942)            forcedCu = .false.
  2943)            limit_shcu(i) = 0._r8
  2944)        endif  
  2945)        
  2946)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2947)        ! Filtering of unerasonable cumulus adjustment here.  This is a very !
  2948)        ! important process which should be done cautiously. Various ways of !
  2949)        ! filtering are possible depending on cases mainly using the indices !
  2950)        ! of key layers - 'klcl','kinv','krel','klfc','kbup','kpen'. At this !
  2951)        ! stage, the followings are all possible : 'kinv >= 2', 'klcl >= 1', !
  2952)        ! 'krel >= kinv', 'kbup >= krel', 'kpen >= krel'. I must design this !
  2953)        ! filtering very cautiously, in such that none of  realistic cumulus !
  2954)        ! convection is arbitrarily turned-off. Potentially, I might turn-off! 
  2955)        ! cumulus convection if layer-mean 'ql > 0' in the 'kinv-1' layer,in !
  2956)        ! order to suppress cumulus convection growing, based at the Sc top. ! 
  2957)        ! This is one of potential future modifications. Note that ppen < 0. !
  2958)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2959) 
  2960)        cldhgt = ps0(kpen-1) + ppen
  2961)        if( forcedCu ) then
  2962)            ! write(iulog,*) 'forcedCu - did not overcome initial buoyancy barrier'
  2963)            exit_cufilter(i) = 1._r8
  2964)            id_exit = .true.
  2965)            go to 333
  2966)        end if
  2967)        ! Limit 'additional shallow cumulus' for DYCOMS simulation.
  2968)        ! if( cldhgt.ge.88000._r8 ) then
  2969)        !     id_exit = .true.
  2970)        !     go to 333
  2971)        ! end if
  2972)        
  2973)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2974)        ! Re-initializing some key variables above the 'kpen' layer in order to suppress !
  2975)        ! the influence of non-physical values above 'kpen', in association with the use !
  2976)        ! of 'iter_scaleh' loop. Note that umf, emf,  ufrc are defined at the interfaces !
  2977)        ! (0:mkx), while 'dwten','diten', 'fer', 'fdr' are defined at layer mid-points.  !
  2978)        ! Initialization of 'fer' and 'fdr' is for correct writing purpose of diagnostic !
  2979)        ! output. Note that we set umf(kpen)=emf(kpen)=ufrc(kpen)=0, in consistent  with !
  2980)        ! wtw < 0  at the top interface of 'kpen' layer. However, we still have non-zero !
  2981)        ! expelled cloud condensate in the 'kpen' layer.                                 !
  2982)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2983) 
  2984)        umf(kpen:mkx)     = 0._r8
  2985)        emf(kpen:mkx)     = 0._r8
  2986)        ufrc(kpen:mkx)    = 0._r8
  2987)        dwten(kpen+1:mkx) = 0._r8
  2988)        diten(kpen+1:mkx) = 0._r8
  2989)        fer(kpen+1:mkx)   = 0._r8
  2990)        fdr(kpen+1:mkx)   = 0._r8
  2991)        
  2992)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  2993)        ! Calculate downward penetrative entrainment mass flux, 'emf(k) < 0',  and !
  2994)        ! thermodynamic properties of penetratively entrained airs at   entraining !
  2995)        ! interfaces. emf(k) is defined from the top interface of the  layer  kbup !
  2996)        ! to the bottom interface of the layer 'kpen'. Note even when  kbup = krel,!
  2997)        ! i.e.,even when 'kbup' was not updated in the above buoyancy  sorting  do !
  2998)        ! loop (i.e., 'kbup' remains as the initialization value),   below do loop !
  2999)        ! of penetrative entrainment flux can be performed without  any conceptual !
  3000)        ! or logical problems, because we have already computed all  the variables !
  3001)        ! necessary for performing below penetrative entrainment block.            !
  3002)        ! In the below 'do' loop, 'k' is an interface index at which non-zero 'emf'! 
  3003)        ! (penetrative entrainment mass flux) is calculated. Since cumulus updraft !
  3004)        ! is negatively buoyant in the layers between the top interface of 'kbup'  !
  3005)        ! layer (interface index, kbup) and the top interface of 'kpen' layer, the !
  3006)        ! fractional lateral entrainment, fer(k) within these layers will be close !
  3007)        ! to zero - so it is likely that only strong lateral detrainment occurs in !
  3008)        ! thses layers. Under this situation,we can easily calculate the amount of !
  3009)        ! detrainment cumulus air into these negatively buoyanct layers by  simply !
  3010)        ! comparing cumulus updraft mass fluxes between the base and top interface !
  3011)        ! of each layer: emf(k) = emf(k-1)*exp(-fdr(k)*dp0(k))                     !
  3012)        !                       ~ emf(k-1)*(1-rei(k)*dp0(k))                       !
  3013)        !                emf(k-1)-emf(k) ~ emf(k-1)*rei(k)*dp0(k)                  !
  3014)        ! Current code assumes that about 'rpen~10' times of these detrained  mass !
  3015)        ! are penetratively re-entrained down into the 'k-1' interface. And all of !
  3016)        ! these detrained masses are finally dumped down into the top interface of !
  3017)        ! 'kbup' layer. Thus, the amount of penetratively entrained air across the !
  3018)        ! top interface of 'kbup' layer with 'rpen~10' becomes too large.          !
  3019)        ! Note that this penetrative entrainment part can be completely turned-off !
  3020)        ! and we can simply use normal buoyancy-sorting involved turbulent  fluxes !
  3021)        ! by modifying 'penetrative entrainment fluxes' part below.                !
  3022)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3023)        
  3024)        ! -----------------------------------------------------------------------!
  3025)        ! Calculate entrainment mass flux and conservative scalars of entraining !
  3026)        ! free air at interfaces of 'kbup <= k < kpen - 1'                       !
  3027)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3028)  
  3029)        do k = 0, mkx
  3030)           thlu_emf(k) = thlu(k)
  3031)           qtu_emf(k)  = qtu(k)
  3032)           uu_emf(k)   = uu(k)
  3033)           vu_emf(k)   = vu(k)
  3034)           do m = 1, ncnst
  3035)              tru_emf(k,m)  = tru(k,m)
  3036)           enddo
  3037)        end do
  3038) 
  3039)        do k = kpen - 1, kbup, -1  ! Here, 'k' is an interface index at which
  3040)                                   ! penetrative entrainment fluxes are calculated. 
  3041)                                   
  3042)           rhos0j = ps0(k) / ( r * 0.5_r8 * ( thv0bot(k+1) + thv0top(k) ) * exns0(k) )
  3043) 
  3044)           if( k .eq. kpen - 1 ) then
  3045) 
  3046)              ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ ! 
  3047)              ! Note that 'ppen' has already been calculated in the above 'iter_scaleh'  !
  3048)              ! loop assuming zero lateral entrainmentin the layer 'kpen'.               !
  3049)              ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !       
  3050)              
  3051)              ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3052)              ! Calculate returning mass flux, emf ( < 0 )                           !
  3053)              ! Current penetrative entrainment rate with 'rpen~10' is too large and !
  3054)              ! future refinement is necessary including the definition of 'thl','qt'! 
  3055)              ! of penetratively entrained air.  Penetratively entrained airs across !
  3056)              ! the 'kpen-1' interface is assumed to have the properties of the base !
  3057)              ! interface of 'kpen' layer. Note that 'emf ~ - umf/ufrc = - w * rho'. !
  3058)              ! Thus, below limit sets an upper limit of |emf| to be ~ 10cm/s, which !
  3059)              ! is very loose constraint. Here, I used more restricted constraint on !
  3060)              ! the limit of emf, assuming 'emf' cannot exceed a net mass within the !
  3061)              ! layer above the interface. Similar to the case of warming and drying !
  3062)              ! due to cumulus updraft induced compensating subsidence,  penetrative !
  3063)              ! entrainment induces compensating upwelling -     in order to prevent !  
  3064)              ! numerical instability in association with compensating upwelling, we !
  3065)              ! should similarily limit the amount of penetrative entrainment at the !
  3066)              ! interface by the amount of masses within the layer just above the    !
  3067)              ! penetratively entraining interface.                                  !
  3068)              ! -------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3069)              
  3070)              if( ( umf(k)*ppen*rei(kpen)*rpen ) .lt. -0.1_r8*rhos0j )         limit_emf(i) = 1._r8
  3071)              if( ( umf(k)*ppen*rei(kpen)*rpen ) .lt. -0.9_r8*dp0(kpen)/g/dt ) limit_emf(i) = 1._r8             
  3072) 
  3073)              emf(k) = max( max( umf(k)*ppen*rei(kpen)*rpen, -0.1_r8*rhos0j), -0.9_r8*dp0(kpen)/g/dt)
  3074)              thlu_emf(k) = thl0(kpen) + ssthl0(kpen) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kpen) )
  3075)              qtu_emf(k)  = qt0(kpen)  + ssqt0(kpen)  * ( ps0(k) - p0(kpen) )
  3076)              uu_emf(k)   = u0(kpen)   + ssu0(kpen)   * ( ps0(k) - p0(kpen) )     
  3077)              vu_emf(k)   = v0(kpen)   + ssv0(kpen)   * ( ps0(k) - p0(kpen) )   
  3078)              do m = 1, ncnst
  3079)                 tru_emf(k,m)  = tr0(kpen,m)  + sstr0(kpen,m)  * ( ps0(k) - p0(kpen) )
  3080)              enddo
  3081) 
  3082)           else ! if(k.lt.kpen-1). 
  3083)               
  3084)              ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3085)              ! Note we are coming down from the higher interfaces to the lower interfaces. !
  3086)              ! Also note that 'emf < 0'. So, below operation is a summing not subtracting. !
  3087)              ! In order to ensure numerical stability, I imposed a modified correct limit  ! 
  3088)              ! of '-0.9*dp0(k+1)/g/dt' on emf(k).                                          !
  3089)              ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3090) 
  3091)              if( use_cumpenent ) then  ! Original Cumulative Penetrative Entrainment
  3092) 
  3093)                  if( ( emf(k+1)-umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen ) .lt. -0.1_r8*rhos0j )        limit_emf(i) = 1
  3094)                  if( ( emf(k+1)-umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen ) .lt. -0.9_r8*dp0(k+1)/g/dt ) limit_emf(i) = 1         
  3095)                  emf(k) = max(max(emf(k+1)-umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen, -0.1_r8*rhos0j), -0.9_r8*dp0(k+1)/g/dt )    
  3096)                  if( abs(emf(k)) .gt. abs(emf(k+1)) ) then
  3097)                      thlu_emf(k) = ( thlu_emf(k+1) * emf(k+1) + thl0(k+1) * ( emf(k) - emf(k+1) ) ) / emf(k)
  3098)                      qtu_emf(k)  = ( qtu_emf(k+1)  * emf(k+1) + qt0(k+1)  * ( emf(k) - emf(k+1) ) ) / emf(k)
  3099)                      uu_emf(k)   = ( uu_emf(k+1)   * emf(k+1) + u0(k+1)   * ( emf(k) - emf(k+1) ) ) / emf(k)
  3100)                      vu_emf(k)   = ( vu_emf(k+1)   * emf(k+1) + v0(k+1)   * ( emf(k) - emf(k+1) ) ) / emf(k)
  3101)                      do m = 1, ncnst
  3102)                         tru_emf(k,m)  = ( tru_emf(k+1,m)  * emf(k+1) + tr0(k+1,m)  * ( emf(k) - emf(k+1) ) ) / emf(k)
  3103)                      enddo
  3104)                  else   
  3105)                      thlu_emf(k) = thl0(k+1)
  3106)                      qtu_emf(k)  =  qt0(k+1)
  3107)                      uu_emf(k)   =   u0(k+1)
  3108)                      vu_emf(k)   =   v0(k+1)
  3109)                      do m = 1, ncnst
  3110)                         tru_emf(k,m)  =  tr0(k+1,m)
  3111)                      enddo
  3112)                  endif   
  3113)                      
  3114)              else ! Alternative Non-Cumulative Penetrative Entrainment
  3115) 
  3116)                  if( ( -umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen ) .lt. -0.1_r8*rhos0j )        limit_emf(i) = 1
  3117)                  if( ( -umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen ) .lt. -0.9_r8*dp0(k+1)/g/dt ) limit_emf(i) = 1         
  3118)                  emf(k) = max(max(-umf(k)*dp0(k+1)*rei(k+1)*rpen, -0.1_r8*rhos0j), -0.9_r8*dp0(k+1)/g/dt )    
  3119)                  thlu_emf(k) = thl0(k+1)
  3120)                  qtu_emf(k)  =  qt0(k+1)
  3121)                  uu_emf(k)   =   u0(k+1)
  3122)                  vu_emf(k)   =   v0(k+1)
  3123)                  do m = 1, ncnst
  3124)                     tru_emf(k,m)  =  tr0(k+1,m)
  3125)                  enddo
  3126) 
  3127)              endif
  3128) 
  3129)           endif
  3130) 
  3131)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3132)           ! In this GCM modeling framework,  all what we should do is to calculate  heat !
  3133)           ! and moisture fluxes at the given geometrically-fixed height interfaces -  we !
  3134)           ! don't need to worry about movement of material height surface in association !
  3135)           ! with compensating subsidence or unwelling, in contrast to the bulk modeling. !
  3136)           ! In this geometrically fixed height coordinate system, heat and moisture flux !
  3137)           ! at the geometrically fixed height handle everything - a movement of material !
  3138)           ! surface is implicitly treated automatically. Note that in terms of turbulent !
  3139)           ! heat and moisture fluxes at model interfaces, both the cumulus updraft  mass !
  3140)           ! flux and penetratively entraining mass flux play the same role -both of them ! 
  3141)           ! warms and dries the 'kbup' layer, cools and moistens the 'kpen' layer,   and !
  3142)           ! cools and moistens any intervening layers between 'kbup' and 'kpen' layers.  !
  3143)           ! It is important to note these identical roles on turbulent heat and moisture !
  3144)           ! fluxes of 'umf' and 'emf'.                                                   !
  3145)           ! When 'kbup' is a stratocumulus-topped PBL top interface,  increase of 'rpen' !
  3146)           ! is likely to strongly diffuse stratocumulus top interface,  resulting in the !
  3147)           ! reduction of cloud fraction. In this sense, the 'kbup' interface has a  very !
  3148)           ! important meaning and role : across the 'kbup' interface, strong penetrative !
  3149)           ! entrainment occurs, thus any sharp gradient properties across that interface !
  3150)           ! are easily diffused through strong mass exchange. Thus, an initialization of ! 
  3151)           ! 'kbup' (and also 'kpen') should be done very cautiously as mentioned before. ! 
  3152)           ! In order to prevent this stron diffusion for the shallow cumulus convection  !
  3153)           ! based at the Sc top, it seems to be good to initialize 'kbup = krel', rather !
  3154)           ! that 'kbup = krel-1'.                                                        !
  3155)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3156)           
  3157)        end do
  3158) 
  3159)        !------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3160)        !                                                                   ! 
  3161)        ! Compute turbulent heat, moisture, momentum flux at all interfaces !
  3162)        !                                                                   !
  3163)        !------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3164)        ! It is very important to note that in calculating turbulent fluxes !
  3165)        ! below, we must not double count turbulent flux at any interefaces.!
  3166)        ! In the below, turbulent fluxes at the interfaces (interface index !
  3167)        ! k) are calculated by the following 4 blocks in consecutive order: !
  3168)        !                                                                   !
  3169)        ! (1) " 0 <= k <= kinv - 1 "  : PBL fluxes.                         !
  3170)        !     From 'fluxbelowinv' using reconstructed PBL height. Currently,!
  3171)        !     the reconstructed PBLs are independently calculated for  each !
  3172)        !     individual conservative scalar variables ( qt, thl, u, v ) in !
  3173)        !     each 'fluxbelowinv',  instead of being uniquely calculated by !
  3174)        !     using thvl. Turbulent flux at the surface is assumed to be 0. !
  3175)        ! (2) " kinv <= k <= krel - 1 " : Non-buoyancy sorting fluxes       !
  3176)        !     Assuming cumulus mass flux  and cumulus updraft thermodynamic !
  3177)        !     properties (except u, v which are modified by the PGFc during !
  3178)        !     upward motion) are conserved during a updraft motion from the !
  3179)        !     PBL top interface to the release level. If these layers don't !
  3180)        !     exist (e,g, when 'krel = kinv'), then  current routine do not !
  3181)        !     perform this routine automatically. So I don't need to modify !
  3182)        !     anything.                                                     ! 
  3183)        ! (3) " krel <= k <= kbup - 1 " : Buoyancy sorting fluxes           !
  3184)        !     From laterally entraining-detraining buoyancy sorting plumes. ! 
  3185)        ! (4) " kbup <= k < kpen-1 " : Penetrative entrainment fluxes       !
  3186)        !     From penetratively entraining plumes,                         !
  3187)        !                                                                   !
  3188)        ! In case of normal situation, turbulent interfaces  in each groups !
  3189)        ! are mutually independent of each other. Thus double flux counting !
  3190)        ! or ambiguous flux counting requiring the choice among the above 4 !
  3191)        ! groups do not occur normally. However, in case that cumulus plume !
  3192)        ! could not completely overcome the buoyancy barrier just above the !
  3193)        ! PBL top interface and so 'kbup = krel' (.forcedCu=.true.) ( here, !
  3194)        ! it can be either 'kpen = krel' as the initialization, or ' kpen > !
  3195)        ! krel' if cumulus updraft just penetrated over the top of  release !
  3196)        ! layer ). If this happens, we should be very careful in organizing !
  3197)        ! the sequence of the 4 calculation routines above -  note that the !
  3198)        ! routine located at the later has the higher priority.  Additional ! 
  3199)        ! feature I must consider is that when 'kbup = kinv - 1' (this is a !
  3200)        ! combined situation of 'kbup=krel-1' & 'krel = kinv' when I  chose !
  3201)        ! 'kbup=krel-1' instead of current choice of 'kbup=krel'), a strong !
  3202)        ! penetrative entrainment fluxes exists at the PBL top interface, & !
  3203)        ! all of these fluxes are concentrated (deposited) within the layer ! 
  3204)        ! just below PBL top interface (i.e., 'kinv-1' layer). On the other !
  3205)        ! hand, in case of 'fluxbelowinv', only the compensating subsidence !
  3206)        ! effect is concentrated in the 'kinv-1' layer and 'pure' turbulent !
  3207)        ! heat and moisture fluxes ( 'pure' means the fluxes not associated !
  3208)        ! with compensating subsidence) are linearly distributed throughout !
  3209)        ! the whole PBL. Thus different choice of the above flux groups can !
  3210)        ! produce very different results. Output variable should be written !
  3211)        ! consistently to the choice of computation sequences.              !
  3212)        ! When the case of 'kbup = krel(-1)' happens,another way to dealing !
  3213)        ! with this case is to simply ' exit ' the whole cumulus convection !
  3214)        ! calculation without performing any cumulus convection.     We can !
  3215)        ! choose this approach by specifying a condition in the  'Filtering !
  3216)        ! of unreasonable cumulus adjustment' just after 'iter_scaleh'. But !
  3217)        ! this seems not to be a good choice (although this choice was used !
  3218)        ! previous code ), since it might arbitrary damped-out  the shallow !
  3219)        ! cumulus convection over the continent land, where shallow cumulus ! 
  3220)        ! convection tends to be negatively buoyant.                        !
  3221)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !  
  3222) 
  3223)        ! --------------------------------------------------- !
  3224)        ! 1. PBL fluxes :  0 <= k <= kinv - 1                 !
  3225)        !    All the information necessary to reconstruct PBL ! 
  3226)        !    height are passed to 'fluxbelowinv'.             !
  3227)        ! --------------------------------------------------- !
  3228) 
  3229)        xsrc  = qtsrc
  3230)        xmean = qt0(kinv)
  3231)        xtop  = qt0(kinv+1) + ssqt0(kinv+1) * ( ps0(kinv)   - p0(kinv+1) )
  3232)        xbot  = qt0(kinv-1) + ssqt0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )        
  3233)        call fluxbelowinv( cbmf, ps0(0:mkx), mkx, kinv, dt, xsrc, xmean, xtop, xbot, xflx )
  3234)        qtflx(0:kinv-1) = xflx(0:kinv-1)
  3235) 
  3236)        xsrc  = thlsrc
  3237)        xmean = thl0(kinv)
  3238)        xtop  = thl0(kinv+1) + ssthl0(kinv+1) * ( ps0(kinv)   - p0(kinv+1) )
  3239)        xbot  = thl0(kinv-1) + ssthl0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )        
  3240)        call fluxbelowinv( cbmf, ps0(0:mkx), mkx, kinv, dt, xsrc, xmean, xtop, xbot, xflx )
  3241)        slflx(0:kinv-1) = cp * exns0(0:kinv-1) * xflx(0:kinv-1)
  3242) 
  3243)        xsrc  = usrc
  3244)        xmean = u0(kinv)
  3245)        xtop  = u0(kinv+1) + ssu0(kinv+1) * ( ps0(kinv)   - p0(kinv+1) )
  3246)        xbot  = u0(kinv-1) + ssu0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )
  3247)        call fluxbelowinv( cbmf, ps0(0:mkx), mkx, kinv, dt, xsrc, xmean, xtop, xbot, xflx )
  3248)        uflx(0:kinv-1) = xflx(0:kinv-1)
  3249) 
  3250)        xsrc  = vsrc
  3251)        xmean = v0(kinv)
  3252)        xtop  = v0(kinv+1) + ssv0(kinv+1) * ( ps0(kinv)   - p0(kinv+1) )
  3253)        xbot  = v0(kinv-1) + ssv0(kinv-1) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )
  3254)        call fluxbelowinv( cbmf, ps0(0:mkx), mkx, kinv, dt, xsrc, xmean, xtop, xbot, xflx )
  3255)        vflx(0:kinv-1) = xflx(0:kinv-1)
  3256) 
  3257)        do m = 1, ncnst
  3258)           xsrc  = trsrc(m)
  3259)           xmean = tr0(kinv,m)
  3260)           xtop  = tr0(kinv+1,m) + sstr0(kinv+1,m) * ( ps0(kinv)   - p0(kinv+1) )
  3261)           xbot  = tr0(kinv-1,m) + sstr0(kinv-1,m) * ( ps0(kinv-1) - p0(kinv-1) )        
  3262)           call fluxbelowinv( cbmf, ps0(0:mkx), mkx, kinv, dt, xsrc, xmean, xtop, xbot, xflx )
  3263)           trflx(0:kinv-1,m) = xflx(0:kinv-1)
  3264)        enddo
  3265) 
  3266)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3267)        ! 2. Non-buoyancy sorting fluxes : kinv <= k <= krel - 1         !
  3268)        !    Note that when 'krel = kinv', below block is never executed !
  3269)        !    as in a desirable, expected way ( but I must check  if this !
  3270)        !    is the case ). The non-buoyancy sorting fluxes are computed !
  3271)        !    only when 'krel > kinv'.                                    !
  3272)        ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !          
  3273) 
  3274)        uplus = 0._r8
  3275)        vplus = 0._r8
  3276)        do k = kinv, krel - 1
  3277)           kp1 = k + 1
  3278)           qtflx(k) = cbmf * ( qtsrc  - (  qt0(kp1) +  ssqt0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )          
  3279)           slflx(k) = cbmf * ( thlsrc - ( thl0(kp1) + ssthl0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) * cp * exns0(k)
  3280)           uplus    = uplus + PGFc * ssu0(k) * ( ps0(k) - ps0(k-1) )
  3281)           vplus    = vplus + PGFc * ssv0(k) * ( ps0(k) - ps0(k-1) )
  3282)           uflx(k)  = cbmf * ( usrc + uplus -  (  u0(kp1)  +   ssu0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) 
  3283)           vflx(k)  = cbmf * ( vsrc + vplus -  (  v0(kp1)  +   ssv0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3284)           do m = 1, ncnst
  3285)              trflx(k,m) = cbmf * ( trsrc(m)  - (  tr0(kp1,m) +  sstr0(kp1,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3286)           enddo          
  3287)        end do
  3288) 
  3289)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3290)        ! 3. Buoyancy sorting fluxes : krel <= k <= kbup - 1                       !
  3291)        !    In case that 'kbup = krel - 1 ' ( or even in case 'kbup = krel' ),    ! 
  3292)        !    buoyancy sorting fluxes are not calculated, which is consistent,      !
  3293)        !    desirable feature.                                                    !  
  3294)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3295) 
  3296)        do k = krel, kbup - 1      
  3297)           kp1 = k + 1
  3298)           slflx(k) = cp * exns0(k) * umf(k) * ( thlu(k) - ( thl0(kp1) + ssthl0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3299)           qtflx(k) = umf(k) * ( qtu(k) - ( qt0(kp1) + ssqt0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3300)           uflx(k)  = umf(k) * ( uu(k) - ( u0(kp1) + ssu0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3301)           vflx(k)  = umf(k) * ( vu(k) - ( v0(kp1) + ssv0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3302)           do m = 1, ncnst
  3303)              trflx(k,m) = umf(k) * ( tru(k,m) - ( tr0(kp1,m) + sstr0(kp1,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )
  3304)           enddo
  3305)        end do
  3306) 
  3307)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3308)        ! 4. Penetrative entrainment fluxes : kbup <= k <= kpen - 1                 !
  3309)        !    The only confliction that can happen is when 'kbup = kinv-1'. For this !
  3310)        !    case, turbulent flux at kinv-1 is calculated  both from 'fluxbelowinv' !
  3311)        !    and here as penetrative entrainment fluxes.  Since penetrative flux is !
  3312)        !    calculated later, flux at 'kinv - 1 ' will be that of penetrative flux.!
  3313)        !    However, turbulent flux calculated at 'kinv - 1' from penetrative entr.!
  3314)        !    is less attractable,  since more reasonable turbulent flux at 'kinv-1' !
  3315)        !    should be obtained from 'fluxbelowinv', by considering  re-constructed ! 
  3316)        !    inversion base height. This conflicting problem can be solved if we can!
  3317)        !    initialize 'kbup = krel', instead of kbup = krel - 1. This choice seems!
  3318)        !    to be more reasonable since it is not conflicted with 'fluxbelowinv' in!
  3319)        !    calculating fluxes at 'kinv - 1' ( for this case, flux at 'kinv-1' is  !
  3320)        !    always from 'fluxbelowinv' ), and flux at 'krel-1' is calculated from  !
  3321)        !    the non-buoyancy sorting flux without being competed with penetrative  !
  3322)        !    entrainment fluxes. Even when we use normal cumulus flux instead of    !
  3323)        !    penetrative entrainment fluxes at 'kbup <= k <= kpen-1' interfaces,    !
  3324)        !    the initialization of kbup=krel perfectly works without any conceptual !
  3325)        !    confliction. Thus it seems to be much better to choose 'kbup = krel'   !
  3326)        !    initialization of 'kbup', which is current choice.                     !
  3327)        !    Note that below formula uses conventional updraft cumulus fluxes for   !
  3328)        !    shallow cumulus which did not overcome the first buoyancy barrier above!
  3329)        !    PBL top while uses penetrative entrainment fluxes for the other cases  !
  3330)        !    'kbup <= k <= kpen-1' interfaces. Depending on cases, however, I can   !
  3331)        !    selelct different choice.                                              !
  3332)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3333)        !   if( forcedCu ) then                                                                                              !
  3334)        !       slflx(k) = cp * exns0(k) * umf(k) * ( thlu(k) - ( thl0(kp1) + ssthl0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )         !
  3335)        !       qtflx(k) =                 umf(k) * (  qtu(k) - (  qt0(kp1) +  ssqt0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )         !
  3336)        !       uflx(k)  =                 umf(k) * (   uu(k) - (   u0(kp1) +   ssu0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )         !
  3337)        !       vflx(k)  =                 umf(k) * (   vu(k) - (   v0(kp1) +   ssv0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )         !
  3338)        !       do m = 1, ncnst                                                                                              !
  3339)        !          trflx(k,m) = umf(k) * ( tru(k,m) - ( tr0(kp1,m) + sstr0(kp1,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) )                 !
  3340)        !       enddo                                                                                                        !
  3341)        !   else                                                                                                             !
  3342)        !       slflx(k) = cp * exns0(k) * emf(k) * ( thlu_emf(k) - ( thl0(k) + ssthl0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )           !
  3343)        !       qtflx(k) =                 emf(k) * (  qtu_emf(k) - (  qt0(k) +  ssqt0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )           !
  3344)        !       uflx(k)  =                 emf(k) * (   uu_emf(k) - (   u0(k) +   ssu0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )           !
  3345)        !       vflx(k)  =                 emf(k) * (   vu_emf(k) - (   v0(k) +   ssv0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )           !
  3346)        !       do m = 1, ncnst                                                                                              !
  3347)        !          trflx(k,m) = emf(k) * ( tru_emf(k,m) - ( tr0(k,m) + sstr0(k,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )                   !
  3348)        !       enddo                                                                                                        !
  3349)        !   endif                                                                                                            !
  3350)        !                                                                                                                    !
  3351)        !   if( use_uppenent ) then ! Combined Updraft + Penetrative Entrainment Flux                                        !
  3352)        !       slflx(k) = cp * exns0(k) * umf(k) * ( thlu(k)     - ( thl0(kp1) + ssthl0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) + & !
  3353)        !                  cp * exns0(k) * emf(k) * ( thlu_emf(k) - (   thl0(k) +   ssthl0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )       !
  3354)        !       qtflx(k) =                 umf(k) * (  qtu(k)     - (  qt0(kp1) +  ssqt0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) + & !
  3355)        !                                  emf(k) * (  qtu_emf(k) - (    qt0(k) +    ssqt0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )       !
  3356)        !       uflx(k)  =                 umf(k) * (   uu(k)     - (   u0(kp1) +   ssu0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) + & !
  3357)        !                                  emf(k) * (   uu_emf(k) - (     u0(k) +     ssu0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )       !
  3358)        !       vflx(k)  =                 umf(k) * (   vu(k)     - (   v0(kp1) +   ssv0(kp1) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) + & !
  3359)        !                                  emf(k) * (   vu_emf(k) - (     v0(k) +     ssv0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )       !
  3360)        !       do m = 1, ncnst                                                                                              !
  3361)        !          trflx(k,m) = umf(k) * ( tru(k,m) - ( tr0(kp1,m) + sstr0(kp1,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(kp1) ) ) ) + &             ! 
  3362)        !                       emf(k) * ( tru_emf(k,m) - ( tr0(k,m) + sstr0(k,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )                   ! 
  3363)        !       enddo                                                                                                        !
  3364)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3365) 
  3366)        do k = kbup, kpen - 1      
  3367)           kp1 = k + 1
  3368)           slflx(k) = cp * exns0(k) * emf(k) * ( thlu_emf(k) - ( thl0(k) + ssthl0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )
  3369)           qtflx(k) =                 emf(k) * (  qtu_emf(k) - (  qt0(k) +  ssqt0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) ) 
  3370)           uflx(k)  =                 emf(k) * (   uu_emf(k) - (   u0(k) +   ssu0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) ) 
  3371)           vflx(k)  =                 emf(k) * (   vu_emf(k) - (   v0(k) +   ssv0(k) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) )
  3372)           do m = 1, ncnst
  3373)              trflx(k,m) = emf(k) * ( tru_emf(k,m) - ( tr0(k,m) + sstr0(k,m) * ( ps0(k) - p0(k) ) ) ) 
  3374)           enddo
  3375)        end do
  3376) 
  3377)        ! ------------------------------------------- !
  3378)        ! Turn-off cumulus momentum flux as an option !
  3379)        ! ------------------------------------------- !
  3380) 
  3381)        if( .not. use_momenflx ) then
  3382)            uflx(0:mkx) = 0._r8
  3383)            vflx(0:mkx) = 0._r8
  3384)        endif       
  3385) 
  3386)        ! -------------------------------------------------------- !
  3387)        ! Condensate tendency by compensating subsidence/upwelling !
  3388)        ! -------------------------------------------------------- !
  3389)        
  3390)        uemf(0:mkx)         = 0._r8
  3391)        do k = 0, kinv - 2  ! Assume linear updraft mass flux within the PBL.
  3392)           uemf(k) = cbmf * ( ps0(0) - ps0(k) ) / ( ps0(0) - ps0(kinv-1) ) 
  3393)        end do
  3394)        uemf(kinv-1:krel-1) = cbmf
  3395)        uemf(krel:kbup-1)   = umf(krel:kbup-1)
  3396)        uemf(kbup:kpen-1)   = emf(kbup:kpen-1) ! Only use penetrative entrainment flux consistently.
  3397) 
  3398)        comsub(1:mkx) = 0._r8
  3399)        do k = 1, kpen
  3400)           comsub(k)  = 0.5_r8 * ( uemf(k) + uemf(k-1) ) 
  3401)        end do    
  3402) 
  3403)        do k = 1, kpen
  3404)           if( comsub(k) .ge. 0._r8 ) then
  3405)               if( k .eq. mkx ) then
  3406)                   thlten_sub = 0._r8
  3407)                   qtten_sub  = 0._r8
  3408)                   qlten_sub  = 0._r8
  3409)                   qiten_sub  = 0._r8
  3410)                   nlten_sub  = 0._r8
  3411)                   niten_sub  = 0._r8
  3412)               else
  3413)                   thlten_sub = g * comsub(k) * ( thl0(k+1) - thl0(k) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3414)                   qtten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  qt0(k+1) -  qt0(k) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3415)                   qlten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  ql0(k+1) -  ql0(k) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3416)                   qiten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  qi0(k+1) -  qi0(k) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3417)                   nlten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  tr0(k+1,ixnumliq) -  tr0(k,ixnumliq) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3418)                   niten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  tr0(k+1,ixnumice) -  tr0(k,ixnumice) ) / ( p0(k) - p0(k+1) )
  3419)               endif
  3420)           else
  3421)               if( k .eq. 1 ) then
  3422)                   thlten_sub = 0._r8
  3423)                   qtten_sub  = 0._r8
  3424)                   qlten_sub  = 0._r8
  3425)                   qiten_sub  = 0._r8
  3426)                   nlten_sub  = 0._r8
  3427)                   niten_sub  = 0._r8
  3428)               else
  3429)                   thlten_sub = g * comsub(k) * ( thl0(k) - thl0(k-1) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3430)                   qtten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  qt0(k) -  qt0(k-1) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3431)                   qlten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  ql0(k) -  ql0(k-1) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3432)                   qiten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  qi0(k) -  qi0(k-1) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3433)                   nlten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  tr0(k,ixnumliq) -  tr0(k-1,ixnumliq) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3434)                   niten_sub  = g * comsub(k) * (  tr0(k,ixnumice) -  tr0(k-1,ixnumice) ) / ( p0(k-1) - p0(k) )
  3435)               endif
  3436)           endif
  3437)           thl_prog = thl0(k) + thlten_sub * dt
  3438)           qt_prog  = max( qt0(k) + qtten_sub * dt, 1.e-12_r8 )
  3439)           call conden(p0(k),thl_prog,qt_prog,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  3440)           if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3441)               id_exit = .true.
  3442)               go to 333
  3443)           endif
  3444)         ! qlten_sink(k) = ( qlj - ql0(k) ) / dt
  3445)         ! qiten_sink(k) = ( qij - qi0(k) ) / dt
  3446)           qlten_sink(k) = max( qlten_sub, - ql0(k) / dt ) ! For consistency with prognostic macrophysics scheme
  3447)           qiten_sink(k) = max( qiten_sub, - qi0(k) / dt ) ! For consistency with prognostic macrophysics scheme
  3448)           nlten_sink(k) = max( nlten_sub, - tr0(k,ixnumliq) / dt ) 
  3449)           niten_sink(k) = max( niten_sub, - tr0(k,ixnumice) / dt )
  3450)        end do
  3451) 
  3452)        ! --------------------------------------------- !
  3453)        !                                               !
  3454)        ! Calculate convective tendencies at each layer ! 
  3455)        !                                               !
  3456)        ! --------------------------------------------- !
  3457)        
  3458)        ! ----------------- !
  3459)        ! Momentum tendency !
  3460)        ! ----------------- !
  3461)        
  3462)        do k = 1, kpen
  3463)           km1 = k - 1 
  3464)           uten(k) = ( uflx(km1) - uflx(k) ) * g / dp0(k)
  3465)           vten(k) = ( vflx(km1) - vflx(k) ) * g / dp0(k) 
  3466)           uf(k)   = u0(k) + uten(k) * dt
  3467)           vf(k)   = v0(k) + vten(k) * dt
  3468)         ! do m = 1, ncnst
  3469)         !    trten(k,m) = ( trflx(km1,m) - trflx(k,m) ) * g / dp0(k)
  3470)         !  ! Limit trten(k,m) such that negative value is not developed.
  3471)         !  ! This limitation does not conserve grid-mean tracers and future
  3472)         !  ! refinement is required for tracer-conserving treatment.
  3473)         !    trten(k,m) = max(trten(k,m),-tr0(k,m)/dt)              
  3474)         ! enddo
  3475)        end do        
  3476) 
  3477)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3478)        ! Tendencies of thermodynamic variables.                            ! 
  3479)        ! This part requires a careful treatment of bulk cloud microphysics.!
  3480)        ! Relocations of 'precipitable condensates' either into the surface ! 
  3481)        ! or into the tendency of 'krel' layer will be performed just after !
  3482)        ! finishing the below 'do-loop'.                                    !        
  3483)        ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3484)        
  3485)        rliq    = 0._r8
  3486)        rainflx = 0._r8
  3487)        snowflx = 0._r8
  3488) 
  3489)        do k = 1, kpen
  3490) 
  3491)           km1 = k - 1
  3492) 
  3493)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3494)           ! Compute 'slten', 'qtten', 'qvten', 'qlten', 'qiten', and 'sten'                !
  3495)           !                                                                                !
  3496)           ! Key assumptions made in this 'cumulus scheme' are :                            !
  3497)           ! 1. Cumulus updraft expels condensate into the environment at the top interface !
  3498)           !    of each layer. Note that in addition to this expel process ('source' term), !
  3499)           !    cumulus updraft can modify layer mean condensate through normal detrainment !
  3500)           !    forcing or compensating subsidence.                                         !
  3501)           ! 2. Expelled water can be either 'sustaining' or 'precipitating' condensate. By !
  3502)           !    definition, 'suataining condensate' will remain in the layer where it was   !
  3503)           !    formed, while 'precipitating condensate' will fall across the base of the   !
  3504)           !    layer where it was formed.                                                  !
  3505)           ! 3. All precipitating condensates are assumed to fall into the release layer or !
  3506)           !    ground as soon as it was formed without being evaporated during the falling !
  3507)           !    process down to the desinated layer ( either release layer of surface ).    !
  3508)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3509) 
  3510)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !     
  3511)           ! 'dwten(k)','diten(k)' : Production rate of condensate  within the layer k !
  3512)           !      [ kg/kg/s ]        by the expels of condensate from cumulus updraft. !
  3513)           ! It is important to note that in terms of moisture tendency equation, this !
  3514)           ! is a 'source' term of enviromental 'qt'.  More importantly,  these source !
  3515)           ! are already counted in the turbulent heat and moisture fluxes we computed !
  3516)           ! until now, assuming all the expelled condensate remain in the layer where ! 
  3517)           ! it was formed. Thus, in calculation of 'qtten' and 'slten' below, we MUST !
  3518)           ! NOT add or subtract these terms explicitly in order not to double or miss !
  3519)           ! count, unless some expelled condensates fall down out of the layer.  Note !
  3520)           ! this falling-down process ( i.e., precipitation process ) and  associated !
  3521)           ! 'qtten' and 'slten' and production of surface precipitation flux  will be !
  3522)           ! treated later in 'zm_conv_evap' in 'convect_shallow_tend' subroutine.     ! 
  3523)           ! In below, we are converting expelled cloud condensate into correct unit.  !
  3524)           ! I found that below use of '0.5 * (umf(k-1) + umf(k))' causes conservation !
  3525)           ! errors at some columns in global simulation. So, I returned to originals. !
  3526)           ! This will cause no precipitation flux at 'kpen' layer since umf(kpen)=0.  !
  3527)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3528) 
  3529)           dwten(k) = dwten(k) * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * g / dp0(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3530)           diten(k) = diten(k) * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * g / dp0(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]  
  3531) 
  3532)           ! dwten(k) = dwten(k) * umf(k) * g / dp0(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3533)           ! diten(k) = diten(k) * umf(k) * g / dp0(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3534) 
  3535)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3536)           ! 'qrten(k)','qsten(k)' : Production rate of rain and snow within the layer k !
  3537)           !     [ kg/kg/s ]         by cumulus expels of condensates to the environment.!         
  3538)           ! This will be falled-out of the layer where it was formed and will be dumped !
  3539)           ! dumped into the release layer assuming that there is no evaporative cooling !
  3540)           ! while precipitable condensate moves to the relaes level. This is reasonable ! 
  3541)           ! assumtion if cumulus is purely vertical and so the path along which precita !
  3542)           ! ble condensate falls is fully saturared. This 're-allocation' process of    !
  3543)           ! precipitable condensate into the release layer is fully described in this   !
  3544)           ! convection scheme. After that, the dumped water into the release layer will !
  3545)           ! falling down across the base of release layer ( or LCL, if  exact treatment ! 
  3546)           ! is required ) and will be allowed to be evaporated in layers below  release !
  3547)           ! layer, and finally non-zero surface precipitation flux will be calculated.  !
  3548)           ! This latter process will be separately treated 'zm_conv_evap' routine.      !
  3549)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3550) 
  3551)           qrten(k) = frc_rasn * dwten(k)
  3552)           qsten(k) = frc_rasn * diten(k) 
  3553)  
  3554)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !         
  3555)           ! 'rainflx','snowflx' : Cumulative rain and snow flux integrated from the ! 
  3556)           !     [ kg/m2/s ]       release leyer to the 'kpen' layer. Note that even !
  3557)           ! though wtw(kpen) < 0 (and umf(kpen) = 0) at the top interface of 'kpen' !
  3558)           ! layer, 'dwten(kpen)' and diten(kpen)  were calculated after calculating !
  3559)           ! explicit cloud top height. Thus below calculation of precipitation flux !
  3560)           ! is correct. Note that  precipitating condensates are formed only in the !
  3561)           ! layers from 'krel' to 'kpen', including the two layers.                 !
  3562)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3563) 
  3564)           rainflx = rainflx + qrten(k) * dp0(k) / g
  3565)           snowflx = snowflx + qsten(k) * dp0(k) / g
  3566) 
  3567)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3568)           ! 'slten(k)','qtten(k)'                                                    !
  3569)           !  Note that 'slflx(k)' and 'qtflx(k)' we have calculated already included !
  3570)           !  all the contributions of (1) expels of condensate (dwten(k), diten(k)), !
  3571)           !  (2) mass detrainment ( delta * umf * ( qtu - qt ) ), & (3) compensating !
  3572)           !  subsidence ( M * dqt / dz ). Thus 'slflx(k)' and 'qtflx(k)' we computed ! 
  3573)           !  is a hybrid turbulent flux containing one part of 'source' term - expel !
  3574)           !  of condensate. In order to calculate 'slten' and 'qtten', we should add !
  3575)           !  additional 'source' term, if any. If the expelled condensate falls down !
  3576)           !  across the base of the layer, it will be another sink (negative source) !
  3577)           !  term.  Note also that we included frictional heating terms in the below !
  3578)           !  calculation of 'slten'.                                                 !
  3579)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------------------ !
  3580)                    
  3581)           slten(k) = ( slflx(km1) - slflx(k) ) * g / dp0(k)
  3582)           if( k .eq. 1 ) then
  3583)               slten(k) = slten(k) - g / 4._r8 / dp0(k) * (                            &
  3584)                                     uflx(k)*(uf(k+1) - uf(k) + u0(k+1) - u0(k)) +     & 
  3585)                                     vflx(k)*(vf(k+1) - vf(k) + v0(k+1) - v0(k)))
  3586)           elseif( k .ge. 2 .and. k .le. kpen-1 ) then
  3587)               slten(k) = slten(k) - g / 4._r8 / dp0(k) * (                            &
  3588)                                     uflx(k)*(uf(k+1) - uf(k) + u0(k+1) - u0(k)) +     &
  3589)                                     uflx(k-1)*(uf(k) - uf(k-1) + u0(k) - u0(k-1)) +   &
  3590)                                     vflx(k)*(vf(k+1) - vf(k) + v0(k+1) - v0(k)) +     &
  3591)                                     vflx(k-1)*(vf(k) - vf(k-1) + v0(k) - v0(k-1)))
  3592)           elseif( k .eq. kpen ) then
  3593)               slten(k) = slten(k) - g / 4._r8 / dp0(k) * (                            &
  3594)                                     uflx(k-1)*(uf(k) - uf(k-1) + u0(k) - u0(k-1)) +   &
  3595)                                     vflx(k-1)*(vf(k) - vf(k-1) + v0(k) - v0(k-1)))
  3596)           endif
  3597)           qtten(k) = ( qtflx(km1) - qtflx(k) ) * g / dp0(k)
  3598) 
  3599)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3600)           ! Compute condensate tendency, including reserved condensate                   !
  3601)           ! We assume that eventual detachment and detrainment occurs in kbup layer  due !
  3602)           ! to downdraft buoyancy sorting. In the layer above the kbup, only penetrative !
  3603)           ! entrainment exists. Penetrative entrained air is assumed not to contain any  !
  3604)           ! condensate.                                                                  !
  3605)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3606)   
  3607)           ! Compute in-cumulus condensate at the layer mid-point.
  3608) 
  3609)           if( k .lt. krel .or. k .gt. kpen ) then
  3610)               qlu_mid = 0._r8
  3611)               qiu_mid = 0._r8
  3612)               qlj     = 0._r8
  3613)               qij     = 0._r8
  3614)           elseif( k .eq. krel ) then 
  3615)               call conden(prel,thlu(krel-1),qtu(krel-1),thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  3616)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3617)                   exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  3618)                   id_exit = .true.
  3619)                   go to 333
  3620)               endif
  3621)               qlubelow = qlj       
  3622)               qiubelow = qij       
  3623)               call conden(ps0(k),thlu(k),qtu(k),thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  3624)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3625)                   exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  3626)                   id_exit = .true.
  3627)                   go to 333
  3628)               end if
  3629)               qlu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qlubelow + qlj ) * ( prel - ps0(k) )/( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) )
  3630)               qiu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qiubelow + qij ) * ( prel - ps0(k) )/( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) )
  3631)           elseif( k .eq. kpen ) then 
  3632)               call conden(ps0(k-1)+ppen,thlu_top,qtu_top,thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  3633)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3634)                   exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  3635)                   id_exit = .true.
  3636)                   go to 333
  3637)               end if
  3638)               qlu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qlubelow + qlj ) * ( -ppen )        /( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) )
  3639)               qiu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qiubelow + qij ) * ( -ppen )        /( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) )
  3640)               qlu_top = qlj
  3641)               qiu_top = qij
  3642)           else
  3643)               call conden(ps0(k),thlu(k),qtu(k),thj,qvj,qlj,qij,qse,id_check)
  3644)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3645)                   exit_conden(i) = 1._r8
  3646)                   id_exit = .true.
  3647)                   go to 333
  3648)               end if
  3649)               qlu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qlubelow + qlj )
  3650)               qiu_mid = 0.5_r8 * ( qiubelow + qij )
  3651)           endif
  3652)           qlubelow = qlj       
  3653)           qiubelow = qij       
  3654) 
  3655)           ! 1. Sustained Precipitation
  3656) 
  3657)           qc_l(k) = ( 1._r8 - frc_rasn ) * dwten(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3658)           qc_i(k) = ( 1._r8 - frc_rasn ) * diten(k) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3659) 
  3660)           ! 2. Detrained Condensate
  3661) 
  3662)           if( k .le. kbup ) then 
  3663)               qc_l(k) = qc_l(k) + g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * qlu_mid ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3664)               qc_i(k) = qc_i(k) + g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * qiu_mid ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3665)               qc_lm   =         - g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * ql0(k)  
  3666)               qc_im   =         - g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * qi0(k)
  3667)             ! Below 'nc_lm', 'nc_im' should be used only when frc_rasn = 1.
  3668)               nc_lm   =         - g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * tr0(k,ixnumliq)  
  3669)               nc_im   =         - g * 0.5_r8 * ( umf(k-1) + umf(k) ) * fdr(k) * tr0(k,ixnumice)
  3670)           else
  3671)               qc_lm   = 0._r8
  3672)               qc_im   = 0._r8
  3673)               nc_lm   = 0._r8
  3674)               nc_im   = 0._r8
  3675)           endif
  3676) 
  3677)           ! 3. Detached Updraft 
  3678) 
  3679)           if( k .eq. kbup ) then
  3680)               qc_l(k) = qc_l(k) + g * umf(k) * qlj     / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3681)               qc_i(k) = qc_i(k) + g * umf(k) * qij     / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3682)               qc_lm   = qc_lm   - g * umf(k) * ql0(k)  / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3683)               qc_im   = qc_im   - g * umf(k) * qi0(k)  / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3684)               nc_lm   = nc_lm   - g * umf(k) * tr0(k,ixnumliq)  / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3685)               nc_im   = nc_im   - g * umf(k) * tr0(k,ixnumice)  / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3686)           endif 
  3687) 
  3688)           ! 4. Cumulative Penetrative entrainment detrained in the 'kbup' layer
  3689)           !    Explicitly compute the properties detrained penetrative entrained airs in k = kbup layer.
  3690) 
  3691)           if( k .eq. kbup ) then
  3692)               call conden(p0(k),thlu_emf(k),qtu_emf(k),thj,qvj,ql_emf_kbup,qi_emf_kbup,qse,id_check)
  3693)               if( id_check .eq. 1 ) then
  3694)                   id_exit = .true.
  3695)                   go to 333
  3696)               endif
  3697)               if( ql_emf_kbup .gt. 0._r8 ) then
  3698)                   nl_emf_kbup = tru_emf(k,ixnumliq)
  3699)               else
  3700)                   nl_emf_kbup = 0._r8
  3701)               endif
  3702)               if( qi_emf_kbup .gt. 0._r8 ) then
  3703)                   ni_emf_kbup = tru_emf(k,ixnumice)
  3704)               else
  3705)                   ni_emf_kbup = 0._r8
  3706)               endif
  3707)               qc_lm   = qc_lm   - g * emf(k) * ( ql_emf_kbup - ql0(k) ) / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3708)               qc_im   = qc_im   - g * emf(k) * ( qi_emf_kbup - qi0(k) ) / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3709)               nc_lm   = nc_lm   - g * emf(k) * ( nl_emf_kbup - tr0(k,ixnumliq) ) / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3710)               nc_im   = nc_im   - g * emf(k) * ( ni_emf_kbup - tr0(k,ixnumice) ) / ( ps0(k-1) - ps0(k) ) ! [ kg/kg/s ]
  3711)           endif 
  3712) 
  3713)           qlten_det   = qc_l(k) + qc_lm
  3714)           qiten_det   = qc_i(k) + qc_im
  3715) 
  3716)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3717)           ! 'qlten(k)','qiten(k)','qvten(k)','sten(k)'                                        !
  3718)           ! Note that falling of precipitation will be treated later.                         !
  3719)           ! The prevension of negative 'qv,ql,qi' will be treated later in positive_moisture. !
  3720)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  3721) 
  3722)           if( use_expconten ) then
  3723)               if( use_unicondet ) then
  3724)                   qc_l(k) = 0._r8
  3725)                   qc_i(k) = 0._r8 
  3726)                   qlten(k) = frc_rasn * dwten(k) + qlten_sink(k) + qlten_det
  3727)                   qiten(k) = frc_rasn * diten(k) + qiten_sink(k) + qiten_det
  3728)               else 
  3729)                   qlten(k) = qc_l(k) + frc_rasn * dwten(k) + ( max( 0._r8, ql0(k) + ( qc_lm + qlten_sink(k) ) * dt ) - ql0(k) ) / dt
  3730)                   qiten(k) = qc_i(k) + frc_rasn * diten(k) + ( max( 0._r8, qi0(k) + ( qc_im + qiten_sink(k) ) * dt ) - qi0(k) ) / dt
  3731)                   trten(k,ixnumliq) = max( nc_lm + nlten_sink(k), - tr0(k,ixnumliq) / dt )
  3732)                   trten(k,ixnumice) = max( nc_im + niten_sink(k), - tr0(k,ixnumice) / dt )
  3733)               endif
  3734)           else
  3735)               if( use_unicondet ) then
  3736)                   qc_l(k) = 0._r8
  3737)                   qc_i(k) = 0._r8 
  3738)               endif                      
  3739)               qlten(k) = dwten(k) + ( qtten(k) - dwten(k) - diten(k) ) * ( ql0(k) / qt0(k) )
  3740)               qiten(k) = diten(k) + ( qtten(k) - dwten(k) - diten(k) ) * ( qi0(k) / qt0(k) )
  3741)           endif
  3742) 
  3743)           qvten(k) = qtten(k) - qlten(k) - qiten(k)
  3744)           sten(k)  = slten(k) + xlv * qlten(k) + xls * qiten(k)
  3745) 
  3746)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3747)           ! 'rliq' : Verticall-integrated 'suspended cloud condensate'                 !
  3748)           !  [m/s]   This is so called 'reserved liquid water'  in other subroutines   ! 
  3749)           ! of CAM3, since the contribution of this term should not be included into   !
  3750)           ! the tendency of each layer or surface flux (precip)  within this cumulus   !
  3751)           ! scheme. The adding of this term to the layer tendency will be done inthe   !
  3752)           ! 'stratiform_tend', just after performing sediment process there.           !
  3753)           ! The main problem of these rather going-back-and-forth and stupid-seeming   ! 
  3754)           ! approach is that the sediment process of suspendened condensate will not   !
  3755)           ! be treated at all in the 'stratiform_tend'.                                !
  3756)           ! Note that 'precip' [m/s] is vertically-integrated total 'rain+snow' formed !
  3757)           ! from the cumulus updraft. Important : in the below, 1000 is rhoh2o ( water !
  3758)           ! density ) [ kg/m^3 ] used for unit conversion from [ kg/m^2/s ] to [ m/s ] !
  3759)           ! for use in stratiform.F90.                                                 !
  3760)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------- ! 
  3761) 
  3762)           qc(k)  =  qc_l(k) +  qc_i(k)   
  3763)           rliq   =  rliq    + qc(k) * dp0(k) / g / 1000._r8    ! [ m/s ]
  3764) 
  3765)        end do
  3766) 
  3767)           precip  =  rainflx + snowflx                       ! [ kg/m2/s ]
  3768)           snow    =  snowflx                                 ! [ kg/m2/s ] 
  3769) 
  3770)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3771)        ! Now treats the 'evaporation' and 'melting' of rain ( qrten ) and ! 
  3772)        ! snow ( qsten ) during falling process. Below algorithms are from !
  3773)        ! 'zm_conv_evap' but with some modification, which allows separate !
  3774)        ! treatment of 'rain' and 'snow' condensates. Note that I included !
  3775)        ! the evaporation dynamics into the convection scheme for complete !
  3776)        ! development of cumulus scheme especially in association with the ! 
  3777)        ! implicit CIN closure. In compatible with this internal treatment !
  3778)        ! of evaporation, I should modify 'convect_shallow',  in such that !
  3779)        ! 'zm_conv_evap' is not performed when I choose UW PBL-Cu schemes. !                                          
  3780)        ! ---------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3781) 
  3782)        evpint_rain    = 0._r8 
  3783)        evpint_snow    = 0._r8
  3784)        flxrain(0:mkx) = 0._r8
  3785)        flxsnow(0:mkx) = 0._r8
  3786)        ntraprd(:mkx)  = 0._r8
  3787)        ntsnprd(:mkx)  = 0._r8
  3788) 
  3789)        do k = mkx, 1, -1  ! 'k' is a layer index : 'mkx'('1') is the top ('bottom') layer
  3790)           
  3791)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3792)           ! flxsntm [kg/m2/s] : Downward snow flux at the top of each layer after melting.! 
  3793)           ! snowmlt [kg/kg/s] : Snow melting tendency.                                    !
  3794)           ! Below allows melting of snow when it goes down into the warm layer below.     !
  3795)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3796) 
  3797)           if( t0(k) .gt. 273.16_r8 ) then
  3798)               snowmlt = max( 0._r8, flxsnow(k) * g / dp0(k) ) 
  3799)           else
  3800)               snowmlt = 0._r8
  3801)           endif
  3802) 
  3803)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3804)           ! Evaporation rate of 'rain' and 'snow' in the layer k, [ kg/kg/s ] !
  3805)           ! where 'rain' and 'snow' are coming down from the upper layers.    !
  3806)           ! I used the same evaporative efficiency both for 'rain' and 'snow'.!
  3807)           ! Note that evaporation is not allowed in the layers 'k >= krel' by !
  3808)           ! assuming that inside of cumulus cloud, across which precipitation !
  3809)           ! is falling down, is fully saturated.                              !
  3810)           ! The asumptions in association with the 'evplimit_rain(snow)' are  !
  3811)           !   1. Do not allow evaporation to supersate the layer              !
  3812)           !   2. Do not evaporate more than the flux falling into the layer   !
  3813)           !   3. Total evaporation cannot exceed the input total surface flux !
  3814)           ! ----------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3815) 
  3816)           call qsat(t0(k), p0(k), es, qs)          
  3817)           subsat = max( ( 1._r8 - qv0(k)/qs ), 0._r8 )
  3818)           if( noevap_krelkpen ) then
  3819)               if( k .ge. krel ) subsat = 0._r8
  3820)           endif
  3821) 
  3822)           evprain  = kevp * subsat * sqrt(flxrain(k)+snowmlt*dp0(k)/g) 
  3823)           evpsnow  = kevp * subsat * sqrt(max(flxsnow(k)-snowmlt*dp0(k)/g,0._r8))
  3824) 
  3825)           evplimit = max( 0._r8, ( qw0_in(i,k) - qv0(k) ) / dt ) 
  3826) 
  3827)           evplimit_rain = min( evplimit,      ( flxrain(k) + snowmlt * dp0(k) / g ) * g / dp0(k) )
  3828)           evplimit_rain = min( evplimit_rain, ( rainflx - evpint_rain ) * g / dp0(k) )
  3829)           evprain = max(0._r8,min( evplimit_rain, evprain ))
  3830) 
  3831)           evplimit_snow = min( evplimit,   max( flxsnow(k) - snowmlt * dp0(k) / g , 0._r8 ) * g / dp0(k) )
  3832)           evplimit_snow = min( evplimit_snow, ( snowflx - evpint_snow ) * g / dp0(k) )
  3833)           evpsnow = max(0._r8,min( evplimit_snow, evpsnow ))
  3834) 
  3835)           if( ( evprain + evpsnow ) .gt. evplimit ) then
  3836)                 tmp1 = evprain * evplimit / ( evprain + evpsnow )
  3837)                 tmp2 = evpsnow * evplimit / ( evprain + evpsnow )
  3838)                 evprain = tmp1
  3839)                 evpsnow = tmp2
  3840)           endif
  3841) 
  3842)           evapc(k) = evprain + evpsnow
  3843) 
  3844)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3845)           ! Vertically-integrated evaporative fluxes of 'rain' and 'snow' !
  3846)           ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3847) 
  3848)           evpint_rain = evpint_rain + evprain * dp0(k) / g
  3849)           evpint_snow = evpint_snow + evpsnow * dp0(k) / g
  3850) 
  3851)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3852)           ! Net 'rain' and 'snow' production rate in the layer [ kg/kg/s ] !
  3853)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------- !         
  3854) 
  3855)           ntraprd(k) = qrten(k) - evprain + snowmlt
  3856)           ntsnprd(k) = qsten(k) - evpsnow - snowmlt
  3857)          
  3858)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3859)           ! Downward fluxes of 'rain' and 'snow' fluxes at the base of the layer [ kg/m2/s ] !
  3860)           ! Note that layer index increases with height.                                     !
  3861)           ! -------------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3862) 
  3863)           flxrain(k-1) = flxrain(k) + ntraprd(k) * dp0(k) / g
  3864)           flxsnow(k-1) = flxsnow(k) + ntsnprd(k) * dp0(k) / g
  3865)           flxrain(k-1) = max( flxrain(k-1), 0._r8 )
  3866)           if( flxrain(k-1) .eq. 0._r8 ) ntraprd(k) = -flxrain(k) * g / dp0(k)
  3867)           flxsnow(k-1) = max( flxsnow(k-1), 0._r8 )         
  3868)           if( flxsnow(k-1) .eq. 0._r8 ) ntsnprd(k) = -flxsnow(k) * g / dp0(k)
  3869) 
  3870)           ! ---------------------------------- !
  3871)           ! Calculate thermodynamic tendencies !
  3872)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3873)           ! Note that equivalently, we can write tendency formula of 'sten' and 'slten' !
  3874)           ! by 'sten(k)  = sten(k) - xlv*evprain  - xls*evpsnow - (xls-xlv)*snowmlt' &  !
  3875)           !    'slten(k) = sten(k) - xlv*qlten(k) - xls*qiten(k)'.                      !
  3876)           ! The above formula is equivalent to the below formula. However below formula !
  3877)           ! is preferred since we have already imposed explicit constraint on 'ntraprd' !
  3878)           ! and 'ntsnprd' in case that flxrain(k-1) < 0 & flxsnow(k-1) < 0._r8          !
  3879)           ! Note : In future, I can elborate the limiting of 'qlten','qvten','qiten'    !
  3880)           !        such that that energy and moisture conservation error is completely  !
  3881)           !        suppressed.                                                          !
  3882)           ! Re-storation to the positive condensate will be performed later below       !
  3883)           ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3884) 
  3885)           qlten(k) = qlten(k) - qrten(k)
  3886)           qiten(k) = qiten(k) - qsten(k)
  3887)           qvten(k) = qvten(k) + evprain  + evpsnow
  3888)           qtten(k) = qlten(k) + qiten(k) + qvten(k)
  3889)           if( ( qv0(k) + qvten(k)*dt ) .lt. qmin(1) .or. &
  3890)               ( ql0(k) + qlten(k)*dt ) .lt. qmin(ixcldliq) .or. &
  3891)               ( qi0(k) + qiten(k)*dt ) .lt. qmin(ixcldice) ) then
  3892)                limit_negcon(i) = 1._r8
  3893)           end if
  3894)           sten(k)  = sten(k) - xlv*evprain  - xls*evpsnow - (xls-xlv)*snowmlt
  3895)           slten(k) = sten(k) - xlv*qlten(k) - xls*qiten(k)
  3896) 
  3897)         !  slten(k) = slten(k) + xlv * ntraprd(k) + xls * ntsnprd(k)         
  3898)         !  sten(k)  = slten(k) + xlv * qlten(k)   + xls * qiten(k)
  3899) 
  3900)        end do
  3901) 
  3902)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3903)        ! Calculate final surface flux of precipitation, rain, and snow !
  3904)        ! Convert unit to [m/s] for use in 'check_energy_chng'.         !  
  3905)        ! ------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3906) 
  3907)        precip  = ( flxrain(0) + flxsnow(0) ) / 1000._r8
  3908)        snow    =   flxsnow(0) / 1000._r8       
  3909) 
  3910)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3911)        ! Until now, all the calculations are done completely in this shallow cumulus !
  3912)        ! scheme. If you want to use this cumulus scheme other than CAM3, then do not !
  3913)        ! perform below block. However, for compatible use with the other subroutines !
  3914)        ! in CAM3, I should subtract the effect of 'qc(k)' ('rliq') from the tendency !
  3915)        ! equation in each layer, since this effect will be separately added later in !
  3916)        ! in 'stratiform_tend' just after performing sediment process there. In order !
  3917)        ! to be consistent with 'stratiform_tend', just subtract qc(k)  from tendency !
  3918)        ! equation of each layer, but do not add it to the 'precip'. Apprently,  this !
  3919)        ! will violate energy and moisture conservations.    However, when performing !
  3920)        ! conservation check in 'tphysbc.F90' just after 'convect_shallow_tend',   we !
  3921)        ! will add 'qc(k)' ( rliq ) to the surface flux term just for the purpose  of !
  3922)        ! passing the energy-moisture conservation check. Explicit adding-back of 'qc'!
  3923)        ! to the individual layer tendency equation will be done in 'stratiform_tend' !
  3924)        ! after performing sediment process there. Simply speaking, in 'tphysbc' just !
  3925)        ! after 'convect_shallow_tend', we will dump 'rliq' into surface as a  'rain' !
  3926)        ! in order to satisfy energy and moisture conservation, and  in the following !
  3927)        ! 'stratiform_tend', we will restore it back to 'qlten(k)' ( 'ice' will go to !  
  3928)        ! 'water' there) from surface precipitation. This is a funny but conceptually !
  3929)        ! entertaining procedure. One concern I have for this complex process is that !
  3930)        ! output-writed stratiform precipitation amount will be underestimated due to !
  3931)        ! arbitrary subtracting of 'rliq' in stratiform_tend, where                   !
  3932)        ! ' prec_str = prec_sed + prec_pcw - rliq' and 'rliq' is not real but fake.   ! 
  3933)        ! However, as shown in 'srfxfer.F90', large scale precipitation amount (PRECL)!
  3934)        ! that is writed-output is corrected written since in 'srfxfer.F90',  PRECL = !
  3935)        ! 'prec_sed + prec_pcw', without including 'rliq'. So current code is correct.!
  3936)        ! Note also in 'srfxfer.F90', convective precipitation amount is 'PRECC =     ! 
  3937)        ! prec_zmc(i) + prec_cmf(i)' which is also correct.                           !
  3938)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3939) 
  3940)        do k = 1, kpen       
  3941)           qtten(k) = qtten(k) - qc(k)
  3942)           qlten(k) = qlten(k) - qc_l(k)
  3943)           qiten(k) = qiten(k) - qc_i(k)
  3944)           slten(k) = slten(k) + ( xlv * qc_l(k) + xls * qc_i(k) )
  3945)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3946)           ! Since all reserved condensates will be treated  as liquid water in the !
  3947)           ! 'check_energy_chng' & 'stratiform_tend' without an explicit conversion !
  3948)           ! algorithm, I should consider explicitly the energy conversions between !
  3949)           ! 'ice' and 'liquid' - i.e., I should convert 'ice' to 'liquid'  and the !
  3950)           ! necessary energy for this conversion should be subtracted from 'sten'. ! 
  3951)           ! Without this conversion here, energy conservation error come out. Note !
  3952)           ! that there should be no change of 'qvten(k)'.                          !
  3953)           ! ---------------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3954)           sten(k)  = sten(k)  - ( xls - xlv ) * qc_i(k)
  3955)        end do
  3956) 
  3957)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3958)        ! Prevent the onset-of negative condensate at the next time step  !
  3959)        ! Potentially, this block can be moved just in front of the above !
  3960)        ! block.                                                          ! 
  3961)        ! --------------------------------------------------------------- !
  3962) 
  3963)        ! Modification : I should check whether this 'positive_moisture_single' routine is
  3964)        !                consistent with the one used in UW PBL and cloud macrophysics schemes.
  3965)        ! Modification : Below may overestimate resulting 'ql, qi' if we use the new 'qc_l', 'qc_i'
  3966)        !                in combination with the original computation of qlten, qiten. However,
  3967)        !                if we use new 'qlten,qiten', there is no problem.
  3968) 
  3969)         qv0_star(:mkx) = qv0(:mkx) + qvten(:mkx) * dt
  3970)         ql0_star(:mkx) = ql0(:mkx) + qlten(:mkx) * dt
  3971)         qi0_star(:mkx) = qi0(:mkx) + qiten(:mkx) * dt
  3972)         s0_star(:mkx)  =  s0(:mkx) +  sten(:mkx) * dt
  3973)         call positive_moisture_single( xlv, xls, mkx, dt, qmin(1), qmin(ixcldliq), qmin(ixcldice), &
  3974)              dp0, qv0_star, ql0_star, qi0_star, s0_star, qvten, qlten, qiten, sten )
  3975)         qtten(:mkx)    = qvten(:mkx) + qlten(:mkx) + qiten(:mkx)
  3976)         slten(:mkx)    = sten(:mkx)  - xlv * qlten(:mkx) - xls * qiten(:mkx)
  3977) 
  3978)        ! --------------------- !
  3979)        ! Tendencies of tracers !
  3980)        ! --------------------- !
  3981) 
  3982)        do m = 4, ncnst
  3983)
